hariḥ suparṇa iti prātar ud u tyaṃ citraṃ devānām iti madhyaṃdine atha sauramantrān yathākāmaṃ japed 
ud vayaṃ tamasas parīti ca
ud ghed abhi śrutāmagham ity astamita āsīnaḥ
sāvitryante vāñjalayo japaś ca ।।

athordhvajānur āsīna iti vīrāsanī pratyutthāyābhayaṃ paścād abhayaṃ purastād ity upatiṣṭhate tiṣṭhan prātaḥ prāṅmukha 
āyātu varadety āvāhya
gāyatraṃ chandaḥ savitā devatā viśvāmitra ṛṣir
yathākṣaraṃ daivataṃ rūpaṃ ca manasi samādhāya mahāvyāhṛtibhiḥ saṃdhāya gāyatrīṃ japet ।।

aṣṭakṛtva ekādaśakṛtvo dvādaśakṛtvaḥ pañcadaśakṛtvaḥ śatakṛtvaḥ sahasrakṛtva iti ।।

aṣṭakṛtvaḥ prayuktā gāyatrī gāyatreṇa chandasā saṃmitā bhūlokam abhijayati ।।

ekādaśakṛtvaḥ prayuktā traiṣṭubhena chandasā saṃmitāntarikṣalokam abhijayati ।।

dvādaśakṛtvaḥ prayuktā jāgatena chandasā saṃmitā divaṃ lokam abhijayati ।।

pañcadaśakṛtvaḥ prayuktā pañcadaśena vajreṇa saṃmitā brahmalokam abhijayati ।।

śatakṛtvaḥ prayuktā śataparvaṇā vajreṇa saṃmitā sarvāṇl lokān abhijayati ।।

sahasrakṛtvaḥ prayuktāgniṣṭomāptoryāmādīnāṃ kratūnāṃ phalam avāpnoti ।।

ato yathākāmaṃ japitvā paśyema śaradaḥ śatam indra jīvety āśiṣaḥ prārthayate ।।

stutā mayā varadeti visṛjyodīrāṇā uta sūryasyāvṛtam asapatnaṃ purastād yasmāt kośād iti yathārtham upatiṣṭhate ।।

ya imāṃ na vindanti nādhīyate saṃdhyākāle nopāsate te hy aśrotriyā bhavanty anupanītāḥ kriyāhīnāś chedanabhedanabhojanamaithunāny abhicarantaḥ ।।

saṃdhyākāle hy ajapantaḥ śvasūkarasṛgālakukkuṭasarpayoniṣu varṣasahasrāṇi jāyante ।।

samās tasyaivopajāyante ।।

tasmād yathoktāṃ sāyaṃ prātaḥ saṃdhyām upāsīta ।।

araṇyacarito guptaḥ śuklabrāhmaṇakarmasu । prāyeṇa labhate lokān yathoktāṃs tāṃ samācaran ।।

sāyaṃ saṃdhyām upāsīta kṛtavīrāsano dvijaḥ । kṛtottānas tathā prātaḥ prāñjaliḥ susamāhitaḥ ।।

etad vīrāsanaṃ sthānaṃ brahmaṇā nirmitaṃ purā । dvijānaṃ bālavṛddhānāṃ puraścaraṇam uttamam ।।

sāyaṃ prātas tu yaḥ saṃdhyām askannām upatiṣṭhate । sa tayā pāvito devyā brāhmahaḥ pūtakilbiṣaḥ ।।

na sīdet pratigṛhṇānaḥ pṛthvīm api sasāgarām । ye cāsya viṣamāḥ ke cid divi sūryādayo grahāḥ ।।

te cāsya saumyā jāyante śivāḥ sukhakarāḥ sadā । sthānaṃ vīrāsanaṃ caeṣāṃ pṛthivī ca pradakṣiṇā । agnihotraṃ hutaṃ caiṣāṃ ye vai saṃdhyām upāsate ।।

ardhāstamita āditye ardhodite divākare । gāyatryās tatra sāṃnidhyaṃ saṃdhyākālaḥ sa ucyate ।।

bhūmyādityāntaraṃ yas tu chādayec caturaṅgulam । tāṃ tu saṃdhyāṃ parāṃ vidyāc chāyāsaṃbhedane pare ।।

yāvantas tu karād bhraṣṭāḥ patanti jalabindavaḥ । bhūtvā vajrāṇi te sarve patanti hy asureṣu vai ।।

tato vibhāvasus teṣāṃ prītātmāpyāyate varam । yair ahaṃ mokṣito viprais teṣāṃ loko tathā mama ।।

gāyatryā akṣamālāyāṃ sāyaṃ prātaḥ śataṃ japet । caturṇāṃ khalu vedānāṃ samagraṃ labhate phalam ।।

saṃdhyāṃ ye nopatiṣṭhanti brāhmaṇyaṃ nopapadyate । upapadyeta vā bhūyo yadi syus tīrthamṛtyavaḥ ।।

ṛṣayo dīrghasaṃdhyatvād dīrghāṇy āyumṣy adhārayan । tasmād dīrghām upāsīta samicchan vṛddhim āyuṣaḥ ।।

tad yathāgnir devānāṃ brāhmaṇo manuṣyāṇāṃ vasanta ṛtūnām evaṃ gāyatrī chandasām ।।

tad yathā gāyatrī katyakṣarā katipadā kiṃ vāsyā gotraṃ kiṃ vāsya rūpaṃ kīdṛśaṃ tasyāḥ śarīraṃ bhavati ।।

yad vai bhūḥ sa ṛgvedo yad bhuva iti so atharvaveda iti tad yathedam akṣaram om ity akṣaraṃ tat paramaṃ śam ity akṣaraṃ guhyaṃ tat paramaṃ pavitram ।।

ādityo vai sāvitry ādityena saha sāvitrī stauti suvati prātaḥ prasuvati tasmāt sāvitrītam ।।

akṣaradaivataṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ prathamam āgneyaṃ dvitīyam āśvinaṃ tṛtīyaṃ saumyaṃ caturthaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ sāvitraṃ pañcamaṃ ṣaṣṭhaṃ pauṣṇaṃ saptamaṃ mārutam aṣṭamaṃ bārhaspatyaṃ navamaṃ maitraṃ daśamaṃ vāruṇam ekādaśam aindraṃ dvādaśaṃ vaiśvadevaṃ vasūnāṃ trayodaśaṃ caturdaśaṃ rudrāṇāṃ pañcadaśam ādityānām aditeḥ ṣoḍaśaṃ vāyavyaṃ saptadaśamaṃ bhaumam aṣṭādaśam ekonaviṃśam āntarikṣaṃ divyaṃ viṃśaṃ digdevatāni catvāry akṣarāṇi ।।

atha yat pūrvāṃ saṃdhyām upāste tad gāyatryāḥ śiras tena pṛthivīṃ jayati ।।

atha yan madhyāhne tīkṣṇaṃ rudras tapati dvitīyaṃ śiras tenāntarikṣaṃ jayati ।।

atha yad astamiyāt tat tṛtīyaṃ śiras tena divaṃ jayati ।।

tasyā oṃkāraḥ śiraḥ saha vyāhṛtibhir darbhāḥ keśā oṣadhīvanaspatayo lomāni cakṣuṣī sūryācandramasau vidyud dhasitaṃ viṣṇuvaruṇau urasī rudro hṛdaye paurṇamāsī cāmāvāsyā ca stanau ahaś ca rātrī ca pārśve daśa diśaḥ kukṣī sarvajñānāni vyākaraṇam udaraṃ pṛthivī śroṇī vāyuḥ sthānaṃ bhūṣaṇaṃ nakṣatrāṇi śrīsarasvatīrūpā padakramamantrabrāhmaṇakalpaśarīrā sāvitrī gotreṇa brahmadeyā bhavati brahmadeyā bhavatīti brāhmaṇam ।।

atha snānavidhiṃ puṇyaṃ vakṣyamāṇaṃ nibodhata । yena snātā divaṃ lokaṃ prāpnuvanti dvijottamāḥ ।।

saritsu vā taḍāge vā devakhāte hrade api vā । gartaprasravaṇe vāpi puṇyaṃ snānaṃ samācaret ।।

pārakye tu tāḍāge hi snānaṃ naiva vidhīyate । taḍāgakartur duṣkṛtair lipyate snānam ācāran ।।

saritāṃ sarasāṃ caiva aprāptau nirjharasya ca । uddhṛtya caturaḥ piṇḍān snāyāt tu parakhātake ।।

anvīkṣyamāṇaḥ pārśvāni kuśahastaḥ samāhitaḥ । dvijo madhyaṃdinād arvāg arogī snānam ācaret ।।

yat te bhūma iti mṛdaṃ saṃgṛhya rcā samāhitaḥ । yas te gandha iti tribhir mṛdhir ātmānam ālabhet ।।

aghadviṣṭeti sūktena dūrvāṃ śirasi vinyaset । agramagram ity etayā gomayenānulepayet ।।

agramagraṃ carantīnām oṣadhīnāṃ vanevane । yan me rogaṃ ca śokaṃ ca tan me tvaṃ nuda gomaya ।।

praṇavādyā vyāhṛtīs tu gāyatrīṃ ca śiroyutām । paṭhet trir anavānaṃ hi prāṇāyāmaḥ sa ucyate ।।

ambayo yantīty ādīni trīṇi sūktāni hi kramāt । hiraṇyavarṇā yad ado vāyoḥ pūtaḥ punantu mā ।।

vaiśvānaro raśmibhiś ca tathāpsu ta iti smṛtam । etaiḥ saṃplāvayet sūktais tato aghamarṣaṇam ।।

apo divyāś ca saṃ māgne idam āpaḥ śivena mā । yad āpo naktam iti ca etat syād aghamarṣaṇam ।।

yad āpo naktaṃ mithunaṃ cakāra yad vā dudroha duritaṃ purāṇam । hiraṇyavarṇās tata ut punantu pra mā muñcantu varuṇasya pāśāt ।।

sarasvatīṃ gayāṃ gaṅgāṃ naimiṣaṃ puṣkarāṇi ca । smṛtvā tīrthānipuṇyātni avagāhej jalaṃ tataḥ ।।

gacchataḥ snānakāryāya pitaraḥ saha daivataiḥ । pṛṣṭhataḥ tv anugacchanti tatsamīpaṃ jalārthinaḥ ।।

āśāṃ tyaktvā nivartante vastraniṣpīḍanena tu । tasmān na pīḍayed vastram akṛtvā pitṛtarpaṇam ।।

utsāhaṃ varuṇaḥ snāne agnir hotuḥ śriyaṃ haret । āyuṣyaṃ bhuñjato mṛtyus triṣu maunam ataś caret ।।

snānavastre mṛdas tisraḥ pradadyāc chuddhihetunā । b । snātvā paryukṣya vāso anyac chodhye jaṅghe mṛdā punaḥ ।।

vastraniṣpīḍatoyena apavitrīkṛte hi te । uttirya vastraṃ niṣpīḍya japed ādhyātmikāni tu ।।

adhyātmam asyavāmīyaṃ kautsaṃ kauṣmāṇḍikaṃ tathā । japtvātharvaśiraś caiva bhavāśarvīyam eva ca ।।

prāṇāś ca bhagavān kālaḥ puruṣo manyur eva ca । ucchiṣṭo rohito vrātya etāny ādhyātmikāni tu ।।

saṃvatsareṇa yat pāpaṃ kṛtaṃ ghoram avistaram । japtvaitāni tataḥ pāpān mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ ।।

viṣāsahiṃ manasā hi japtvā gāyatrīṃ ca tathā tridivaṃ prāyāti । paribhraṣṭas tridivāt tapaḥkṣaye jātismaratvaṃ punar eva vindate ।।

om atha tarpaṇavidhim anukramiṣyāmaḥ ।।

snātopasparśanakāle avagāhya devatās tarpayati ।।

vasūnāṃ namo brahmaṇe namo vaiśravaṇāya namo dharmāya namaḥ kāmāya namo lokāya amo devāya namo vedāya nama ṛṣibhyo nama ārṣeyebhyo namo aṅgirobhyo nama āṅgirasebhyo namo atharvebhyo nama ātharvaṇebhyo namo marudbhyo namo mārutebhyo amo vasubhyo namo rudrebhyo nama ādityebhyo namaḥ siddhebhyo namaḥ sādhyebhyo nama āpyebhyo namo aśvibhyāṃ namo gurubhyo namo 
gurupatnībhyo namaḥ
pitṛbhyo namo
mātṛbhyo namaḥ ।।

yamāya namo dharmarājāya namo mṛtyave namo antakāya namo vaivasvatāya namaḥ kālāya namaś citrāya namaś citraguptāya namaḥ sarvabhūtakṣayāya namaḥ kṛtāya namaḥ kṛtāntāya namo mahodarāya namo dhātre namo

kṛṣṇās tṛpyantu ।।

ajās tṛpyantu ।।

yāṃ kāṃ cit saritaṃ gatvā kṛṣṇapakṣe caturdaśīm । ekaikasya tilair miśrān dadyāt trīn udakāñjalīn ।।

ā yāteti hi tisṛbhiḥ pitṝn āvāhayet tataḥ । ud īratām iti tisṛbhiḥ pitṛbhyo dadyāt tilodakam ।।

nābhimātre jale sthitvā cintayen manasā pitṝn । tathā mātāmahebhyaś ca śucau deśe atha barhiṣi ।।

parā yātety etayā pitṝṃs tṛptān visarjayet । mano nv ā hvāmahīty evaṃ pañcabhir mana upāhvayeta ।।

etadd hi tarpaṇaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ svayam uktaṃ svayaṃbhuvā । śraddhadhānaḥ samācaṣṭe brahmalokaṃ sa gacchati ।।

om athātaḥ śrāddhavidhiṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ।।

catuṣprakāraṃ śrāddhaṃ bhavati ।।

nityam ābhyudayikaṃ kāmyam ekoddiṣṭaṃ ceti ।।

tatra nityam amāvāsyāyām ।।

ābhyudayikaṃ mātṛpūrvakaṃ puṃsavanādiṣu saṃskāreṣu ।।

kāmyaṃ tithidravyabrāhmaṇasaṃyoge ।।

ekoddiṣṭaṃ saṃcayanaprabhṛty ā sapiṇḍīkaraṇāt ।।

tatra nitye yugmān daive brāhmaṇān upāmantrayet ।।

ābhyudayike ubhayatra yugmān ।।

yavais tilārthā ṛjavo darbhāḥ pradakṣiṇaṃ kuryāt ।।

kāmyaṃ tu nityavat ।।

athaikoddiṣṭaṃ tūṣṇīṃ yāvad uktam ।।

nāgnevaṃ na daivam ayugmānbrāhmaṇān ।।

dakṣiṇāmukha upaviśya pitryeṇopacaryaikaṃ pavitram ekam udapātram apratyāvṛttim āsanaṃ nāmagotreṇaikaṃ piṇḍam etat te annam iti ।।

śve adyeti vā śrāddhaṃ kariṣyāmīti brāhmaṇān upāmantrayet ।।

trīn pañca sapta vā na prasajyeta vistara iti vacanāt ।।

prāṅmukhān viśvedevān udaṅmukhān pitṝn ।।

vedavedāṅgavidaḥ pañcāgnir anūcāno avyavahārī śrotriyas triṇāciketas trimadhus trisuparṇī chandogo jyeṣṭhasāmago atharvaśiraso adhyetā saṃdhyāsnāyī devapitṛsadāhniko mātṛpitṛśuśrūṣur bhṛgvaṅgirovid dharmaśāstravid iti ।।

prayato aparāhṇe śuciḥ śuklavāsāḥ ।।

svāgatenābhyarcyācamanīyaṃ kṛtvā dattvā brāhmaṇān upasaṃgṛhyopaveśayed 
daive pitrye ca sadarbheṣv āsaneṣu
tato anujñāpayed devān pitṝṃś cāvāhayiṣyāmīti
āvāhaya saumyās te santv ity anujñātaḥ pūrvaṃ devān āvāhayed viśve devāsa ā gateti ।।

viśve devāsa ā gata śṛṇutā ma imaṃ havam । edaṃ barhir ni ṣīdata iti ।।

ā yāteti pitṝn āvāhayed ācyā jānv ity upaveśayet saṃ viśaṃtv iti saṃveśayed iti ।।

yajñopavītī sāvitryodapātram abhimantrya viśvebhyo devebhyaḥ pādayam arghyam ācamanīyam iti brāhmaṇahasteṣu ninayet ।।

trīṇy udapātrāṇi kalpayed gandhamālyatilair miśrāṇi kṛtvā' aud īratām iti tisṛbhir udapātrāṇy anvṛcaṃ sapavitreṣu brāhmaṇahasteṣu ninayet ।।

prapitāmahebhyaḥ pitāmahebhyaḥ pitṛbhyaś ceti dattvā gandhamālyadhūpāñjanādarśapradīpasyopaharanam sarvānnaprakāram ādāyāgnau kariṣyāmīty anujñāpya kuruṣvety anujñāto darbhair dakṣiṇāgrair agniṃ paristīrya juhuyād agnaye kavyavāhanāyeti tisṛbhir 
hutaśeṣaṃ brāhmaṇebhyo dadyād
aṅguṣṭham upayamya pradakṣiṇaṃ daive prasavyaṃ pitrya idaṃ viṣṇur iti japej jānuṃ niṣadya bhūmāv
atas tilair māṃsaiḥ śākair yuṣaiḥ kṛsarāpāyasāpūpair lājair bhakṣair ikṣuvikāraiḥ pānair madhunā ghṛtena dadhnā payasā caiva prabhūtamṛṣṭato annaṃ dadyād anasūyaḥ ।।

pavitrapāṇir dharbheṣv āsīno madhu vātā iti japet
pavitraṃ dharmaśāstram apratirathaṃ prāṇasūktaṃ puruṣasūktam upaniṣadam anyad vādhyātmikaṃ kiṃ cit
tṛptāñ jñātvānnaṃ prakīrya dattvā cāpaḥ sakṛtsakṛd annaṃ ye agnidagdhā iti vikiram ।।

darbhir āstīrya dyuaur darvir akṣiteti tisṛbhiḥ sarvānnaprakāram uddhṛtyājyena saṃnīya trīn piṇḍān saṃhatān nidadhāty etat te pratatāmaheti dakṣiṇataḥ patnībhya idaṃ vaḥ patnyā itīdam āśaṃsūnām idam āśaṃsamānānām ity annena prasavyaṃ parikiranam ।। ye dasyava ity ulmukenābhipariharaṇam 
ekoddiṣṭe tv ekaṃ piṇḍam ekam udapātram ācamyopotthāya etaṃ bhāgam etaṃ sadhasthāḥ śyeno nṛcakṣā iti ca śrāddhaṃ dattvābhimantrayec cheṣam
anujñāpyācamanīyaṃ dattvā puṇyāhaṃ vācayed dakṣiṇāṃ ca dattvā yathāśakty udapātraśeṣaṃ sapavitreṣu brāhmaṇahasteṣu ninayet
putraṃ pautram ity ekam āpo agnim iti dvitīyaṃ yuktābhyāṃ tṛtīyaṃ putraṃ pautram ity ekayodapātram iti kauśikaḥ ।।

prapitāmahebhyaḥ pitāmahebhyaḥ pitṛbhyo mātulamātāmahebhyo nirdiṣṭaṃ tebhyaḥ sarvebhyaḥ sapatnīkebhyaḥ svadhāvad akṣayyam astv akṣayyam astv iti vrāhmaṇavacanam ।।

dātāro no abhivardhantāṃ vedāḥ saṃtatir eva ca । śraddhā ca no mā vyagamad bahudeyaṃ ca no astv ity evaṃ varān vācayitvā namo vaḥ pitara ity evamādi mano nv ā hvāmahīty evamantaṃ samānaṃ piṇḍapitṛyajñena madhyamapiṇḍapradānaṃ ceti ।।

vājevāje avata vājino no dhaneṣu viprā amṛtā ṛtajñāḥ । asya madhvaḥ pibata mādayadhvaṃ tṛptā yāta pathibhir devayānaiḥ ।।

iti brāhmaṇān hasteṣu gṛhītvotthāpya pradakṣiṇaṃ kuryād eṣa śrāddhavidhir anena vidhinā putrān paśūn dhānyaṃ hiraṇyam āyuś ca labhate ya evaṃ vedeti ca brāhmaṇam ।।

māhakiḥ kauśikāc ca māhakiḥ kauśikāc ceti ।।

om agnihotram ।।

sāyam ārambhaḥ prātar apavargaḥ ।।

nāntareṇānyat kuryāt ।।

prātar ārambhamity eke ।।

yajñapātrāṇi prakṣālyāgnihotraṃ śrapayet ।।

śrapyamāṇaṃ ced viṣyandet tad adbhir upaninayet
tad anumantrayate pṛthivīṃ turīyam ity etābhiḥ
pratyānīyodag udvāsya barhir udapātram undayati paryukṣya ।।

ṛtaṃ tvā satyena pariṣiñcāmīti hoṣyan ।।

satyaṃ tva rteneti hute ।।

gārhapatyād āhavanīyam udakadhārāṃ ninayati ।। amṛtam asy amṛtam amṛtena saṃdhehīti ।।

āhavanīyaṃ paryukṣya gārhapatyaṃ prāpyāṅgārān avaloḍya carusthālyā saṃsparśayati ।।

nirūḍhaṃ japaty ubhayam iti pratyūḍham iti pratininayati 
sruvaṃ srucaṃ ca pratitapati niṣṭaptaṃ rakṣo niṣṭaptā arātayaḥ pratyuṣṭaṃ rakṣaḥ pratyuṣṭā arātaya ity
adbhir abhyukṣya carusthālyāṃ sruveṇa sruci gṛhītam iti samānam
srucam ādāya gṛhyāhavanīyam abhikrāmatīdam ahaṃ yajamānaṃ svargaṃ lokam unnayāmīti ।।

barhiṣi srucaṃ nidhāya samidham ādadhāti ।।

agnijyotiṣaṃ tvā vāyumatīṃ prāṇavatīṃ svargyāṃ svargāyopadadhāmi bhāsvatīṃ svāheti ।।

samidhaṃ pradīptām abhijuhoti ।।

sajūr devena savitrā sajū rātryendravatyā juṣāṇo agnir vetu svāheti sāyam ।।

sajūr devena savitrā sajūr uṣasendravatyā juṣāṇaḥ sūryo vetu svāheti prātar
āhutir udayahome agner eva
jyotiṣmān udety āyaṃtanatām iti ।।

prajāpate na tvad etāny anya iti manasaivobhayatra prājāpatyottarābhutīr hutvā 
sruvaṃ trir udañcam unnayati rudrān prīṇāmīti
barhiṣi sruvaṃ nidhāyonmṛjya
pitryupavītaṃ kṛtvā dakṣiṇataḥ pitṛbhyaḥ svadhāṃ karomīti ।।

hutam agnihotraṃ sarveṣv ity eke ।।

carusthālyāḥ sruveṇa ।।

iha puṣṭiṃ puṣṭipatir dadhātv iha prajāṃ janayatu prajāpatiḥ । agnaye gṛhapataye rayimate paśupataye puṣṭipataye svāheti gārhapatye ।।

agnaye annādāyānnapataye svāheti dakṣiṇāgnau hutvā ।।

manasaivobhayatra prajāpateś carusthālī srucaṃ sruvaṃ barhiṣy ādhāyottarato agner upaviśya prāśnāti ।।

prāṇān prīṇāmīty upaspṛśya garbhān prīṇāmīti dvitīyaṃ viśvān devān prīṇāmīty antataḥ sarvam
aprakṣālitayodakaṃ srucā ninayati sarpetarajanān prīṇāmīti
barhiṣā prakṣālya sarpapuṇyajanān prīṇāmīti dvitīyam ।।

gandharvāpsarasaḥ prīṇāmīti apareṇāhavanīyam udakaṃ tṛtīyam ।।

sapta rṣīn prīṇāmīti srucaṃ sruvaṃ ca pratitapati dakṣiṇān nayāmīti rātrau srugdaṇḍam avamārṣṭi ।।

prātar unmārṣṭi ।।

ity uktaṃ samidādhānam agnyupasthānam ।। rātriṃ rātrim aprayātaṃ bharanta iti ।।

yathākālaṃ sāyamsāyaṃ gṛhapatir ayaṃ no agnir iti dve gārhapatyapaścād dugdhānnasyāgnihotraśrapaṇī vidhīyate ।।

yajña te veda pṛṣṭham ity etayālabhyābhimantrayate ।।

ukhāyaṃ sravantyāṃ sa mardakarmabhyo anyasyāṃ dṛḍhatarāyāṃ pratyāsicya sutā deveṣv ity anumantrayate ।।

evaṃ sarvāsūkhāsu somakalaśamahāvīre vā atha yasyāgnihotradhenvādi vyāpadyeta । tatra yathādevataṃ juhuyād apratibhāve vyāhṛtibhiḥ ।।

atha vedavratasyādeśanavidhiṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ।।

sāṃvatsarikaṃ vedavratam ।।

kalpānāṃ ṣāṇmāsikam ।।

romanakhāni dhārayet triṣavaṇaṃ tu snāyād dhaviṣyam aśnīyān na tu naktam aṇūn māśān masūrāṃs tu ।।

daṇḍamathitam uddhṛtasnehaṃ nāśīyāt ।।

daṇḍakamaṇḍaludhāraṇaṃ vāsaś cāthorṇam śirasvrataṃ ca sāṃvatsarikaṃ vedavratenaiva vyākhyātam ।।

atha pramāṇāni vakṣyāmo 
yamānāṃ mitrasya mṛgārthasyākṣīrākṣārabhojanam ayugmam āchādanam anantarhitā śayyā
mṛgārtheṣv aviśeṣeṇa yameṣu sarvam eva śamīdhānyaṃ na bhuñjītā
athopasamādadhāti ।।

samās tvāsmai kṣatrāṇy etam idhmam agnir bhūmyām iti tisṛbhir mamāgne varca iti sarvasūktenāyuṣyair varcasyaiḥ svastyayanair abhayair aparājitaiḥ śarmavarmabhiś copasamādadhāti ।।

vrataṃ nivedya vrātapatībhiḥ samidho abhyādadhyād 
āṅgirasān samāsān hutvā bhārgavair viparyastām āṅgirasīm
vedādibhir vedottamaiḥ vargādibhir vargottamaiḥ padādibhiḥ padottamaiḥ kāṇḍādibhiḥ kāṇḍottamair anuvākādibhir anuvākottamair mahatkāṇḍair viśeṣeṇa sūktādibhiḥ sūktottamair
atraitāny aṣṭarcaprabhṛtīni vyākhyātāni ।।

brahmajyeṣṭheti ekā kāmojajñe kāmas tad iti hutvā kalpavrate viśeṣo vacanakarmasu brāhmaṇaṃ śrāvayet ।।

keśībrāhmaṇaṃ ca yeṣu vrataviśeṣaḥ syān na tān mantrān udāharet samāsavat sa hotavyaḥ purāṇārthaṃ vijānatā ।।

agnim īle purohitaṃ yajñasya devam ṛtvijam । hotāraṃ ratnadhātamam ।।

tac chaṃ yor āvṛṇīmahe gātuṃ yajñāya gātuṃ yajñapataye । daivī svastir astu naḥ svastir mānuṣebhyaḥ । ūrdhvaṃ jigātu bheṣajaṃ śaṃ no astu dvipade śaṃ catuṣpade ।।

iṣe tvorje tvā vāyava sthopāyava stha devo vaḥ savitā prārpayatu śreṣṭhatamāya karmaṇa āpyāyadhvam aghnyā indrāya bhāgam [ūrjasvatīḥ payasvatīḥ] prajāvatīr anamīvā ayakṣmā mā va stena īśata māghaśaṃso rudrasya hetiḥ pari vo vṛṇaktu dhruvā asmin gopatau syāta bahvīr yajamānasya paśūn pāhi ।।

dadhikrāvṇo akāriṣaṃ jiṣṇor aśvasya vājinaḥ । surabhi no mukhā karat pra ṇa āyumṣi tāriṣat ।।

agna ā yāhi vītaye gṛṇāno gavyadātaye । ni hotā satsi barhiṣi ।।

eṣa sya te dhārayā suto avyo vārebhir yavane maditavyam । krīḍan raśmir apārthivaḥ ।।

ye triṣaptā vasyobhūyāya ye triṣaptā marmāṇi te vasyobhūyāya ye triṣaptā ye diśāṃ marmāṇi te yāṃ devā vasyobhūyāya ye triṣaptāḥ samānāṃ māsām ā te nayatv ā arjanyasya ye diśāṃ kṛtyākṛtaṃ valaginam akṣitās te marmāṇi te viṣam evendraṃ mitraṃ vaśāṃ devā yāṃ deyāḥ sūrya enam annādyena yaśasā pra budhyasvāhnā pratyag vasyobhūyāya ।।

ye triṣaptāḥ śaṃ na āpo yathā vāto yadi no gāṃ haṃsy apendra dviṣataḥ putram attu samānāṃ vṛṣāyamāṇaḥ sūryam ṛtaṃ paripāṇam asy ā harāmiye krimaya ā te nayatu parṇo asīndraputre viśvāhā te gosaniṃ vy asmai mitrāvaruṇāv ā parjānyasya svapna svapnābhikaraena devānām asthi mahāntaṃ kośaṃ yo antarikṣeṇopa śreṣṭhā aham eva vāta ivāva bādhe ye diśām 
ardham ardhenaivā mahān arvāñcam indraṃ śīrṣāmayam upahatyām aśvasyāśna indrasya varūthaṃ hiraṇyavarṇā subhagā atrainān indrod āyur ud bṛhatā mano
devo devāya sadyo jātas tastuvann agnir ivaitu śataṃ ca me yady ekādaśo asi nāsya dhenur iṣur iva digdhā na varṣam acyutacyud etā devasenā
gandhāribhyaḥ sarveṣāṃ ca krimīṇāṃ tatas tatāmahāḥ prajāpate śreṣṭhenāśvinā brahmaṇāgne svāhā ghṛtād ulluptaṃ tārṣṭāghīr ayaṃ lokaḥ kṛtyākrtaṃ valaginam ।।

dive cakṣuṣe ayaṃ nas triṃśad dhāma mā no hāsiṣur yat kiṃ cedam ahaṃ jajāna yāvadaṅgīnaṃ yas te aṅkuśas tānūṣ ṭe vājinn āñjanasya dvādaśadhā abhyañjanam akṣitās te yāvanto mā bradhnaḥ samīcīr yadi vāsi bṛhaspatir no yo naḥ śapāt sūyavasād yaṃ devā yathā śepo namaskṛtya marmāṇi te agneḥ śarīram 
prati cakṣvāprajāstvam ito jaya [yat pratyāhanti] viṣam eva yās te śivā etaṃ vo yuvānaṃ jyotiṣmato lokān saṃ te śīrṣṇa indraṃ mitraṃ prabhrājamānām āre abhūd
etam idhmam akāmo dhīro vaśāṃ devā namas te ghoṣiṇībhyaḥ prāṇa mā mad yan mātalī apsu stīmāsu yāṃ devā bhūme mātaḥ pratyañcam arkam ūrdhvāyai tvā yadi hutām
sūrya enaṃ yo yajñasyābodhy agniḥ kṛṣṇāyāḥ putro annādyena yaśasā brahmāparaṃ pra budhyasvainaṃ śraddhā ahnā pratyaṃ śakvarī stha vasyobhūyāya ।।

vratair bhṛgvaṅgiraḥproktair ānupūrvyād vidhānataḥ । upasanne guruḥ kuryād vratavid brahmacāriṇi ।।

grāmād yathoktaṃ bāhyena sthaṇḍile agniṃ praṇīya tu । nityenopasamādhāya saṃskṛtya juhuyādd haviḥ ।।

aupagavyā vyāhṛtayaḥ sāvitrī śāntir eva ca । vrātapatyaḥ samāsau ca tanmantrāṃhomucaiḥ saha ।।

kūṣmāṇḍyaḥ kāmasūktaṃ ca brahmavatyo atha devatāḥ । vratādeśe tathotsarge homaḥ kṣīrodanaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।

utsarge kāmasūktaṃ ca pūrvāṃ cāhutim uddharet । nivedya vrātapatyo ante idāvatsara eva ca ।।

āvartanāntaṃ sāmānyaṃ vyāhṛtyādy ubhayor api । etat sāmāsikaṃ proktam ādeśoddīkṣaṇaṃ budhaiḥ ।।

vrateṣu dakṣiṇā dhenuḥ kalyāṇī taruṇī ca yā । anaḍvān vā dhuraṃdharas tatsamaṃ vāpi kāñcanam ।।

sāvitryā atha vedasya kalpānāṃ tadanantaram । mailaṃ mailottaraṃ caiva ṣaṣṭhaṃ saṃmitam ucyate ।।

ṣaḍvrataṃ brāhmaṇaṃ vidyāt trivrataṃ kṣatriyaṃ viduḥ । dvivratas tu bhaved vaiśya etad ācāryaśāsanam ।।

viṣāsahiṃ sahamānam agnir mā goptā o cit sakhāyam ita eta udāruhan dhanur hastād etad ā roha candramā apsv iti ।।

om āṅgirasānām ādyaiḥ pañcānuvākaiḥ svāhā ।।

ṣaṣṭhāya svāhā ।।

saptamāṣṭamābhyāṃ svāhā ।।

nīlanakhebhyaḥ svāhā ।।

haritebhyaḥ svāhā ।।

kṣudrebhyaḥ svāhā ।।

paryāyikebhyaḥ svāhā ।।

prathamebhyaḥ śaṅkhebhyaḥ svāhā ।।

dvitīyebhyaḥ śaṅkhebhyaḥ svāhā ।।

tṛtīyebhyaḥ śaṅkhebhyaḥ svāhā ।।

upottamebhyaḥ svāhā ।।

uttamebhyaḥ svāhā ।।

uttarebhyaḥ svāhā ।।

ṛṣibhyaḥ svāhā ।।

śikhibhyaḥ svāhā ।।

gaṇebhyaḥ svāhā ।।

mahāgaṇebhyaḥ svāhā ।।

sarvebhyo aṅgirobhyo vidagaṇebhyaḥ svāhā ।।

pṛthak sahasrābhyāṃ svāhā ।।

brahmaṇe svāhā ।।

brahmajyeṣṭhā saṃbhṛtā vīryāṇi brahmāgre jyeṣṭhaṃ divam ā tatāna । bhūtānāṃ brahmā prathamo atha jajñe tenārhati brahmaṇā spardhituṃ kaḥ ।।

ātharvaṇānāṃ caturṛcebhyaḥ svāhā ।।

pañcarcebhyaḥ svāhā ।।

ṣaḍarcebhyaḥ svāhā ।।

saptarcebhyaḥ svāhā ।।

aṣṭarcebhyaḥ svāhā ।।

navarcebhyaḥ svāhā ।।

daśarcebhyaḥ svāhā ।।

ekādaśarcebhyaḥ svāhā ।।

dvādaśarcebhyaḥ svāhā ।।

trayodaśarcebhyaḥ svāhā ।।

caturdaśarcebhyaḥ svāhā ।।

pañcadaśarcebhyaḥ svāhā ।।

ṣoḍaśarcebhyaḥ svāhā ।।

saptadaśarcebhyaḥ svāhā ।।

aṣṭādaśarcebhyaḥ svāhā ।।

ekanaviṃśarcebhyaḥ svāhā ।।

viṃśatiḥ svāhā ।।

mahatkāṇḍāya svāhā ।।

tṛcebhyaḥ svāhā ।।

ekarcebhyaḥ svāhā ।।

kṣudrebhyaḥ svāhā ।।

ekānṛcebhyaḥ svāhā ।।

rohitebhyaḥ svāhā ।।

sūryābhyāṃ svāhā ।।

vrātyābhyāṃ svāhā ।।

prājāpatyābhyāṃ svāhā ।।

viṣāsahyai svāhā ।।

maṅgalikebhyaḥ svāhā ।।

brahmaṇe svāhā ।।

brahmajyeṣṭhā saṃbhṛtā vīryāṇi brahmāgre jyeṣṭhaṃ divam ā tatāna । bhūtānāṃ brahmā prathamo atha jajñe tenārhati brahmanā spardhituṃ ka iti ।।

oṃ varṇān pūrvaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ prākṛtā ye ca vaikṛtāḥ । śrutinirvacanāt sarve vivadante vivṛttiṣu ।।

vṛttiḥ karaṇaṃ varṇānāṃ karṇayos tu śrutir yathā । śrutipradeśād vimatas tad yathā varṇa ucyate ।।

samānasaṃdhyakṣarāṇi sparśā antaḥsthā ūṣmāṇaḥ । etair anye na dṛśyante etāvān varṇasaṃcayaḥ ।।

[yeṣāṃ ca śrutisaṃhitāyāṃ vibhāge asadṛśī syāt ।। tān eva varnān virudrādaye ca pradise kṛtaḥ] ।।

ye varṇābhyāṃ śrūyante ca yeṣāṃ nāsti vibhāgataḥ । mānasāṃś cāpi saṃgrāhyān upadeśena vartayet ।।

krāntān bahir nidhānasya yamāṃś cānanunāsikān । savyākṣepaṃ tato varṇān upadeśena vartayet ।।

iti varṇāḥ svarāḥ proktās teṣām ādyāś caturdaśa । samānākṣarāṇy ucyante śeṣaḥ saṃdhyakṣarāṇi tu ।।

anavarṇasvaro nāmi kādayo vyañjanaṃ smṛtam । pañcaviṃśatir ādyaiṣāṃ sparśā vargāś ca pañcakāḥ ।।

catvāro yādayo antaḥsthāḥ śādir ūṣmāṣṭako gaṇaḥ । ayogavāhā vartante teṣām ādyāḥ pṛthagvidhāḥ ।।

visarjanīyo anusvāro jigvāmūlīya [ity adhaḥ] । upadhmānīya ity ete catvāro atha pare yamāḥ ।।

nāsikyābhinidhānau ca vidyate yena pūraṇam । pañcaṣaṣṭir iyān vāco rāśir yo vedalokayoḥ ।।

mukhanāsike ye varṇā ucyante te anunāsikāḥ । samānāsyaprayatnā ye te savarṇā iti smṛtāḥ ।।

hrasvo avarṇaparas tasya savarṇasya ca vācakaḥ । hrasvottaras tu dīrgho api tasmāt tasmāt tasyaiva vācakaḥ ।।

vargāntaras tu vargādir vargasya grāhako mataḥ । vargāṇāṃ ca yathāsaṃkhyaṃ prathamāditvam iṣyate ।।

akāreṇocyate atas tu kāro yasmāt paro bhavet । tasya tad grahaṇaṃ bodhyaṃ kakāro atra nidarśanam ।।

vyañjanaṃ ghoṣavatsaṃjñam antaḥsthā haḥ parau yamau । trayastrayaś ca vargāntyā agoṣaḥ śeṣa ucyate ।।

śaṣasāś ca yamau dvau ca dvitīyāḥ prathamāś ca ye । aghoṣā vyañjanaśeṣaṃ ghoṣavad dṛśyate budhaiḥ ।।

ataḥ sthānāni varṇānāṃ kaṇṭho avarṇahakārayoḥ । vosarjanīya ai au ca svādyayor mātrayoḥ smṛtaḥ ।।

śeṣas tālvoṣṭhayor bodhyaḥ sa yathāsaṃkhyam iṣyate । dvisthānaṃ yamayoś cāpi vargāntyānāṃ ca śiṣyate ।।

jihvāmūlām ṛvarṇasya kavargasya ca bhāṣyate । yaś caiva jihvāmūlīya lvarṇaś ceti ca smṛtaḥ ।।

tālv eyaśacavargāṇām ivarṇasya ca bhāṣyate । mūrdhā sthānaṃ ṣakārasya ṭavargasya tathā mataḥ ।।

dantā lasatavargāṇām uvarṇas tv oṣṭhya ucyate । upadhmānīya okāro vaḥ pavargaś ca tathā matāḥ ।।

nāsikye nāsikā sthānaṃ tathānusvāra iṣyate । yamā vargottamāś cāpi yathoktaṃ caiva te matāḥ ।।

rephasya dantamūlāni pratyag vā tebhya iṣyate । iti sthānāni varṇānāṃ kīrtitāni yathākramam ।।

apara āha । hanumūle tu rephaḥ syād dantamūleṣu vā punaḥ । pratyag vā dantamūlebhyo mūrdhanya iti cāpare ।।

uraḥstho ghoṣo visṛṣṭaḥ kaṇṭhadeśe nihanyate । tato nādo vitiṣṭhate tasya vikṛtir akṣaram ।।

pūrvābhir aṇumātrābhiḥ kaṇṭhyaṃ saṃsevyate akṣaram । uttarābhis tu mātrābhir mukhavikṛtir ucyate ।।

api prayogasya hetoḥ saṃyogaḥ saha dhāryate । avyavahito akṣareṇa nānāvarṇaḥ svarodayaḥ ।।

dvitīyeṣu tathoṣmaṇāṃ tṛtīyeṣu ca ghoṣāṇām । caturtheṣu ghoṣoṣmaṇām upadeśena vartayet ।।

uttameṣu tu nāsikyam antaḥstheṣu ghoṣaṃ smṛtam । hakārasya ghoṣoṣmāṇāv upadeśena vartayet ।।

ṛkārākṣarayo repham aṇumātra sarva । svaritasya dvaidhībhāve upadeśena vartayet ।।

ṛvarṇadeśasaṃdeho asvaraḥ syāt syād anantaram । paro vā yadi vā pūrvo repham eva tu viddhi tam ।।

akāraś ca ikāraś ca ukāra ṛkāra eva ca । hrasvadīrghaplutāḥ sarve lvarṇe nāsti dīrghatā ।।

ekāraś ca tathāikāra okāra aukāra eva ca । dīrghamātraplutās teṣāṃ saṃjjā saṃdhyakṣarāṇi ca ।।

udāttaś cānudāttāś ca svaritāḥ kampitāś ca ye । anunāsikās tathā śuddhā dṛśyate hrasvatā budhaiḥ ।।

varṇāḥ pañcaṣaṣṭiḥ svarā dvāviṃśatiḥ samānākṣarāṇi caturdaśa aṣṭau saṃdhyakṣarāṇy ekonaviṃśatir nāminas tricatvāriṃśad vyañjanānisparśāḥ pañcaviṃśatiś catvāras tv antaḥsthāḥ catvāro yamāś cāṣṭāv ūṣmāṇo ayogavāhā daśāyogavāhā daśa ।।

om atharvaṇe namaḥ ।।

[pacati । pacate । aśanaśi । sisrate । gameḥ । vāyi । cāyi ।। vyāpi । cakri । devā caṣṭe । ava cākaśat । vyānaśe । triṣi niṣāmayatyoḥ । yoṣṭiḥ sapte ca ।। riñjati] । vaśmi । vaśmi । uśmasi । ava veti । vāñchati । veṣṭi । vanoti । juṣate । haryati । ācake । uśik । manyate । achāntsuḥ ।। chantsat । cākanat । cakamānaḥ । kanati । kāniṣat । kāme ।।

mimeti ।। nardati । dhvanati ।।

dhvaṃsate । [kṛṇati । kiṃśakte ।।] vanati । bhanati । [starṣati ।] sphūrjati ।।

hlādate । [nirṛte ।] hlādayati ।।

śabdayati ।।

arcati । arcati । rebhati । gāyati । jalpati । stobhati । stauti । yauti । rauti । nauti । gadati । nadati । bhanati । bhanate । [tatrate ।] paṇate । paṇasyati । paṇāyate । bhandate । [yatrasyate kṛkṛmdhampāt] kṛpaṇyati । dhamati । sapati । papṛkṣāḥ । gūrdhayati । vedayati । vādayati ।। valgūyati । mahayati । mantrayate । sevate । pṛcchati ।। chandati । śaśamānaḥ । jarate । [charati ।] venati । vandate ।।

irajati । irajyati ।।vidhema । duvasyati । namasyati । vivāsati । ṛdhnoti । ṛṇaddhi । ṛcchati ।।

pari srava । parisrava ।। pavasva । abhy arṣa । āśiṣaḥ ।।

īmahe । īmahe । yāmi । manmahe । daddhi । pūrdhi । śagdhi । mimīhi । rirīhi । ririḍhḍhi । mimiḍhḍhi । pīparat । yantāraḥ । iṣudhyati । vanemahi । manāmahe । yācate ।।

dāsati ।। dāśati । śikṣati । mahate । pṛṇāti । rāti । rāsati । prāti । tuñjati । [matsyati ।] dadāti ।।

yryṣyati । uruṣyati ।। piparti । pārayati । pāti । pāsati । prāti । tuñjati । pṛṇāti । rakṣe ।।

ā vayati । bharvati । babhasti । venati । veti । veveṣṭi । aviṣyan । [praga] psāti । bapsati । bhasathaḥ । babdhām । [vadati । ādeti । tirati । tviṣyati । hinoti । vṛddheḥ ।।] [utpapīti । utpapīti ।। ।। tapati । pippahu । sahoti । yugbhidī bhedayojanayoś ca ।।] heḍate । heḍate ।। bhāmate । hṛṇīyate । bhrīṇāti । bhreṣate । dodhati । heḍaḥ । haraḥ । hṛṇiḥ । tyajaḥ । bhāmaḥ । manyuḥ । krodhe nāmāni ca krodhasya ।।

śnathati । śnathati ।। [dovati । kurvati ।] tūrvati । [manuṣyati । dhanuṣyati ।] śṛṇāti । mṛṇāti । bhṛjjati । amati । tṛṇeḍhi । dabhnoti । [śūṣati ।] dhvarati । dhūrvati । kṛntati । śvasati । snehayati । mṛdnāti । [sradhnāti ।] dāsati । stṛṇute । starate । [kṛṇāti ।] ni tojati । ni vapati । [amati । riti ।] yātayate । ākhaṇḍala । taḍit । hiṃsāyām ।।

inaddhi । inaddhi ।। svarati । hṛṣyati । pathati । sṛjati । jyotate । dyotate । [dyopyate ।] bhrājate । bhrāśate । dīdayati । sādhate । dyumat । jamat । kalmalīkinam । malmalābhavan । jañjaṇābhavan । arciḥ । śociḥ । tapaḥ । tejaḥ । haraḥ । sṛṅgāṇi । jvalejvalataś ca nāmāni ।।

sūrkṣati । [rādale । cvyucchati । ra prasāde । śarulipsāyām । mukṣati ।] sādare । [vyucchati । apramāde । śarulipsāyām । vyākhadi । pṛthagbhāve oṣadhikicchrajīvane । daśasyati । drohe । pīyati । spardhāyām । vakṣati । nivāse । iṣṭāti । svādane ।।

[dānapanuparivasyate ।। ।। rodasī । rodhasī । kṣoṇī । svadhe । puraṃdhī । ṛtāvṛtau । prapitve । pratiṣṭhe । praśasye । urūcī । [sāntāpe] । rajasī । viṣāṇe । dhiṣṇye । gabhīre । gambhīre ।। ।। oṇyau । caṃvau । naptyau । naptyau ।। ।। pārśvau । dūre ante । anante । dyāvāpṛthivyoḥ ।।

apaḥ । apaḥ ।। apnaḥ । daṃsaḥ । vepaḥ । [vedaḥ ।] veṣaḥ । viṣṭvī । vratam । karvaram । śakma । kratuḥ । karaṇāni । karāṃsi । karikrat । karantī । cakrat । kartum । kartā । kartave । [thalita । hiṃsāyām । inaddhi ।] dhīḥ । savaḥ । śamī । śaktiḥ । śilpam । karmaṇaḥ ।।

araṇaḥ । araṇaḥ ।। garaḥ । kṣodaḥ । kṣadma । nabhaḥ । ambhaḥ । kabandham । salilam । vāḥ । vanam । ghṛtam । madhu । purīṣam । pippalam । kṣīram । viṣam । retaḥ । śakam । jahma । bṛbūkam । busam । tugryāḥ । sukṣemam । varuṇaḥ । surā । ararindrāni । dhvasmanvat । jāmi । āyudhāni । kṣapaḥ । ahiḥ । akṣarāḥ । tṛptiḥ । rasaḥ । saraḥ । payaḥ । bheṣajam । sravaḥ । śavaḥ । sahaḥ । ojaḥ । sukham । kṣatram । āvayāḥ । śubham । yādaḥ । bhūtam । bhuvanam । bhaviṣyat । āpaḥ । mahat । vyoma । yaśaḥ । sarṇīkam । [svarṇīkaram ।] gahanam । gabhīram । [gambhīram ।] gahvaram । kam । annam । [su] haviḥ । sadma । sadanam । ṛtam । [ṛta] yoniḥ । ṛtasya yoniḥ । satyam । nīram । rayiḥ । sat । pūrṇam । sarvam । akṣitam । sarpiḥ । apaḥ । pavitram । amṛtam । induḥ । hema । sargāḥ । śambaram । abhvam । vapuḥ । ambu । toyam । tūyam । kṛpīṭam । akṣaram । kṣarāḥ । vāri । jalam । [cūrṇāḥ । saṃstyānāḥ । dhānāpyam ।] visrutam । jalāṣam ।। karburam । kāṣṭhāḥ । [idam] idam । śukram । medhyam । pāvakam । pāvanam । hrādanam । hlādanam । [pārvam ।] ambhaḥ । [bhūrī ।] udakasya ।।

avanayaḥ । avanayaḥ ।। yahvyaḥ । khāḥ । sīrāḥ । srotyāḥ । enyaḥ । dhunayaḥ । rujānāḥ । vakṣaṇāḥ । khādo arṇāḥ । rodhacakrāḥ । haritaḥ । yoṣitaḥ । svasṛtaḥ । arṇavāḥ । sindhavaḥ । kulyāḥ । vahāḥ । urvyaḥ । irāvatyaḥ । pārvatyaḥ । ojasvatyaḥ । sarasvatyaḥ । harasvatyaḥ । ajirāḥ । mātaraḥ । nadīnām ।। [madhuḥ । vathaḥ] kāṭaḥ । kāṭaḥ । khātaḥ । avataḥ । avaṭaḥ । kriviḥ । sūdaḥ । utsaḥ । ṛśyadaḥ । kārotaraḥ । kuśayaḥ । kevataḥ । [trapuḥ] kūpasya ।।

[khare । svāram । suṣṭi ।] nu । nu । makṣu । dravat । oṣam । jīrāḥ । jūrṇiḥ । śūrtāḥ । śūghanāḥ । śībham । tṛṣu । tūyam । tūrṇiḥ । ajiram । bhuraṇyuḥ । āśu । prāśu । tūtujānaḥ । tūtujiḥ । tujyamānāsaḥ । ajrāḥ । sācīvit । dyugat । tājat । taraṇiḥ । vātaraṃhā । kṣiprasya ।।

āryaḥ । āryaḥ । rāṣṭrī । niyutvān । inaḥ । īśvarasya ।।

saṃyogaḥ । saṃyogaḥ । āśuśukṣaṇiḥ । jahā । śitāma । mehanā । mūṣaḥ । mandū । īrmāntāsaḥ । [vājarāndhyam ।] kāyamānaḥ । vidradhe । tugvani । [nodhāt । nadaḥ ।] cyavanaḥ । kaśyapaḥ । nū cit । akūpārasya । aprāyuvaḥ । rajaḥ । juhure । krāṇā । viṣuṇaḥ । jāmiḥ । jasuriḥ । cayase । andhaḥ । dugdham । āhanaḥ । nadaḥ । arkaḥ । sacā । cit । pavitram । pṛthujrayāḥ । kāṇukā । adhriguḥ । āṅgūṣaḥ । āpāntamanyuḥ । śmaśā । vājagandhyam । [jarādhya ।] pākasthāmā kaurayāṇaḥ । vrandī । niṣṣapī । kṣumpam । nicumpuṇaḥ । [majāyema । dhṛruḥ ।] joṣavākam । kuṭasya । kepayaḥ । salalūkam । askṛdhoyuḥ । niśṛmbhāḥ । [dhruvadrakṣam ।] upalaprakṣiṇī । upasi । savīmani । vidathāni । śrāyanta iva । amūraḥ । vijāmātuḥ । amavān । amīvā । amatiḥ । riśādasaḥ । ānuṣak । girvaṇāḥ । amyak । yādṛśmin । śurudhaḥ । apratiṣkutaḥ । dvibarhāḥ । urāṇaḥ । javāru । tatanuṣṭim । ilībiśaḥ । [irāviṇaḥ ।] kiyedhāḥ । turīpam । pratadvasū । diviṣṭiṣu । dūtaḥ । ṛcīṣamaḥ । anarśarātim ।। anarvā । [anarvā । cāṇḍā । vālhā] jaḍhavaḥ । bakuraḥ । [vaktāraḥ] bekanāṭān । abhi dhetana । sadānve । parāśaraḥ । karūḍatī । danaḥ ।।

ikṣuṇā । kīlālam । vijāmni । doṣā । [aṣṭamartyaḥ] ।। jyeṣṭham । [jyeṣṭham । asipakva ।] viśvāhā । vivasavān । vāte । [tanyantaḥ । vrālma । kāmpīvakaṃsam । jasyatyam । jalālī ।] andhaḥ । vipaśyan । ayā ciṣṭhā । [āṃsā । rantu । tamāyīvayaḥ ।] śamopyāt । gulphaḥ । biṣkale khargalā । pratodaḥ । vedaḥ । [yatrāsmannataḥ । radhraḥ । cikriḥ । nuluḥ ।] pucchadhau । [suniḥ ।] apāṣṭhaḥ । medī । [jyenā ।] maryaḥ । [saptaghnetaḥ ।] vālini । yātāram । [ruṣaṃkiḥ । siktaḥ ।] sagaṇāḥ । [muḍimnānā । liṅgakāḥ । nādinā ।] malvaḥ । amnaḥ । [juguḥ ।] nīlāgalasālā । ailabaḥ । [daridraḥ ।] nīlalohitaḥ । śvāpadaḥ । kunakhī । kurīram । [upasaḥ ।] tāduri । [kamatha । rumathā । sarvartebhyaḥ । idam । adhvaryuḥ । dyumnī । kuvitaḥ । damnanā ।] duroṇe । [parektauti] । titau । [utpavādhata ।] kimīdī । vāmasya । ekacakram । amatiḥ । sumatiḥ । [dayate । dayanti । vrīhi । vṛtte] ।। īḍe । īḍe । kṣayati । tapati । rajati । anekārthāḥ ।।

prapitve । abhīke । prāptasya ।।

tiraḥ । sataḥ । aprāptasya ।।

tvaḥ । nemaḥ । ardhasya ।।

ṛkṣāḥ । stṛbhiḥ । iti nakṣatrāṇām ।।

vamrībhiḥ । upajihvikā । sīmikānām ।।

rambhaḥ । [rathaḥ ।] pinākam । iti daṇḍasya ।।

śepaḥ । vaitasaḥ । iti puṃsprajananasya ।।

[paraṃgativilīke] । iti strīprajananasya ।।

anena । anayā । [panasya]] maki । hvakir] । iti pratiṣedhasya ।।

varūtham । [asagram] । carmaṇo arutsāhasya ।।

paṇiḥ prakalavid vaṇijaḥ ।।

śvaghnī । kitavasya । akṣadhūrtasya ।।

[mṛṇyaḥ] । sīmikasya ।।

kuṭasya । kuliśaḥ ।।

agniḥ । jātavedāḥ । vaiśvānaraḥ । draviṇodāḥ । vanaspatir iti sūktabhāñji ।।

idhmaḥ । [viṣṇuḥ ।] tanūnapāt । narāśaṃsaḥ । devīr dvāraḥ । uṣāsānaktā । daivyā hotārā । tisro devīḥ । tvaṣṭā । vanaspatiḥ । svāhākṛtaya iti nipātabhāñji ।।

indraḥ । viṣṇuḥ । somaḥ । parjanyaḥ । ṛtuḥ । agnāyī । pṛthivī । iḍā । bhṛgavaḥ । atharvāṇa iti saṃstavikās tasyaikavad bahuvat strīvac ca ।।

vahanam devānāṃ yac ca dāeṣṭiviṣayikaṃ tad asya karma ।।

ayaṃ lokaḥ । vasantaḥ । prātaḥsavanam । gāyatrī trivṛd rathaṃtaram iti tadbhaktīni ।।

vāyuḥ । varuṇaḥ । indraḥ । rudraḥ । parjanyaḥ । bṛhaspatiḥ । brahmaṇaspatiḥ । vāstoṣpatiḥ । kṣetrasya patiḥ । kaḥ । yamaḥ । apāṃ napāt । mitraḥ । viśvakarmā । manyuḥ । tārkṣyaḥ । dadhikrāḥ । sarasvān । agniḥ । asunītiḥ । vājaḥ । kutaḥ । vātaḥ । ṛtaḥ । mṛtyuḥ । dhātā । vidhātā । purūravāḥ । gandharvāḥ । anaḍvān । prāṇāḥ । stambhaḥ । vrātya iti sūktabhāñji ।।

prajāpatiḥ । candramāḥ । somaḥ । induḥ । aditiḥ । dhenavaḥ । ahir budhnya iti nipātabhāñji ।।

sarasvatī । vāk । aditiḥ । urvaśī । gauḥ । dhenuḥ । saramā । uṣā । indrāṇī । pṛthivī । dasya । godhukasā । virāṭ । aghnyā । sinīvālī । kuhūḥ । anumatiḥ । rākā । yamī । saraṇyūḥ । pathyā । rodasī । devapatnyaḥ । marutaḥ । rudrāḥ । ṛbhavaḥ । aṅgirasaḥ । bhṛgavaḥ । atharvāṇa iti saṃstavikās tasyaikavad bahuvat strīvac ca ।।

snehānupradānaṃ vṛtravadho yā cakā ca balakṛtis tad asya karma ।।

antarikṣalokaḥ । grīṣmaḥ । madhyaṃdinaṃ savanam । triṣṭup pañcadaśaḥ । bṛhad iti tadbhaktīni ।।

ādityaḥ । savitā । bhagaḥ । sūryaḥ । pūṣā । viṣṇuḥ । keśī । viśvānaraḥ । vṛṣākapiḥ । kālaḥ । brahmacārī । rohita iti sūktabhāñji ।।

dadhyaṅ । atharvā । yamaḥ । aja ekapāt । manuḥ । vivasvān । dakṣaḥ । aryamā । vaiśvānaraḥ । suparṇa iti nipātabhāñji ।।

uṣāḥ । sūryā । vṛṣākapāyī । sādhyāḥ । vasavaḥ । ādityā । sapta ṛṣayaḥ । vājinaḥ । viśve devā iti saṃstavikās tasyaikavad bahuvat strīvac ca ।।

raśmibhiś ca rasādhāraṇaṃ yac ca tad asta karma ।।

asya lokaḥ । varaṣās । tṛtīyasavanam । jagatī । saptadaśaḥ । vairūpām iti tadbhaktīni ।।

eteṣām eva lokānām ṛtuchandaḥstomapṛṣṭhānām ānupūrveṇa bhaktiśeṣo anukalpo devatādvandve ca pūrvasyāparaḥ saṃstavikaḥ ।। pūrvasyāparaḥ saṃstavikaḥ ।। ।।

om athātaś caraṇavyūhaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ।।

tatra catvāro vedā bhavanti । ṛgvedo yajurvedaḥ sāmavedo brahmavedaś ceti ।।

tatra ṛgvedasyārthaśāstram upavedaḥ । yajurvedasya dhanurvedopavedaḥ । sāmavedasya gāndharvavedopavedaḥ । brahmavedasyāyurvedopavedaḥ । abhicārakārthaśāstram ity ucyate ।।

ṛgveda ātreyasagotro agnir devatā । yajurvedaḥ kāśyapasagotro vāyur devatā । sāmavedo bhāradvājasagotro viṣṇur devatā । brahmavedo vaitāyanasagotro brahmā devatā ।।

athāta ṛgvedaḥ pītavarṇaḥ padmapattrākṣaḥ suvibhaktagrīvaḥ kuñcitakeśaśmaśruḥ supratiṣṭhitajānujaṅghaḥ । pramāṇena sa vitastayaḥ pañca ।।

tatra ṛgvedasya sapta śākhā bhavanti । tad yathā । āśvalāyanāḥ । śāṅkhāyanāḥ । sādhyāyanāḥ । śākalāḥ । bāṣkalāḥ । audumbarāḥ । māṇḍūkāś ceti ।।

teṣām adhyayanam । ṛcāṃ daśa sahasrāṇi ṛcāṃ pañca śatāni ca । ṛcām aśītiḥ pādaś ca etat pāraṇam ucyate ।।

tatra yajurvedasya caturviṃśatir bhedā bhavanti ।। tad yathā । kāṇvāḥ । mādhyaṃdināḥ । jābālāḥ । śāpeyāḥ । śvetāḥ । śvetatarāḥ । tāmrāyaṇīyāḥ । paurṇavatsāḥ । āvaṭikāḥ । paramāvaṭikāḥ । hauṣyāḥ । dhauṣyāḥ । khāḍikāḥ । āhvarakāḥ । carakāḥ maitrāḥ । maitrāyaṇīyāḥ । hāritakarṇāḥ । śālāyanīyāḥ । marcakaṭhāḥ । prācyakaṭhāḥ । kapiṣṭhalakaṭhāḥ । upalāḥ । taittirīyāś ceti ।।

teṣām adhyayanam । dve sahasre śate nyūne vede vājasaneyake । sakalaṃ parisaṃkhyātaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ tu caturguṇam ।।

aṣṭādaśa śatāni bhavanti । tāny eva triguṇam adhītya kramapāro bhavati । saptasu vīrāś ceti ।।

śākhās tisro bhavanti । tad yathā । vārcikam arthādhyayanīyāḥ । pāraścaryāḥ । pāraśramaṇīyāḥ । pārakramavaṭaḥ । kramapāraś ceti ।।

ṣaḍ aṅgāny adhītya ṣaḍaṅgavid bhavati । śikṣā kalpo vyākaraṇaṃ niruktaṃ chando jyotiṣam iti ṣaḍ aṅgāni ।।

atha yajurvedaḥ prāṃśuḥ pralambajaṭharaḥ sthūlagalakapālo rakto varṇena prādeśāḥ ṣaḍ dīrghatvena yajurvedasyaitad rūpaṃ bhavati ।।

tatra sāmavedasya śākhāsahasram āsīd anadhyāyeṣv adhīyānāḥ sarve te śakreṇa vinihatāḥ । [pravilīnās] tatra ke cid avaśiṣṭāḥ pracaranti । tad yathā । rāṇāyanīyāḥ । sādyamugrāḥ । kālapāḥ । mahākālapāḥ । kauthumāḥ । lāṅgalikāś ceti ।।

kauthumānāṃ ṣaḍ bhedā bhavanti । tad yathā । sārāyaṇīyāḥ । vātarāyaṇīyāḥ । vaitadhṛtāḥ । prācīnās tejasāḥ । aniṣṭakāś ceti ।।

teṣām adhyayanam । aṣṭau sāmasahasrāṇi sāmāni ca caturdaśa । sohyāni sarahasyāni etat sāmagaṇaṃ smṛtam ।।

atha sāmavedaḥ suvarcāḥ sugandhis tejasvī mṛduvaktā brahmaṇyaḥ pralambabāhur duścarmī kṛṣṇo varṇena kātaraḥ svareṇeti ।।

ṣaḍaratniḥ pramāṇena ca smṛtaḥ । stuvanty ṛṣayo brahmā sāmāni tiṣṭhati saṃnidhau sa bhagavān sāmavedo maheśvarabhaktaḥ ।।

tatra brahmavedasya nava bhedā bhavanti । tad yathā । paippalādāḥ । staudāḥ । maudāḥ । śaunakīyāḥ । jājalāḥ । jaladāḥ । brahmavadāḥ । devadarśāḥ । cāraṇavaidyāś ceti । teṣām adhyayanam । ṛcāṃ dvādaśa sahasrāṇy aśītis triśatāni ca । paryāyikaṃ dvisahasrāṇy anyāṃs caivārcikān bahūn ity etadgrāmyāraṇyakāni ṣaṭ sahasrāṇi bhavanti ।।

tatra brahmavedasyāṣṭāviṃśatir upaniṣado bhavanti । muṇḍakā praśnakā brahmavidyā kṣurikā cūlikā atharvaśiro atharvaśikhā garbhopaniṣan mahopaniṣad brahmopaniṣat prāṇāgnihotraṃ māṇḍukyaṃ nādabindu brahmabindu amṛtabindu dhyānabindu tejobindu yogaśikhā yogatattvaṃ nīlarudraḥ pañcatāpinī ekadaṇḍī saṃnyāsavidhiḥ aruṇiḥ haṃsaḥ paramahaṃsaḥ nārāyaṇopaniṣad vaitathyaṃ ceti ।।

tatra gopathaḥ śataprapāṭhakaṃ brāhmaṇam āsīt tasyāvaśiṣṭe dve brāhmaṇe pūrvam uttaraṃ ceti ।।

tatra ṣaḍ aṅgāny adhītya ṣaḍaṅgavid bhavati ṣaḍ aṅgāni bhavanti, śikṣā kalpo vyākaraṇaṃ niruktaṃ chando jyotiṣam iti ।।

pakca kalpā bhavanti । nakṣatrakalpo vaitānakalpas tṛtīyaḥ saṃhitāvidhiḥ । caturtha āṅgirasaḥ kalpaḥ śāntikalpas tu pañcamaḥ ।।

lakṣaṇagranthā bhavanti । caturādhyāyikā prātiśākhyaṃ pañcapaṭalikā dantyoṣṭhavidhir bṛhatsarvānukramaṇī ceti ।।

tatra dvāsaptatiḥ pariśiṣṭāni bhavanti kauśikoktāni । kṛttikārohiṇī । rāṣṭrasaṃvargaḥ । rājaprathamābhiṣekaḥ । purohitakarmāṇi । puṣyābhiṣekaḥ । piṣṭarātryāḥ kalpaḥ । ārātrikam । ghṛtāvekṣaṇam । tiladhenuḥ । bhūmidānam । tulāpuruṣaḥ । ādityamaṇḍakaḥ । hiraṇyagarbhaḥ । hastirathaḥ । aśvarathaḥ । gosahasradānam । hastidīkṣā । aśvadīkṣā । vṛṣotsargaḥ । indrotsavaḥ । brahmayāgaḥ । skandayāgāḥ । saṃbhāralakṣaṇam । araṇilakṣaṇam । yajñapātralakṣaṇam । vedilakṣaṇam । kuṇḍalakṣaṇam । samillakṣaṇam । sruvalakṣaṇam । hastalakṣaṇam । jvālālakṣaṇam । lakṣahomaḥ । kāṅkāyanokto bṛhallakṣahomaḥ । koṭihomaḥ । gaṇamālā । ghṛtakambalam । anulomakalpaḥ । āsurīkalpaḥ । ucchuṣmakalpaḥ । samuccayaprāyaścittāni । brahmakūrcavidhiḥ । paiṭhīnasitaḍāgavidhiḥ । pāśupatavratavidhiḥ । saṃdhyopāsanavidhiḥ । snānavidhiḥ । tarpaṇavidhiḥ । śrāddhavidhiḥ । agnihotravidhiḥ । uttamapaṭalam । varṇapaṭalam । nighaṇtuḥ । caraṇavyūhaḥ । candraprātipadikam । grahayuddham । grahasaṃgrahaḥ । rāhucāraḥ । ketucāraḥ । ṛtuketulakṣaṇam । kūrmavibhāgaḥ । maṇḍalāni । digdāhalakṣaṇam । ulkālakṣaṇam । vidyullakṣaṇam । nirghātalakṣaṇam । pariveṣalakṣaṇam । bhūmikampalakṣaṇam । nakṣatragrahotpātalakṣaṇam । utpātalakṣaṇam । sadyovṛṣṭilakṣaṇam । gośāntiḥ । adbhutaśāntiḥ । svapnādhyāyaḥ । atharvahṛdayam । bhārgavīyagārgyabārhaspatyośanasādbhutāni । mahādbhutāni bṛhatsarvānukramaṇī ceti ।।

tatra pañcadaśopaniṣado bhavanti । muṇḍakā । praśnakā । brahmavidyā । kṣurikā । cūlikā । atharvaśiraḥ । atharvaśikhā । garbhopaniṣat । mahopaniṣat । brahmopaniṣat । prāṇāgnihotram । māṇḍūkyam । vaitathyam । advaitam । alātaśāntiś ceti ।।

tatra brahmavede aṣṭādaśa vratāni cariṣyan sāvitrīvratam । vedavratam । vedottaravratam । mailavratam । mailottaravratam । mṛgāravratam । rohitavratam । viṣāsahivratam । yamavratam । śāntivratam । śikhivratam । gaṇavratam । śirovratam । śikhāvratam । marudvratam । adhivratam । aṅgirovratam । pāśupatavrataṃ caret ।।

kṛcchram । taptakṛcchram । atikṛcchram । sarvakṛcchram । maundabhāyaḥ । tulāpuruṣaḥ । sāṃtapanam । mahāsāṃtapanaṃ ceti ।।

yo vai brahmavedeṣūpanītaḥ sa sarvavedeṣūpanito yo vai brahmavedeṣv anupanītaḥ sa sarvavedeṣv anupanītaḥ ।।

anyavede dvijo yo brahmavedam adhītukāmaḥ sa punar upaneyo devāś ca ṛṣayaś ca brahmāṇam ūcuḥ ।।

ko no [smo] jyeṣṭhaḥ । ka upanetā । ka ācāryaḥ । ko brahmatvaṃ ceti ।।

tān brahmābravīt ।।

atharvā vo jyeṣṭho atharvopanetātharvācāryo atharvā brahmatvaṃ ceti ।।

tad apy etad ṛcoktam । brahmajyeṣṭheti etayā । iti tasyārhaṃ brahmavedaś caturṇāṃ vedānāṃ sāṅgopāṅgānām [tam] savākovākyānāṃ setihāsapurāṇānām ।।

athāto brahmavedaḥ kapilo varṇena tīkṣṇaḥ pracaṇḍaḥ kāmarūpī viśvātmā jitendriyaḥ । sa tasmin bhagavati durvārajvālaḥ । kṣudrakarmā sa ca bhagavān brahmavedaś caturmukho dvipakṣo dānto dharmī balavān prājñaḥ kṛtotthāpanīyaḥ krūraḥ ṣaḍrātrāṇi vimṛśī [ṣaḍrātrāṇi ṣaḍ] vaitāyano gotreṇa ya ekaikasmin vedānāṃ nāmavarṇagotrarūpapramāṇaṃ ca kīrtayed yo vidvān jātismaro bhavati mṛtaḥ sa brahmalokaṃ gacchati ।।

oṃ vṛttaṃ prātar amāvāsyāṃ paścād dṛśyeta candramāḥ । tasya varṇaṃ gatiṃ rūpaṃ sthānaṃ caivoccanīcatām ।।

hrāsavṛddhiṃ ca śṛṅgāṇāṃ nakṣatraṃ yac ca yojayet । tāni lakṣeta somasya varṣāvarṣaṃ bhayābhayam ।।

prathame darśane tv indoḥ samāsādya yadā graham । uttaraṃ vardhate śṛṅgaṃ nīcībhavati dakṣiṇam ।।

evam eva śraviṣṭhābhyas teṣām ante ca candramāḥ । udyacched dakṣiṇaṃ śṛṅgaṃ nīcībhavati cottaram ।।

anupaśyeta rāṣṭraṃ ca antargirimahāgirim । vidarbhān madrakāṃś caiva bharatāṃś cāpi sarvataḥ ।।

sārāṇāṃ vijarāṇāṃ ca samudre ye ca dakṣiṇe । etāñ janapadān hanti yadā syād uttaronnataḥ ।।

kāśmīrān daradān darvāñ śūrasenān yayāvarān । śālvānāṃ ca virājānāṃ samudre ye ca paścime ।।

etāj janapadān hanti yadā syād dakṣinonnataḥ । puruṣaḥ strīnṛpaṃ hanti aparānto vinaśyati ।।

bālhikān yavanakāmbojāñ śālvān madrān uśīnarān । godhāṃś ca bhadrakāṃś caiva madhyaṃ ca kurubhiḥ saha ।।

saurāṣṭrān sindhusauvīrān vāneyāṃś cāpi siṃsakān । kṣudrakān mālavān matsyān mlecchān saha pulindakaiḥ ।।

śastropajījikuḍyāṃś ca brāhmaṇā yodhinaś ca ye । etāñ janapadān hanti somaḥ puruṣalakṣaṇaḥ ।।

lakṣaṇād vā bhavet sthūlaḥ kāye śṛṅge ca hīyate । alpe śarīre durbhikṣaṃ bhayaṃ rogaṃ vinirdiśet ।।

yadā pratipadaś candraḥ prakṛtyā vikṛto bhavet । anudbhinno vilūno vā rājamṛtyuṃ vinirdiśet ।।

ṣaṣṭhyāṃ madhyaṃ yadā gacched rājā vadhyeta pārthivaḥ । avantīnāṃ ca pūrvārdhaṃ māgadhāś ca viśeṣataḥ ।।

paraṃ kumāreṣv aṣṭamyāṃ rājānaṃ daśamī param । evaṃ ca pakṣāpacaye madhye dṛśyeta dvādaśī ।।

hanti pañcanadaṃ tatra rājānaṃ sumahadbalam । sarvāṃś ca kuryād rājñas tu tasminn utpātadarśane ।।

adbhutāni ca dṛśyante tasminn utpātadarśane । vaiśvānarapathaṃ prāptaḥ samudram api śoṣayet ।।

kṛttikānāṃ maghānāṃ ca rohiṇyāś ca viśākhayoḥ । eteṣām uttaro mārgo rājavīthīti tāṃ viduḥ ।।

yadīmaṃ mārgam āsthāya candramā vinivartate । nāvarṣā uttamā jñeyā yogakṣemaṃ tathaiva ca ।।

gajavīthīṃ nāgavīthīṃ yadi gacchati candramāḥ । govīthīti tadāpy āhur gargasya vacanaṃ yathā ।।

aṣṭau sthānāni candrasya kroṣṭukir yāni veda vai । nausthāyī lāṅgalī caiva tṛtīyaś cottaronnataḥ ।।

daṇḍasthāyī caturthas tu daṇḍaśāyī tu pañcamaḥ । ṣaṣthas tu yūpasthāyī syāt pārśvaśāyī tu saptamaḥ ।।

aṣṭamo avāṅśirāś caiva phalam asya nibodhata । rājānaḥ sveṣu rāṣṭreṣu yuktadaṇḍāḥ praśāsati ।।

lāṅgalī grasate lokān yugāntaṃ pratipādayet । mārīṃ samadhikām āhur yadā syād uttaronnataḥ ।।

daṇḍasthāyī tv amātyānāṃ bhayaṃ rogaṃ vinirdiśet । śaktichedā granthichedā gostenāḥ pāradārikāḥ ।।

ete deśān vilumpanti daṇḍasthāyī yadā bhavet । daṇḍaśāyī tu viprāṇāṃ bhayaṃ tatra vinirdiśet ।।

yūpasthāyī tu dhānyānāṃ bhayaṃ tatra vinirdiśet । harite śarīre somasya paśūnāṃ vadham ādiśet ।।

kṛṣṇe śarīre somasya śūdrāṇāṃ vadham ādiśet । pīte śarīre somasya vaiśyānāṃ vadham ādiśet rakte śarīre somasya rājñāṃ tu vadham ādiśet । śukle śarīre somasya brahmavṛddhiṃ vinirdiśet ।।

snigdhaḥ pītaḥ suvarṇābhaḥ pakṣādau yadi candramāḥ । gosthāyī saṃpradṛśyeta vipravṛddhiṃ vinirdiśet ।।

uccasthāne yadā pītaḥ samaśṛṅgaḥ śaśī bhavet । nāgavīthīgataḥ snigdhaḥ sa sarvaguṇapūjitaḥ ।।

dhūmrābho lāṅgalasthāyī śrīmān salakṣmamaṇḍalaḥ । pakṣādau yadi dṛśyeta brahmakṣatrasukhāvaḥ ।।

rājavīthīṃ tu saṃprāpta ugradaṇḍī yadā bhavet । haridrākuṅkumābhaś ca śmaśānam avalokayet ।।

mṛtyuṃ saṃyojayet somo bālākṛtir avāṅchirāḥ । lākṣārudhirasaṃkāśo dhanuḥsthāyī yadā bhavet ।।

saṃgrāmaṃ yojayet somo loke tu tumulaṃ bhayam । dvicandraṃ gaganaṃ dṛṣṭvā brūyād brahmavadho mahān ।।

dvau sūryau vā yadā syātāṃ tadā kṣatravadho mahān । dṛṣṭvā tu caturaḥ sūryān uditān sarvatodiśam ।।

śastreṇa janamāreṇa tad yugāntasya lakṣaṇam । āditye pāṇḍuraṃ chattraṃ saṃdhyāvelāṃ yadā bhavet ।।

deśasya vidravaṃ sūryo rājamṛtyuṃ vinirdiśet । ādityasya rathaḥ śvetaḥ saṃdhyāvelāṃ yadā bhavet ।।

pratyāsannaṃ bhayaṃ vidyāt tasminn utpātadarśane ।।

ādityaḥ sarvataś chinno dvaidhībhutaḥ pradṛśyate deśasya vidravaṃ sūryo rājamṛtyuṃ vinirdiśet ।।

kṣemaṃ vikukṣile brūyāt sthālīpiṭharasaṃsthite । saṃkṣipte kṣīyate loko durbhikṣaṃ vajrasaṃsthite ।।

divā hy asmin pataty ulkā satataṃ kampate mahī । aparvāśaninirghoṣāḥ saṃdhyā ca jvalanacchavā ।।

nakṣatrapātasyotpattir dhūmasya rajaso api vā । śṛṅgaṃ bhavaty ādityasya tṛṇakāṣṭhaṃ ca śuṣyati ।।

rājāno hy aśivās tatra citraṃ varṣati mādhavaḥ । dvādaśānāṃ tu māsānāṃ madhye naśyati pārthivaḥ ।।

kārttikyāṃ śuklapakṣasya bahulasya trayodaśīm । vidyāt tu svātisaṃpātaṃ divasān ekaviṃśatim ।।

saptāhaṃ tu bhaved goṣu saptāhaṃ mṛgapakṣiṣu । mānuṣeṣu ca saptāhaṃ tataḥ śreyas tu kalpayet ।।

oṃ ke cid grahā nārarān āśrayante ke cid grahā [jyotiṣi] saṃgrahe ca । graho graheṇaiva hataḥ kathaṃ syād vijñāya tattvaṃ bhagavān bravītu ।।

evaṃ sa pṛṣṭo munibhir mahātmā provāca gargo grahayuddhatantram । parājayaṃ caiva jayaṃ ca teṣāṃ śubhāsubham caiva jagaddhitāya ।।

arko jātaḥ kaliṅgeṣu yavaneṣu ca candramāḥ । aṅgārakas tv avantyāyāṃ magadhāyāṃ budhas tathā ।।

bṛhaspatiḥ saindhaveṣu mahārāṣṭre tu bhārgavaḥ । śanaiścaraḥ surāṣṭrāyāṃ rāhus tu giriśṛṅgajaḥ । ketur malayake jāta ity etad grahajātakam ।।

yasmin deśe tu yo jātaḥ sa grahaḥ pīḍyate yadā taṃ deśaṃ ghātitaṃ vidyād durbhikṣeṇa bhayena vā ।।

divākaraś caiva śanaiścaras tathā bṛhaspatiś caiva budhaś ca nāgarāḥ । prajāpatiḥ ketur athāpi candramās tathaiva rāhūśanasau ca yāyinaḥ ।।

yadā graho nagara eva nāgaraṃ vijeṣyate yāyy atha vāpi yāyinam । tadā nṛpo nāgara eva nāgaraṃ vijeṣyate vāyy atha vāpi yāyinam ।।

ārohaṇaṃ ca bhedaś ca lekhanaṃ savyadakṣiṇam । raśmisaṃsarjanaṃ caiva grahayuddhaṃ caturvidham ।।

prasavye vigrahaṃ brūyāt saṃgrāmaṃ raśmisaṃgame । lekhane amātyapūḍā syād bhedane tu janakṣayaḥ ।।

sarveṣāṃ nabhasi samāgame grahāṇām uktṛṣṭo bhavati tathaiva raśmivān yaḥ । snigdhatvaṃ bhavati tu yasya [sa graho graheṇa] saṃyukto bhavati [tu yaḥ] parājayeta śeṣaḥ ।।

śyāmo vā vyapagataraśmimaṇḍalo vā rūkṣo vā vyapagataraśmivān kṛśo vā । ākrānto vinipatitas tato apasavyo vijñeyo hata iti sa graho graheṇa ।।

budhaś ca bhaumaḥ śanibhārgavāṅgirāḥ pradakṣiṇaṃ yāti yadā niśākaram । anamayatvaṃ triṣu saukhyam uttamaṃ viparyaye cāpi mahāñ janakṣayaḥ ।।

dhanakanakarajatasaṃcayāś ca sarve śamadamamantraparāś caye manuṣyāḥ । śakayavanatukhārabālhikāś ca kṣayam upayānti divākarasya ghāte ।।

atha some hate vidyād dhrvaṃ rājño viparyayaḥ । saṃharanti ca bhūtāni bhūmipālāḥ pṛthakpṛthak ।।

parasparaṃ virudhyante kṣudbhayaṃ cāpi dāruṇām । anāvṛṣṭibhayaṃ ghoraṃ vidyāt somaviparyaye ।।

traigartāḥ kṣitipatayaḥ sayodhamukhyāḥ pīḍyante girinilayāgnijīvinaś ca । saṃgrāmāḥ sarudhirapāṃsuvarṣamiśrā durbhikṣaṃ bhavati dharāsutasya ghāte ।।

sāgaranilayāḥ paurāḥ kṣayam upayānti narā vaṇikpradhānāḥ । bhavati tu [rājā] vijayī prayāyī budhabandhane prapatanti cātra sobhyāḥ ।।

daivajñās tapasi ciraṃ suniścitārthāḥ syur dāntā nṛpatigaṇaḥ purohitāś ca । āgantur jayati vadhaś ca nāgarāṇāṃ trailokyam bhayam upaiti guros tu ghāte ।।

yo rājā prathitaparākramaḥ pṛthivyāṃ vaṅgāṅgādiṣu madadhāḥ saśūrasenāḥ । ye yodhāḥ samaraṇabhumilabdhaśabdās te sainyaiḥ kṣayam upayānti śukraghāte ।।

mahiṣakavṛṣabhāḥ sabhasmapauṇḍrāḥ kṛṣipaśupālyaratāś ca ye manuṣyāḥ । vividhabhayasamāhitās tu sarve kṣayam upayānti śanaiścarasya ghāte ।।

ye ke cin nṛpatiṣu dāmbhikāḥ piśācāḥ kāryāṇāṃ vrataniyameṣu channapāpāḥ । ye cānye śabarapulindacedigādhā bādhyante yadi bhavate atra rāhughātaḥ ।।

ākrāntaṃ samanubhavanti yāyisaṃghā vadhyante yadi bhavate [paras] paro ahighātaḥ । saṃgrāmāḥ sarudhirapāṃsuvarṣamiśra durbhikṣaṃ bhavati tu ketupīḍanena ।।

yat kiṃ cid divigatam antarikṣajaṃ vā bhaumaṃ vā bhavati nimittam apraśastam । tat savaṃ stanitamahābhrabidyudvarṣaiḥ śāntaṃ syād bhavati sadakṣiṇaiś ca homaiḥ ।।

ye deśā grahagaṇabhinnabhūmikampā yeṣāṃ vā graha upayātacandrasūryaḥ । tān deśān [grahagaṇabhinnabhumikampān] parjanyaḥ śamayati saptarātravṛṣṭyā ।।

prasavyas triṣu māseṣu saṃsargo māsikaḥ smṛtaḥ । lekhane pakṣa ity āhur bhedane saptarātrikam ।।

āgneyā vāsavāś caiva vāyavyā vāruṇās tathā । sarva eva śubhā jñeyā gargasya vacanaṃ yathā ।।

om atharvāṇaṃ namaskṛtya uvāca bhagavān ṛṣiḥ । kīdṛśā grahaputrāś ca kiyanto vā vadasva me ।।

pṛṣṭaha sa śaunakenātha brāhmaṇānāṃ hitāya vai । saṃkhyām uvāca bhagavān padmayonimataṃ yathā ।।

dikcāriṇo divicarā bhūcarā vyomacāriṇaḥ । divācarā rātricarā divārātricarāś caye ।।

pṛthikcarāś ca ye tatra te ca syuḥ saṃghacāriṇaḥ । caranty aparavīthīṣu ye ca vibhrāntamaṇḍalāḥ ।।

te grahāḥ saṃgraheṇāhaṃ śataśo atha sahasraśaḥ । anekavidhasaṃsthānaṃ pravakṣyāmy anupūrvaśaḥ ।।

gokṣīrakumudaprakhyās tīvreṇa vapuṣānvitāḥ । caranty antaravīthīṣu snigdhā vipulatejasaḥ ।।

ete visarpakā nāma arciṣmanto mahāprabhāḥ । vijñeyāś caturaśītiḥ śukraputrā mahāgrahāḥ ।।

śuklā nikarāḥ saurābhās tyajanta iva cārciṣaḥ । sphuranta iva cākāśe bimbakā raśmibhir vṛtāḥ ।।

prāyaśo dakṣiṇe mārge nīcair vibhrāntamaṇḍalāḥ । vikacāḥ pañcaṣaṣṭis te bṛhaspatisutāḥ smṛtaḥ ।।

ye śvetāḥ kiṃcid ākṛṣṇā viśikhāḥ syur vitārakāḥ । te ṣaṣṭiḥ kanakā nāma śanaiścarasutā grahāḥ ।।

ekapakcāśato jñeyās taskarāḥ sūkṣmaraśmayaḥ । baudhāḥ kamalagarbhābhāḥ kiṃcit pāṇḍuratejasaḥ ।।

kauṅkumā lohitāṅgasya putrā vidrumatejasaḥ । triśikhā vā tribhāgā vā ṣaṣṭir ity uttare pathi ।।

nānādhūmanibhā rūkṣā dhūmavyākularaśmayaḥ । śatam ekādhikaṃ mṛtyoḥ putrāḥ syur dhūmaketavaḥ ।।

kṛṣṇābhāḥ kṛṣṇaparyantāḥ kaluṣākṛtiraśmayaḥ । rāhoḥ putrās trayas triṃśad grahās tāmasakīlakāḥ ।।

nānāvarṇāgnisaṃkāśā jvālāmālā visarpiṇaḥ । viśvarūpāḥ sutā agner grahā viṃśaṃ śataṃ smṛtam ।।

aruṇās tu sutā vāyor dāruṇāḥ saptasaptatiḥ । vāteritā bhramantīva rūkṣā vikīrṇaraśmayaḥ ।।

tārāpuñjapratīkāśās tārāmaṇḍalasaṃvṛtāḥ । prājāpatyā grahās tv aṣṭau gaṇakā nāmanāmataḥ ।।

catvāras tārajā yuktāḥ sūkṣmāṇo rūparaśmayaḥ । brahmasaṃtānakā nāma dve śate caturuttare ।।

vaṃśagulmapratīkāśā [vaṃśagulmasaraśmayaḥ] । kākatuṇḍanibhābhiś ca raśmibhiḥ kiṃcid āvṛtāḥ ।।

udakaṃ cotsṛjantīva snigdhatvāt saumyadarśanāḥ । ete nāmnā smṛtāḥ kaṅkās triṃśad dvau vāruṇā grahāḥ ।।

muṇḍatārāḥ kabandhābhā rukmakeśāś ca raśmayaḥ । kālaputrāḥ kabandhās te smṛtāḥ ṣaṇṇavatir grahāḥ ।।

arciṣmāṃś ca prabhāsaś ca romaśo viṣamāṃs tathā । asnigdhāś cātikāyāś ca kiṃśuko rājasāyakaḥ ।।

ṛṣakaiś caiva rādhātaḥ kumudaḥ phanako ghanaḥ । eṣām aśveti vijñeyā ārās tu parisarpakāḥ ।।

nakṣatracāriṇo hy ete bhṛguputrā mahābalāḥ । pāṇḍurābhiḥ sudīrghābhiḥ śikhābhiḥ śītaraśmayaḥ ।।

atisaṃtānakāś tv anye ṣaṣṭir vāyoḥ sutā grahāḥ । vikesarāḥ prakāśante kṛṣṇalohitaraśmayaḥ ।।

miśrībhūtās tu te jñeyā guṇṭhitā iva reṇunā । dhūmaketoḥ sutā jñeyāḥ śatam ekādhikaṃ ca tat ।।

atyarthaṃ kanakās tv anye prataptakanakaprabhāḥ । antakaputrakāḥ ṣaṣṭir asnigdhā madhyacāriṇaḥ ।।

ye tu nakṣatravaṃśasya bhāgam uttaram āśritāḥ । ekatārā vapuṣmanto mahākāyāḥ prabhānvitāḥ ।।

vyālakasya tu ye putrāḥ saptaṣaṣṭiḥ samantataḥ । nāmato adhikacā nāma tattvajñaiḥ parikīrtitāḥ ।।

saṃtānakanibhā ye tu dṛśyante sūkṣmaraśmayaḥ । ekatārā dvitārā vā atha vā pañcatārakaḥ ।।

brahmarāśes tu te putrā grahāḥ saṃtānasaṃsthitāḥ । saṃcaranti nabhaḥ sarvam utpanne puruṣakṣaye ।।

aṇavo lohitās tv anye prakāśante adhikeśakāḥ । pañcaṣaṣṭis tu te jñeyāḥ prājāpatyā grahāḥ smṛtāḥ ।।

pariveṣeṣu jāteṣu grahāṇāṃ maṇḍaleṣu ca । dṛśyante kārmukā nāma saptatyekā samāḥ smṛtāḥ ।।

adharmasaṃbhavās tv anye caturdaśa parikramāḥ । adhaḥśikhāḥ prakāśante vivarṇā ghoratārakāḥ ।।

karṇachidraprātīkāśāḥ kṛṣṇās te tārakākṛtau । kīlakā rāhuputrās tu candrasūryatalāśrayāḥ ।।

vajraḥ kavandhas triśirāḥ śaṅkhabhedī śikhāvataḥ । daṇḍāś ca rāhuputrāḥ syur nāmabhis tulyavarcasaḥ ।।

yathā somārkayor jyoter maṇḍalābhyāśasevinaḥ । rājanyatvāt pradṛśyante prajānāṃ saṃkṣayāvahāḥ ।।

tatra mandaphalā jñeyāḥ śaśāṅkatalasevinaḥ । divākaratalābhyāśaṃ sevino bhṛśadāruṇāḥ ।।

pannagās tu caturviṃśat kṛṣṇā dvātriṃśatir grahāḥ । dakṣiṇādyāsu vīkṣyante nīcair vibhrāntamaṇḍalāḥ ।।

kevalaṃ tārakākārā dṛśyante niḥprabhaprabhāḥ । pītaraktā grahāḥ pañca pūrvadakṣiṇataḥ smṛtaḥ ।।

dakṣiṇāparataś cāpi pītaraktau grahau smṛtau । uttarāparatas tv ekaḥ pītarakto grahaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।

aiśānyāṃ śvetaraktābha ekas tiṣṭhati sūryakaḥ । yaḥ saṃdhivelāsv arkābho dikṣu sarvāsu dṛśyate ।।

nātidūre raveḥ snigdhaḥ sa varṣāyābhayāya ca । yavakrītoṣaraibhyāś ca nāradaḥ sarvatas tathā ।।

karṇaś ca raibhyasya putrau cārvāvasuparāvasū । saptaite sthāvarā jñeyāḥ saha sūryeṇa sarpiṇaḥ ।।

sthāvarāṇāṃ narendrāṇāṃ prācyānāṃ pakṣam āśritāḥ । svastyātreyo mṛgavyādha ṛmucuḥ pramṛcus tathā ।।

prabhāsaś candrabhāsaś ca tathāgastyaḥ pratāpavān । dṛḍhavratas triśaṅkuś ca ajau vaiśvānare mṛḍaḥ ।।

aruṇaś ca danuś caiva yāmyāyāṃ sthāvarāḥ smṛtāḥ । gautamo atrir vasiṣṭhaś ca viśvāmitras tu kaśyapaḥ ।।

ṛcīkaputraś ca tathā bharadvājaś ca vīryavān । ete sapta mahātmāna udīcyāṃ sthāvarāḥ smṛtāḥ ।।

śiśumāreṇa sahitā dhruveṇa ca mahātmanā । pulastyaḥ pulahaḥ somo bhṛgur aṅgirasā saha ।।

hāhāhūhū ca vijñeyau viṣṇoś ca padam uttamam । madhyāntasthāvarāṇāṃ tu niyatāv iti buddhimān ।।

kūṭasthānāni sarvāṇi dikṣv etāny upadhārayet । prabhānvitāni śvetāni snigdhāni vimalāni ca ।।

arciṣmanti prasannāni tāni kuryuḥ prajāhitam । niḥprabhāṇi vivarṇāni nirarcīmṣy amalāni ca ।।

hrasvāny asnehayuktāni na bhāvāya bhavanti hi । yat kiṃcit sthāvaraṃ loke tat prasanneṣu vardhate ।।

kūṭastheṣv aprasanneṣu sthāvaraṃ parihīyate । ādityaś caiva śukraś ca lohitāṅgas tathaiva ca ।।

rāhuḥ somaḥ śanaiścaro bṛhaspatibudhau tathā । aindra āgneyo yāmyaś ca nairṛto vāruṇas tathā ।।

vāyavyaś caiva saumyaś ca brāhmaś caivāṣṭamo grahaḥ । navamaś caiva vijñeyo dhūmaketur mahāgrahaḥ ।।

yugagrahā na cānye te tatrāṣṭau diggrahāḥ smṛtāḥ । sanakṣatreṣu mārgeṣu dṛśyante tu yugagrahāḥ ।।

vibhrāntamaṇḍalāḥ śeṣā dṛśyante khacarā grahaḥ । mṛtyor niśvāsajāś cānye jñeyāḥ ṣoḍaśa ketavaḥ ।।

kūṣmāṇḍavad visaṃchannas triṇavā dakṣiṇe pathi । ekādaśaiva vijñeyā dvādaśādityasaṃbhavāḥ ।।

sūryavarcanirīkṣās te tejodhātumayā grahāḥ । dakṣayajñe tu rudrasya krodhād anye tu niḥsṛtāḥ ।।

bhīmarūpā daśaikaś ca jvalāṅkuśadharā grahāḥ । sapta paitāmahās tv anye tiryaggā jarjaragrahāḥ ।।

śikhāḥ sṛjanto vitatās tantuśuklapaṭopamāḥ । śvetaketava ity anye vyākhyātā daśa pañca ca ।।

uddālakarṣiputrās te nīcair vibhrāntamaṇḍalāḥ । te syuḥ śvetaśikhāḥ sarve saumyāḥ kāntās tanuprabhāḥ ।।

aṣṭādaśendunā sārdhaṃ mathyamāne purāmṛte । ketavaḥ kundapuṣpābhāḥ kṣīrodanabhasi smṛtāḥ ।।

viraśmayaś ca viśikhā mahākāyā nirarciṣaḥ । raupyakumbhanibhāḥ saumyā grahāḥ syuḥ śītatejasaḥ ।।

brahmakopamayas tv eko viśvātmā sarvato grahaḥ । caturyugānte lokānām udayas tasya vidyate ।।

nakṣatrapatham utsṛjya nabhoaṃśāḥ pārśvacāriṇaḥ । pūrvato abhyuditā vā syur nīcair uttaratas tathā ।।

bhūmyām abhyuditā vā syur hrasvasnehapariplutāḥ । sarva eva tu vijñeyā grahā mandaphalodayāḥ ।।

sarveṣāṃ paitṛkaṃ karma prajābhāgyodbhavaṃ mahat । sarve te sarvato hanyur aśubhaṃ yad vadanti ca ।।

tatkarmajanmamāhātmyaṃ śīlābhijanam eva ca । tadrūpāṃs tadguṇāṃś cāpi tanmayāṃs tatparigrahān ।।

sarva eva rogapradā mṛtyuśastrāgnitaskaraiḥ । paśusasyopaghātaiś ca hanyur anyaiś ca kāraṇaiḥ ।।

dhūpanāt sparśanāt sthānād udayāstamasaṃbhavāt । hanyuḥ pañcavidhaṃ sarve ketavo nātra saṃśayaḥ ।।

mṛdudhruvograkṣipreṣu sādhāraṇacareṣu ca । dāruṇeṣu ca ṛkṣeṣu sādhāraṇacareṣu ca । dāruṇeṣu ca ṛkṣeṣu vidyāt tatsadṛśaṃ phalam ।।

yathādiṣṭaṃ yathāvarṇaṃ yathāvargaparigraham । sarva evoditā hanyuḥ sarva eva mahāgrahāḥ ।।

mṛtyoḥ kālasya sūryasya brahmaṇas tryambakasya ca । bhaumasya rāhor agneś ca prajātā ye sudāruṇāḥ ।।

prajāpateś ca dharmasya somasya varuṇasya ca । pītādyāś ca diśāṃ putrā vijñeyā mṛdudāruṇāḥ ।।

kaśyapasya ca marīcer uddālakaṛṣes tathā । putrā mandaphalā jñeyās teṣām amṛtasaṃbhavāḥ ।।

śukrādīnāṃ ca ye putrā grahāṇāṃ parikīrtitāḥ । teṣāṃ vīryāṇi jāniyāt pitṛbhyaḥ sādhikāni tu ।।

nāradātreyagargāṇāṃ guror uśanasas tathā । grahāṇāṃ saṃgraho hy evam eṣa kārtsnyena kīrtitaḥ ।।

anekaśatasāhasra anekaśatalakṣaṇaḥ । devalabdhavarākāśe prāha sarvān pṛthakpṛthak ।।

etadutthe tu sarvasmin bhaye atha samupasthite । mahāśāntiṃ prakurvīta rājā rāṣṭrasya rakṣaṇe ।।

tat prayāti śamaṃ sarvaṃ prajānāṃ tu sukhaṃ bhavet । rājāno muditās tatra pālayanti vasuṃdharām ।।

om upetya yaś candramasaṃ raviṃ vā gṛhṇāti sūnor asurasya putraḥ । nibodhataitasya śubhāśubhāni grahasya mṛtyoḥ praticeṣṭitāni ।।

yadā tu rāhuḥ śaśino raver [grahe] grahītukāmo bhavati prasahya । tadā karoty adbhutadarśanāni yair jñāyate rāhur upaiṣyatīti ।।

udvepate tadā candro yadā rāhuḥ pradṛśyate ।। pāṇḍur vā jāyate klībaḥ śaśo vāsya vivardhate ।।

rekhāntarāpurārāṇi kalmaṣāṇi divākare । vadanti ca bhaṛśaṃ śvāno vānti vātāś ca bhīṣaṇāḥ ।।

saṃdhyayor ubhayoś colkā gavāṃ prakṣīyate payaḥ । kṣīriṇām aiva vṛkṣāṇāṃ tad ahar naśyate payaḥ ।।

apsu snigdhāni dṛśyante kākābadhnanti maṇḍalam । ūrdhvaṃ vadati gomāyur yadā rāhuḥ pradṛśyate ।।

candragrahanimittāni śuklapakśāṣṭamīparam । ā paurṇamāsyā dṛśyeran sūryasya ca tathobhayoḥ ।।

udito gṛhyamāṇas tu hanti vedavido janān । bālāṃś ca jaṭilān hanti ye ca kāṣāyavāsasaḥ ।।

yauvanasthāṃś ca pūrvāhṇe hanti yajñavido janān । audakāni ca sarvāṇi nāgendrāś cātra duḥkhitāḥ ।।

atha madhyapathaṃ prāptaḥ śūdrān hanti ca taskarān । parivṛkto nṛpaṃ hanti candraś caraṇacāraṇān ।।

pralambaḥ pramadān hanti kṣatraṃ rāṣṭraṃ ca sarvaśaḥ । traigartāś cātra pīḍyante ye ca daṇḍabhṛto janāḥ ।।

uparakto yadodeti yadā vā pratitiṣṭhati । ayogakṣemam ādiśyet triṣu lokeṣu dāruṇam ।।

śāradaṃ trīṇi varṣāṇi sasyaṃ jātaṃ na pacyate । naidāghenātra jīvanti prajā mūlaphalena vā ।।

sarvaṃ saṃgrasate jyotiś ciram antardadhāti vā । hanti sphītāni rāṣṭrāṇi pradhānaṃ ca mahīpatim ।।

yadi rāhur ubhau śaśibhāskarau grasati pakṣam anantaram antataḥ । puruṣaśoṇitakardamavāhinī bhavati bhūr na ca varṣati mādhavaḥ ।।

gṛhītvā bhāskaraṃ pūrvaṃ gṛhṇāti śaśinaṃ yadi । taṃ tu somottaraṃ nāśas tatra rdhyante hi devatāḥ ।।

vayasāṃ maraṇaṃ chidre prakīrṇe rakṣasāṃ vadhaḥ । nāgānāṃ tu mahānāge chidre devo na varṣati ।।

śveto varṇo brāhmaṇānāṃ kṣatriyāṇāṃ tu lohitaḥ । vaiśyānāṃ pītako varṇaḥ śūdrāṇāṃ kṛṣṇa ucyate ।।

eteṣāṃ yena varṇena rāhuś carati bhāskare । yā jātis tasya varṇasya tāṃ sa pīḍayate grahaḥ ।।

śyāmo bhavati vātāya draukṣo bhavati vṛṣṭaye । haridraḥ sarvadhānyānāṃ kopaṃ sṛjati dāruṇam ।।

tāmro bhavati śastrāya śastrāya rūkṣo bhavati mṛtyave । bahvākāras tu bhūtānāṃ ghoraṃ janayate jvaram ।।

dhūmavarṇo agnivarṇo vā grāmeṣu nagareṣu vā । agnyutpātān gṛhasthānāṃ karotīha mahāgrahaḥ ।।

nīlalohitaparyanto rāhuś carati bhāskare । amātyo hanti rājānaṃ rājā vāmātyam ātmaha ।।

yasya rājñaś ca nakṣatre svarbhānur uparajyati । rājyabhraṃśaṃ suhṛnnāśaṃ maraṇaṃ cātra nirdiśet ।।

snigdhavarṇo yadārciṣmān parvasthaḥ snehavān grahaḥ । kṣipraṃ vāpy uditaṃ brūhi sarvabhūtabhayāya vai ।।

pradakṣiṇe tu somasya apasavye tu vigrahaḥ । raśmibhede bhayaṃ ghoram ullekhe mantriṇāṃ vadhaḥ ।।

darśayitvā tu rūpāṇi yadā rāhur na dṛśyate । śastradurbhikṣasaṃpātair bhayaṃ ghoraṃ vinirdiśet ।।

gṛhītāstamitayos tu na bhuñjīran dvijātayaḥ । ā punardarśanāt tābhyāṃ japahomau vivartayet ।।

candrasūryagrahe nādyād adyāt snātvā tu muktayoḥ । amuktayor astaṃgayor adyāt snātvā pare ahani ।।

tataḥ ṣaṭsu tataḥ ṣaṭsu tato adhyardheṣū vā punaḥ । ardhavarṣeṣu māseṣu ādityasya tato grahaḥ ।।

tataḥ ṣaṭsu tataḥ ṣaṭsu triṣu varṣeṣu vā punaḥ । etāvad eva rāhos tu cāram āhur manīṣiṇaḥ ।।

oṃ bhārgavas tu purovāca maharṣīn bhagavān ṛṣiḥ । ketusaṃcāraṃ śṛṇuta utthānaṃ caiva yādṛśam ।।

nimittani ca vakṣyāmitasyoktāni hi yāni tu । tāni sarvāṇi jāniyād utpātajñānakovidaḥ ।।

viprāñ śvetākṛtir hanti kṣatriyān hanti lohitaḥ । vaiśyāṃs tu pītako hanti śūdrān hanti tathāsitaḥ ।।

itarān pīḍayet ketur anyavarṇo yadā bhavet । ṣaṇmāsābhyantare rājño maraṇaṃ ca tadādiśet ।।

śvetaḥ śastrākulaṃ kuryāl lohitas tv agnito bhayam kṣudbhayaṃ pītakaḥ kuryāt kṛṣṇo rogam atholbaṇam ।।

yasmin deśe śiras tasya sa deśaḥ pīḍyate bhṛśam । madhye tu madhyamā pīḍā yato pucchaṃ tato jayaḥ ।।

śaktyākāro atināśāya duḥkhāya musalākṛtiḥ । dīrghaḥ sūkṣmaḥ sukhāyaiva hrasvaḥ sthūlo vināśakṛt ।।

utthānaṃ caiva ketūnāṃ vināśāyaiva hi smṛtam । tasmād ātharvaṇair mantraiḥ śamanam ārayed budhaḥ ।।

māhendrūn anṛtān raydrūn vauśvadevīm athāpi vā । utpāteṣu mahāśāntiṃ kārayed bahudakṣiṇām ।।

ārādhitāḥ śamaṃ yānti tadutpātā na saṃśayaḥ । homair japyaiś ca vividhair dānaiś cabahurūpakaiḥ ।।

tasya yatra śiro deśe tata utthāya vāvrajet । dhanaṃ vā sarvam utsṛjya mṛtyor mucyetā vā na vā ।।

dattvā vā pṛthivīṃ sarvāṃ rājā śāntiṃ niyacchati ।।

om ṛtuketūn pravakṣyāmi yathāvad anupūrvaśaḥ । yāvanto yasya putrāḥ syuḥ kuryur yac coditā divi ।।

sarve te dharaṇījātā māsā ye devanirmitāḥ । ādityaraśmibhir baddhāḥ saure tiṣṭhanti maṇḍale ।।

daśa vai vāruṇās tatra sūryaputrās tu viṃśatiḥ । caturviṃśatir āgneyā yamaputrā nava smṛtāḥ ।।

aṣṭādaśa ca kauberā vāyuputrās tu viṃśatiḥ । eṣā saṃkhyā tu ketūnāṃ śatam ekottaraṃ smṛtam ।।

śrāvaṇaprauṣṭhapadayor vāruṇāṃs tu vinirdiśet ।।

[ārādhitāḥ śamaṃ yānti tadutpātā na saṃśayaḥ । homair jāpaiś ca vividhair dānaiś ca bahurūpakaiḥ ।।] āvāhayet tato meghān pūrṇāṃ kuryād vasuṃdharām । unmattāḥ sarito yānti jalavegasamāhitāḥ ।।

dhānyaṃ samarghatāṃ yāti ītayo na bhavanti hi udaye vāruṇānāṃ tu etad bhavati lakṣaṇam ।।

aśvayuji kārttike ca sūryaputrān vinirdiśet । teṣāṃ caiva tu karmāṇi lakṣaṇaiḥ śṛṇu yādṛśaiḥ ।।

tato dahati dīptāṃśuḥ sarvānnāni divākaraḥ । mriyante ca tathā gāvaḥ śvāpadāś ca viśeṣataḥ ।।

viṣaṃ ca prabalaṃ tatra sarvadamṣṭriṣu dāruṇam । udaye sūryaputrāṇām etad bhavati lakṣaṇam ।।

mārgaśīrṣe ca pauṣe ca agniputrān vinirdiśet । teṣāṃ caiva tu karmāṇi lakṣaṇaiḥ śṛṇu yādṛśaiḥ ।।

agnir dahati rāṣṭrāṇi haritāni vanāni ca vidravanti tato deśāḥ samantād bhayapīḍitāḥ ।।

kasmiṃś cij jāyate kṣemaṃ kasmiṃś cij jāyate bhayam । udaye hy agniputrāṇām etad bhavati lakṣaṇam ।।

māghaphālbunayor madhye yamaputrān vinirdiśet । teṣāṃ caiva tu karmāṇi lakṣaṇaiḥ śṛṇu yādṛśaiḥ ।।

śīghraṃ bhavati durbhikṣaṃ hāhābhūtam acetanam । chardijvarātisārāś ca glāniś caivākṣivedanā ।।

udaye yamaputrāṇām etad bhavati lakṣaṇam ।।

caitravaiśākhayor madhye kauberāṃs tu vinirdiśet । teṣāṃ caiva tu karmāṇi lakṣaṇaiḥ śṛṇu yādṛśaiḥ ।।

ucchritair dhvajavedībhir ucchritair dhvajatoraṇaiḥ । havirdhūmākulā tatra dṛśyate vasudhā tadā ।।

triviṣṭapaṃ samāpannas tadā śakro mahīpatiḥ । evaṃ prajñās tu manyante kubere graham āgate ।।

udaye tu kuberāṇām etad bhavati lakṣaṇam ।।

jyaiṣṭhe caiva tathāṣāḍhe vāyuputrān vinirdiśet । teṣāṃ caiva tu karmāṇi lakṣaṇaiḥ śṛṇu yādṛśaiḥ ।।

vāyanti ca mahāvātā mahāyuddhaṃ mahābhayam । bhajyante ca mahāvṛkṣās toraṇāṭṭālakāni ca ।।

gṛhāṇi rāmaṇīyāni kṣayaṃ yānti jalāni ca । udaye vāyuputrāṇām etad bhavati lakṣaṇam ।।

ṛtugatam udayanam eṣāṃ mahaujasāṃ vāruṇādiketūnām । jānāti yaḥ phalaṃ ca protkṛṣṭāḥ saṃpadas tasya ।।

oṃ kṛttikārohiṇīsaumyaṃ madhyaṃ kūrmasya nirdiśet ।। śeṣān ṛkṣavibhāge tu trikaṃ prati vinirdiśet ।।

sāketamithile mekalālayāv ahichattranāgapuraṃ kāśipāriyātrakurupāñcālāḥ ।। atha kosalakauśāmbītīraṃ pāṭaliputraṃ kaliṅgapurapṛthivīmaṇḍalamadhye abhihate abhihanyāt ।।

aṅgavaṅgakaliṅgamāgadhamahendragavasam ambaṣṭhāḥ ।। bhāgāḥ pūrvasamudrāḥ śirasy abhihate abhihanyāt ।।

khaśabhadrā samataṭasamavardhamānakavaidehā gāndhārāḥ ।। kosalatosalaveṇātaṭasajjapurā mādreyatāmaliptā dakṣiṇapūrve hate abhihanyāt ।।

āvantyakā vidarbhā matsyā cakorabhīma[gam]rathā yavanavalayakāntīsiṃhalalaṅkuṇanāsikyakarmaṇoyāmimahi^narmadabhṛgukacchā dakṣiṇapaścād dhate abhihanyāt ।।

sahyagirivaijayantī kuṇkuṇanāsikyakarmaṇoyāmimahinarmadabhṛgukacchā dakṣiṇapaścād dhate abhihanyāt ।।

saurāṣṭrasindhusauvīramālavā rāmarāṣṭrakānvītān ।। ānartagacchayantrān pucche abhihate abhihanyāt ।।

sārasvatāṃs trigartān matsyān nānvārabālhikān ।। mathurāpuraṃgadeśān uttarabhāge hate abhihanyāt ।।

brahmāvartaṃ śatadruhimavantaṃ parvataṃ ca mainākaṃ kāśmīraṃ caiva tathā uttarapārśve hate abhihanyāt ।।

nepālakāmarūpaṃ ca videhodumbaraṃ tathā ।। tathāvantyaḥ kaikayaś ca uttarapūrve hate abhihanyāt ।।

viśākhe kṛttikāḥ puṣyaḥ pūrvau proṣṭhapadau tathā । bharaṇyaś ca maghāś caiva phalgunyau prathame tathā ।।

yady atra calate bhūmir nirghātolkāsta eva vā । aśarīrāś ca nardante kampante daivatāni ca ।।

ādityo vātra gṛhyeta somo vāpy uparajyate । āgneyaṃ tad vijānīyād durbhikṣaṃ cātra nirdiśet ।।

alpakṣīrās tathā gāvo agner vyādhiś ca jāyate । purāṇi deśā grāmāś ca pīḍyante hy agninā tadā ।।

pīḍyante cāgnikarmāṇo agniveśāś ca ye narāḥ । pittajvaras tathā śvāsaha prajāḥ pīḍayate tadā ।।

akṣirogās tathā ghorāḥ puruṣāṇāṃ viśeṣataḥ । āpagāś cātra śuṣyanti na ca sasyavatī mahī ।।

tapyate ca tadā bhūmir na ca devo abhivarṣati । nīlalohitaparyaktā aphalāḥ pādapās tathā ।।

durbhikṣaṃ marako vyādhiḥ paracakrabhayaṃ tathā । etai rūpais tu vijñeyam āgneyaṃ caladarśanam ।।

hasto aśvinyau tathā citrā ṛkṣam aryamadaivatam । brāhmaṃ mṛgaśiraḥ svātir vāyavyaṃ maṇḍalaṃ smṛtam ।।

yady atra calate bhūmir nirghātolkāsta eva vā । aśarīrāś ca nardante kampante daivatāni ca ।।

ādityo vātra gṛhyeta somo vāpy uparajyate । vāyavyaṃ tad vijānīyād akṣemaṃ cātra nirdiśet ।।

pāṃsuvarṣaṃ tadā ghoraṃ kṣīre sarpir na vidyate । prāsādatoraṇādīni prapatanti mahītale ।।

madrakā yavanāś caiva śakāḥ kāmbojabālhikāḥ । gandhārāś ca vinaśyanti etaiḥ sārdhaṃ tathā kila ।।

gajā vājina uṣṭrāś ca vṛkā nakulaceṭakāḥ । pīḍyante vyādhinā sarve ye ca śastropajīvinaḥ ।।

pure śreṣṭhā vinaśyanti gaṇeṣu guṇasaṃmitāḥ । gṛhāṇi ramaṇīyāni viśīryante ca sarvaśaḥ ।।

āyāsaś colbaṇas tatra śastrabhrāmaḥ samantataḥ । etai rūpais tu vijñeyaṃ vāyavyaṃ caladarśanam ।।

ārdrāśleṣās tathā mūlan pūrvāṣāḍhās tathaiva ca । vāruṇaṃ revatī caiva sūryadaivatyam eva ca ।।

yady atra calate bhūmir nirghātolkāsta eva vā । aśarīrāś ca nardante kampante daivatāni ca ।।

ādityo vātra gṛhyeta somo vāpy uparajyate । vāruṇaṃ tad vijānīyāt subhikṣaṃ cātra nirdiśet ।।

bahukṣīrās tathā gāvo nāgāś ca phalinas tathā । śāntārayaḥ prajāḥ sarvā gomino jaṅgalaṃ payaḥ ।।

jalopajīvinaḥ sarve prāpnuvanty ṛddhim uttamām । khecarāś cātra dṛśyante snigdhavarṇāḥ samantataḥ ।।

nyastaśastrāś ca rājāno brahmakṣatraṃ ca vardhate । etai rūpais tu vijñeyaṃ vāruṇaṃ caladarśanam ।।

jyeṣṭhānurādhā śravaṇaḥ śraviṣṭhāś ca punarvasū । prājāpatyam āṣāḍhāś ca māhendraṃ maṇḍalaṃ smṛtam ।।

yady atra calate bhūmir nirghātolkāsta eva vā । aśarīrāś ca nardante kampante daivatāni ca ।।

ādityo vātra gṛhyeta somo vāpy uparajyate । māhendraṃ tad vijānīyāt sukṣemaṃ cātra nirdiśet ।।

gāvaḥ samagravatsāś ca striyaḥ putrasamanvitāḥ । kīṭā vyālā mriyante ca ye cānye svedajantavaḥ ।।

vedādhyayanayajñeṣu brāhmaṇā niratāḥ sadā । viṭkṣatriyāḥ svakarmāṇaḥ śūdrāḥ śuśrūṣakārakāḥ ।।

viṃśatiśataṃ tv āgneyaṃ vāyavyaṃ navatiṃ calet । aśītiṃ calate tv aindraṃ vāruṇaṃ saptatiṃ calet ।।

āgneyo bhūmikampo yaḥ sa dvimāsād vipacyate । vāruṇas tu phalaṃ sadyo vāyavyas tu trimāsikaḥ ।। māhendrasya phalaṃ vidyān māsam ardhaṃ tathaiva ca ।।

om ata ūrdhvaṃ ca digdāhān kīrtyamānān nibodhata । yathā diśaḥ pradahyante tāsāṃ dāhaphalaṃ ca yat ।।

indro agnir marutaś caiva pradahanti diśo daśa । śubhāśubhāya lokānāṃ kṛtāntenābhicoditāḥ ।।

yadāstamita āditye vahner jvālā pradṛśyate diśāṃ dāhaṃ tu tad vidyād bhārgavasya vaco yathā ।।

nānārāgasamutthānāṃ nānāvidhaphalodayāḥ । pāṃśuneva ca saṃchannā digdāhāyogam āśritāḥ ।।

diśaḥ sarvāḥ pradahyante akṣemāya phalāya ca । avadāhād ṛte dāhaṃ yadi snigdhāḥ pradarśanāḥ ।।

tamodhūmarajaskā ye dīptadvijamṛgāvṛtāḥ । pradīptalakṣaṇāḥ satyāḥ sarva evāhitāvahāḥ ।।

tathā kanakakiṃjalkataḍitkalpāḥ śivāś ca ye । rūkṣāḥ kṛṣṇātha māñjiṣṭhā bandhujīvakavac ca ye ।।

śvetā raktāś ca pītāś ca dāhāḥ kṛṣṇāś ca varṇataḥ । brahmakṣatriyaviṭśūdravināśāya prakīrtitāḥ ।।

raktāḥ śastrabhayaṃ kuryur pītā vyādhiprakopanāḥ । agnivarṇās tathā kuryur agniśastrabhayaṃ mahat ।।

sapītaparuṣaśyāmā ye ca vāruṇasaṃnibhāḥ । sarva eva kṣudhārogamṛtyuśastrāgnikopanāḥ ।।

ṛtau tu varṣaṃ tīvraṃ syāt sainyavidravam eva ca । bhṛśam uddyotanī saṃdhyā kurute vā grahāgamam ।।

dikṣu dagdhāsu pīḍyante yathādig deśabhaktayaḥ । śakunajñānanirdiṣṭā ye ca tatrādhikārakāḥ ।।

yathoktā tu mahāśāntir yathoktavidhinā kṛtā । sarvaṃ digdāhajaṃ ghoraṃ śamayet sā sadakṣiṇā ।।

om ulkādayo hi nirdiṣṭā nirghātās tu purātra ye । teṣām idānīṃ vakṣyāmi viśeṣāṃs tu pṛthakpṛthak ।।

aṅgānām āntarikṣāṇāṃ yad aṅgam abhipūjitam । tad ulkālakṣaṇaṃ śrīmad aṅgaṃ kārtsnyena vakṣyate ।।

apradhṛṣyāṇi yāni syuḥ śarīrāṇīndriyair dṛḍhaiḥ । kṣamāvanti viśuddhāni satyavratarātāni ca ।।

tāny etāni prakāśante bhābhir vitimiraṃ nabhaḥ । samantāj jvalayantīha yasmād asukaraṃ nabhaḥ ।।

tāni bhāvakṣayād bhūyaḥ pracyutāni nabhastalāt । kṣitau salakṣaṇāny eva nipatantīha bhārgava teṣāṃ nipatatāṃ tatra yatrayatropalakṣyate । tatratatraiva vividhaṃ prajānāṃ jāyate bhayam ।।

rūpavarṇaprabhāsnehapramaṇākṛtisaṃgamaiḥ । teṣāṃ balābalaṃ jñātvā guṇadoṣaḥ pravakṣyate ।।

tārā dhiṣṇyās tatholkāś ca vidyuto aśanayas tathā । vikalpāḥ pañcadhā caiṣāṃ parasparabalottarāḥ ।।

tatra śabdenba mahatā visvareṇa vikarṣiṇā । mahācakram ivāgacchad āyatākṣā nabhastalāt ।।

manuṣyamṛgahastyaśvavṛkṣāśmapathaveśmasu । patanty aśanayo dīptāḥ sphoṭayantyo dharātalam ।।

sahasaivopapanneṣu bhṛśaṃ tadanuyāyinā । sattvavibhraṃśinātyarthaṃ śabdenodvegakāriṇā ।।

jvālābhāravisarpiṇyaḥ prakṛtyā duḥkhadarśanāḥ । vidyuto nipatanty āśu jīveṣu vanarāśiṣu ।।

tīkṣṇaśūlaviśālāgrā patantī cāpi vardhate । prakṛtyā pauruṣī tūlkā tasyā bhedān nibodhata ।।

kṛśā nārīva dīptā syāc chikhā sāṅgāravarṣiṇī । uddyotayantī gaganaṃ kāñcanenaiva varmaṇā ।।

pītena pāṇḍunā vāpi dhūmadhūmāruṇena vā । viśīryatā mahābhreṇa mahatā cānuṣaṅgiṇā ।।

vaṃśagulmanibhāś cāpi kāś cid indradhvajopamāḥ । kāś cid indrāyudhaprakhyāḥ kāś cin maṇḍalasaṃsthitāḥ ।।

chattravac cāpu dṛśyante cakravan nipatanti ca । daṇḍavac cāpi tiṣṭhanti pradhāvanti ca sarpavat ।।

prakīrṇena kalāpena khe gacchantīva barhiṇaḥ । abhyucchritena pucchena yāti kā cid dharātalam ।।

tejāṃsi vikiranty anyāḥ pradhāvanti ca golavat ।।

pranṛttapretamārjātavarāhānugatās tathā । sasvanā niḥsvanāś cāpi patanti dharaṇītale ।।

etāsāṃ phalam ulkānāṃ pravakṣyāmi pṛthakpṛthak । tantunaiva hi saṃbaddhā uhyamāneva vāyunā ।।

patantī dṛśyate kā cit kā cid bhramati cāmbare । ulkāsaṃghaiḥ parivṛtā kā cid yāti dharātalam ।।

sāmānyaṃ tu phalaṃ tāsāṃ tat samāsena vakṣyate । varāhapretaśārdūlasiṃhamārjāravārāiḥ ।।

tulyā bhayāvahā ulkā nikṛṣṭāhinibhā ca yā । śūlapaṭṭiśaśaktyṛṣṭimudgarāsiparaśvadhaiḥ ।।

vṛṣṭyākāreṇa tulyāś ca vṛkṣābhāś ca vigarhitāḥ । padmaśaṅkhenduvajrāhimatsyadhvajanibhāḥ śubhāḥ ।।

śrīvṛkṣasvastikāvārtahaṃsadviradavarcasaḥ । jvalitāṅgārasaṃkāśā jihmagā atha śīghragāḥ ।।

vinā pucchāvakāśena hrasvenātikṛśena vā । daśāntarāṇi dhanuṣaḥ pucchaṃ cāpi pradṛśyate ।।

ulkāvikāro boddhavyo dhiṣṇya ity abhisaṃjñitaḥ । yas tu śuklena varṇena vapuṣā pelavena vā ।।

padmatantunikāśena dhūmarājīnibhena vā । ulkāvikāraḥ so apy uktas tārakā nāmanāmataḥ ।।

evaṃ pañcavidhā hy etāḥ śaunakena prakīrtitāḥ । svargacyutānāṃ patatāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ puṇyakarmaṇām ।।

etāsām indraśirasi patanaṃ nṛpater bhayam । devatārcāsu patane rājarāṣṭrabhayaṃ bhavet ।।

puradvare purakṣobha indrakīle janakṣayaḥ । brahmāyatanaghāteṣu brāhmaṇānām upadravaḥ ।।

caityavṛkṣābhighāteṣu satkṛtyānāṃ mahad bhayam । dvāre cāyuḥkṣayaṃ vidyād gṛhe tu svāmino bhayam ।।

goṣṭheṣu gomināṃ vidyāt karṣakāṇāṃ khaleṣu ca । gṛheṣu rājñāṃ jānīyād bheṣu tadbhaktināṃ bhayam ।।

āśāgrahopaghāteṣu taddeśyānāṃ tapasvinām । adhomukhīnṛpaṃ hanyād brāhmaṇān ūrdhvagāminī ।।

tiryaggā rājapatnīṃ ca śreṣṭhinaḥ pratilomanī । vaṃśagulmanibhā rāṣṭraṃ nṛpam indradhvajopamā ।।

gajam indrāyudhaprakhyā puraṃ maṇḍalasaṃsthitā । mantriṇaś cakrasaṃsthānā chattrākārā purodhasam ।।

mayūrapucchānugatā kuryād ulkā jalakṣayam । vilīyamānā nabhasi pibaty ulkā payodharān ।।

sphuliṅgān visṛjantyo yāḥ pradhāvanti samantataḥ । golavac ca pradhāvanti tāsu rāṣṭrabhayaṃ bhavet ।।

ulkāsaṃghaiḥ parivṛtā yāḥ patanti nabhastalāt । anusāriṇya ulkās tā rājarāṣṭrabhayāvahāḥ ।।

pretānugatamārgāś ca varāhānugatāś ca yāḥ । kravyāgnivyālarūpāś ca tā janakṣayakārikāḥ ।।

kṣeveḍitāsphoṭitotkruṣṭā gītavāditranisvanāḥ । ulkāpāteṣu boddhavyā rājarāṣṭrabhayāvahāḥ ।।

sasvanā dāruṇāḥ saṃdhyāvāyoś ca pratilomagāḥ । nabho madhyaṃ ca yā yānti yāś ca kuryur gatāgatam ।।

hinasti śuklā śirasā madhyena kṣatajaprabhā । pārśvābhyāṃ pītakā hanti kṛṣṇolkā pucchayoginī ।।

śuklā devanṛpān hanyāt kṣatriyān kṣatajaprabhā । pītā vaiśyopaghātāya śūdrān hanyāt sitetarā ।।

patantyo nopalakṣyante karma tāsāṃ prakāśate । kṣitāv aśanayo yatra tatra nāsti bhayāgamaḥ ।।

satārā nipatanty anyā mārutapratilomagāḥ । bhavanti vidyuto neṣṭā iṣṭāś ca syur ato anyathā ।।

tārā dhiṣṇyāś ca boddhavyāś cirān mṛduphalodayāḥ । tāsām api ca bhūyiṣṭhaṃ patanaṃ doṣakārakam ।।

yatoyato vikārāḥ syur nipatanty atimātraśaḥ । tatastato nṛpo yāyād daivo mārgaḥ sa ucyate ।।

nimitteṣu mahāśāntim ulkāyāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ । kṛtvā siddhim avāpnoti ulkādoṣāc ca mucyate ।।

ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi vidyullakṣaṇam uttamam । varṇarūpavikārāṃś ca deśabhāgāñ śubhāśubhān ।।

caturthīṃ pañcamīṃ caiva pratīkṣeta sadā śuciḥ । āṣāḍhaśuddhe niyataṃ vidyuddarśanam adbhutam ।।

ativṛṣṭim anāvṛṣṭiṃ bhāvābhāvau tathaiva ca । sarvasasyeṣu niṣpattir vidyuto darśane naraḥ ।।

aindryāṃ cet syandate vidyud aindrasthaś cāpi mārutaḥ । subhikṣaṃ kṣemam ārogyaṃ nirītiṃ ca vinirdiśet ।।

āgneyyāṃ ced ubhau syātāṃ bhayaṃ śastrāgnivṛṣṭihtaḥ । yāmyāyāṃ viṣamāriś ca vyādhimṛtyubhayaṃ tathā ।।

kanīyasī tu nairṛtyāṃ tathā bahvītikā samā । madhyamā sasyasaṃpattir vāruṇyāṃ vyādhisaṃkulā ।।

pataṃgadaṃśamaśakā vāyavyāṃ madhyasapadaḥ । ativāribhayaṃ vidyāt saumyāyāṃ bhūrisaṃpadaḥ ।।

nirītiḥ sasyasaṃpat tu pradhānāiśyāṃ manoramā । pratilomeṣu vāteṣu ītibāhulyam ādiśet ।।

anulomeṣu vāteṣu nirītiṃ tu samādiśet । śubhāyāṃ syandamānāyām aniṣṭā syandate yadi ।।

saṃpadyate mahāsasyān mahāṃś cet syād avagrahaḥ । aśubhā syandate pūrvaṃ yadi paścāc ca śobhanā ।।

suvṛṣṭim eva tatrāhur na ca sasyaṃ samṛdhyati । yadā tu sarvāḥ syandante viṣamāṃ vṛṣṭim ādiśet ।।

bahulāyāṃ vidyuti tu bahuvāribhayaṃ bhavet । savidyutaḥ sastanito darśayanti yadā śubhām ।।

pūrvottarāṃ diśaṃ meghāḥ suvṛṣṭiṃ tāṃ vijānate । pūrvataḥ pūrvavarṣeṣu dṛśyante yadi toyadāḥ ।।

pradakṣiṇāvartaśubhāḥ suvṛṣṭim iti nirdiśet । āgneyeṣv ativṛṣṭiḥ syāt sasyaṃ cāpi vipadyate ।।

viṣamā vṛṣṭir yāmyeṣu vyādhiṃ mṛtyuṃ ca nirdiśet । bahvītikā nairṛteṣu samūlaphaladāyinī ।।

vāruṇeṣu payodeṣu madhyamaṃ sasyam ādiśet । vāyavyāṃ prathamaṃ varṣaṃ yatra varṣati vāsavaḥ ।।

tatrātivṛṣṭir bhavati svalpabījāni vāpayet । varṇasnebhopapannās tu pūrvavṛṣṭyāṃ payodharāḥ ।।

saumyāṃ yatra pravarṣeyus tatra sarvavṛṣṭyāṃ payodharāḥ ।।

ity etat pūrvavarṣeṣu lakṣaṇaṃ vidyutāṃ sphuṭam । varṣārāvagataṃ sarvaṃ yathāvat parikīrtitam ।।

śubheṣv api mahāśāntir avighātāya vocyate । aśubheṣu samarghāya tasmāt sarveṣu śāntikam iti ।।

aṣṭau bhavanti nirghātās teṣām indraḥ praśasyate । pūrveṇa vṛṣṭiṃ sasyaṃ ca rājavṛddhiṃ ca nirdiśet ।।

pūrvottare subhikṣaṃ tu bhūmilābhas tathottare । aparottare caurabhayaṃ vājināṃ cāpy upadravaḥ ।।

paścimāyāṃ bhayaṃ rājño jalajātiś ca pīḍyate । nairṛte sasyagostrīṇāṃ gaṇānāṃ ca mahad bhayam ।।

dakṣiṇe rājapīḍā syād āyuś cātra vinirdiśet । ānartasya bhayaṃ vidyād yadi syāt pūrvadakṣiṇaḥ ।।

sa yojanaparaḥ śabdo nirghātasya viśāmyati । sarvatra ca bhayaṃ vidyāt tatra yatra viśāmyati ।।

bhaye raudrīṃ prakurvīta abhayāṃ vābhayapradām । tayā śāmyanti cotpātāḥ sukhaṃ cātyantikaṃ bhavet ।।

om athātaḥ pariveṣāṇāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ caiva vakṣyate । vṛddhagargo yathā pūrvam uvāca mama suvrata ।।

svāyaṃbhuvaniyogena vikāraṃ kurute amalaḥ ।।

śvetaḥ śyāmo hariḥ kṛṣṇa iti varṇā vyavasthitāḥ । proktā megheṣu catvāro vyaktāḥ snigdhāḥ supūjitāḥ ।।

snigdheṣu pariveṣeṣu vaturṣv eteṣu nārada । saṃdhyāyām atra varṇeṣu vṛṣṭiṃ teṣv abhinirdiśet ।।

kācanīlāñjanāriṣṭāśanisarpanibheṣu ca । raupyadravasamābheṣu meghas triṣv api varṣati ।।

nimagnā tu yadā saṃdhyā bhavaty etat suvṛṣṭaye । ebhyaś ca viparītā ye te avṛṣṭibhayadā ghanāḥ ।।

varāhair makarair uṣṭrair vṛkaiḥ kaṅkais tathā kharaiḥ । śaśakākṛtayaḥ kuryuḥ saṃdhyāyāṃ jaladā bhayam ।।

hemapāvakavarṇāś ca vipulaṃ ca janakṣayam । śabdaṃ śvakharagomāyugṛdhravāyasasaṃsthitāḥ ।।

pūrvāparāsu saṃdhyāsu saṃgrāmaṃ prāhur unmukhāḥ । aśvasthā vāraṇasthāś ca yeṣu yodhā narā iva ।।

megheṣu saṃpradṛśyante ye pāśāṅkuśasaṃnibhāḥ । tathā savāraṇāś caiva vinighnantaḥ parasparam ।।

kravyādbhir bhakṣyamāṇāś ca gṛdhragomāyuvāyasaiḥ । udyudhyante yadā yuktā rāñjaḥ saṃśayakārakāḥ ।।

mayūrāṭṭālapadmendukāśanīlanibhāni tu । saṃdhyāsv abhrāṇi dṛśyante tīvraṃ varṣam upasthitam ।।

savidyut sadhanuṣkaś ca saghoṣaḥ śikhisaṃnibhaḥ । saṃdhyāsv abhrāṇi dṛśyante tīvraṃ varṣam upasthitam ।।

nīlalohitaparyantaṃ kṛṣṇagrīvaṃ savidyutam । vivarṇaṃ parighaṃ dṛṣṭvā vidyād udakavāhakam ।।

trivarṇe parighe vāpi trivarṇair vā balāhakaiḥ । udayāstamayam iyād yadi sūryaḥ kadā cana ।।

pṛthivyāṃ rājavaṃśyānāṃ mahad bhayam upasthitam । lokakṣayakaraṃ vidyād yadi devo na varṣati ।।

matsyarūpī sādṛśyena yady uttiṣṭheta bhāskaraḥ । sphuṭaraśmis tadādityaḥ sa nirdahati medinīm ।।

etad dṛṣṭvā mahad rūpam āditye samupasthite । vispaṣṭaṃ jyotir vispaṣṭaṃ sadyovarṣasya lakṣaṇam ।।

grahasaṃchādanaṃ cāpi garjanaṃ pratigarjanam । paraspareṇa kurvanti meghā vegasamīritāḥ ।।

tasmiṃś caturvidhe yuddhe meghānāṃ vyomacārinām । utpadyante trayo bhāvās tan me nigadataḥ śṛṇu ।।

garjamāneṣu megheṣu vāraṇaḥ pratigarjati । tāṃ diśaṃ yojayet snenāṃ garjanaṃ yatra mīyate ।।

vidyuto abhravikāreṣu śakrāyudhanibhāyudhāḥ । sphoṭitāśanighaṇṭāś ca yāṃ diśaṃ meghavāraṇāḥ ।।

saṃghaṭṭeṣu samudbhutāḥ parasparajighāṃsavaḥ । tāṃ diśaṃ yojayet senāṃ rājā jayati tāṃ diśam ।।

grahaṇāchādane caiva garjane pratigarjane । evam eva vidhir jñeyaḥ sarvaś caiva viniścayaḥ ।।

parimāṇaṃ na śakyaṃ tat samīritum aśeṣataḥ । aparābhravikārāṇāṃ ratnānām iva sāgare ।।

saṃdhyā yojanabhāk proktā stanitaṃ tu dviyojanam । parighaḥ pañcayojanyaḥ pratyādityas triyojanaḥ ।।

nirghātaḥ ṣaṭ tathā vidyut pariveṣo dviṣaḍyataḥ । dāhaṃ yojanakaṃ cāpi ulkā tv amitabhāginī ।।

daśasaṃsthā samāptāni śāyāṅgāni pramāṇataḥ । aṅgāni tv āntarikṣāṇi vijñeyāni samāsataḥ ।।

oṃ catvāro bhumikampās tu gargaḥ provāca buddhimān । agnir vāyus tathāpaś ca caturthas tv indra ucyate ।।

teṣāṃ rūpaṃ vikārāṃś ca vyākhyāsyāmo anupūrvaśaḥ । yaj jñātvā buddhimān dhīro nirdiśed vividhaṃ phalam ।।

prakampitāyāṃ bhūmau cet saptāhābhyantareṇā tu । [bhaveyur atra saṃgrāmā rājñāṃ mṛtyubhayapradāḥ ।।

rājñāṃ virodho bhavati maraṇāni bhavanti ca ।] tāmraḥ sūryaś ca candraś ca pītāś ca mṛgapakṣiṇaḥ ।।

diśaḥ sarvā bhaveyuś ca sūryodayasamaprabhāḥ । yad etallakṣaṇopetaṃ vidyād agniprakampitam ।।

tasmin bhavati nirdeśaḥ śaunakasya vaco yathā । hiraṇyaṃ ca suvarṇaṃ ca yac cānyad vidyate gṛhe ।।

sarvam etat parityajya kartavyo dhānyasaṃgrahaḥ । rāṣṭrāṇi saṃdahed agnir grāmāṃś ca nagarāṇi ca saṃgrāmāś cātra vartante māṃsaśoṇitakardamāḥ । rājānaś ca virudhyante devaś cātra na varṣati ।।

evam etatprakampānāṃ garhitam agnikampitam ।।

prakampitāyāṃ bhūmau ced iti ।।

atipracaṇḍo bahulo vāyur bhavati dāruṇaḥ । śarkarākarṣaṇaś cāpi dikṣu caiva vidikṣu ca ।।

tad etallakṣaṇopetaṃ vidyād vāyuprakampitam । śastrair āvaraṇaṃkuryāt prākāraṃ parikhāṃ tathā ।।

na tadā pravased grāmaṃ jñātvātmānaṃ tu gopayet । saṃgrāmāś cātra vardhante māṃsaśoṇitakardamāḥ ।।

virudhyante ca rājāno maraṇāni bhavanti hi । rājaputrasahastrāṇāṃ bhūmiḥ pibati śoṇitam ।।
