māsaṃ viṃśatirātraṃ vā devas tatra na varṣati । dvābhyāṃ gatābhyāṃ māsābhyāṃ paraṃ syād bahulaṃ jalam ।।

daṣṭaṃ dūṣayate cātra kṣatabaddhāni cādhikam । eṣām eva tu kampānāṃ garhitaṃ vāyukampitam ।।

prakampitāyāṃ bhūmau ।।

varṣantas tu samāyānti mahāmeghāḥ samantataḥ । nakrāś ca śiśumārāś ca kūrmā makarasaṃsthitāḥ ।।

abhrākṛtiṣu dṛśyante grasantaś candrabhāskarau । tad etallakṣaṇopetaṃ vidyād ambuprakampitam ।।

parvateṣu vaped bījam ūṣare jāṅgale tathā । tatroptaṃ nandate bījam anyatra bhuvi naśyati ।।

udajāni tu puṣpāṇi mūlāni ca phalāni ca । gacchanti tatra vṛddhiṃ ca sattvāny udakajāni ca ।।

[kṣemaṃ subhikṣam ārogyaṃ suvṛṣṭiṃ cātra nirdiśet] ।।

prakampitāyāṃ bhūmau ।।

gambhīraṃ garjamānas tu megha āyāti pārthivaḥ । snigdho hy añjanasaṃkāśaḥ sumahatparvatopamaḥ ।।

vitrāsayan diśaḥ sarvā drutaṃ cāpi pravarṣati । indrāyudhaṃ bhavec cātra vidyut stanitam eva ca ।।

suvṛṣṭiṃ kṣemam ārogyaṃ subhikṣaṃ paramā mudaḥ । yajñodbhavais tu modante ānandair moditāḥ prajāḥ ।।

eteṣāṃ bhūmikampānāṃ praśastaṃ hīndrakampanam । jānīyāl lakṣaṇair etaiḥ sarvam eva śubhāśubham ।।

eteṣu triṣu kampeṣu atharvā śāstrakovidaḥ । māhendrīm amṛtāṃ vāpi kuryāc chāntiṃ sadakṣiṇām ।।

indrakampe tu vidhivad aindrair mantrair vidhānavit । tatohalasya pradhānārthaṃ juhuyāc ca japet tathā ।।

om atha paraṃ pravakṣyāmi vakṣatreṣu graheṣu ca । pariveṣān bahuvidhān nānāvidhaphalodayān ।।

aindravāruṇakauberān raktapāṇḍuramecakān । pāṇḍūn babhrūṃś ca pītāṃś cānīlānalayamātmanaḥ ।।

prājāpatyāṃś ca raudrāṃś ca nairṛtyāṃś cāpi bhārgava । hariśabalakāpotān pariveṣān uvāca ha ।।

navaite pariveṣāṇāṃ varṇā daivatayonayaḥ । bahutvam ete gacchanti anyonyaguṇasaṃśrayāt ।।

gṛhītvābhrarajaḥ sūkṣmaṃ varṇayog saṃnipatya ca । pitāmahaniyogena māturo maṇḍalīkṛtaḥ ।।

śubhāśubhārthaṃ lokānāṃ jyotīmṣy avaruṇaddhi saḥ । tasya rūpaṃ guṇaṃ jñātvā guṇadoṣaḥ pracakṣyate ।।

nakṣatratārakāṇāṃ ca parato viṣayasya ca niviṣṭo bhāva āgantuṃ pariveṣa iti smṛtaḥ ।।

dhṛtatīkṣṇārkakiraṇe prasannā mṛdumaṇḍale । prasnigdhe caikavarṇe ca māṃsale vyaktalakṣaṇe ।।

lohitākṣau kṣurakrānte saraśmau pītamaṇḍale । ā pradoṣād vimadhyāhnād ā nakṣatrāntagāmini ।।

sahābhrabhārastanite pariveṣe prakāśini । anṛtāv api jānīyān mahad bhayam upasthitam ।।

kṛṣṇanīhāratimire prakṛtyākrāntamaṇḍale । vikārair nābhasaiḥ kīrṇe sphuliṅgopacite aśubhe ।।

viṣame vigatasnehe vidhvastakaluṣābhrake । triṣu saṃdhiṣu bhūyiṣṭhaṃ darśanaṃ copagacchati ।।

dvitrinakṣatrage vāpi nakṣatrārdhagate api vā । pradīptair vā rasadbhiś ca vīkṣyamāṇe mṛgadvijaiḥ ।।

pariveṣe vijānīyān nṛpādyānām upasthitam । saptarātrād bhayaṃ ghoraṃ cauraśastrāgnimṛtyubhiḥ ।।

dhūmakarburamāñjiṣṭharaktapītāsitākṛtiḥ । bhavaty ekatare pārśve rūpeṇāvilamaṇḍalaḥ ।।

tanunā cātra jālena samantāt pariveṣṭitaḥ । muhurmuhuś ca vilayaṃ saṃsthānaṃ cāpi gacchati ।।

so api vāyvātmako jñeyo mṛdumandadivākaraḥ । pariveṣo alpaphalado vātavṛṣṭiḥ pravṛṃhate ।।

atha ced vātavṛṣṭis tu trirātrān nāpajāyate । jalajvalanacaurāṇāṃ prādurbhāvaḥ prajāyate ।।

pariveṣagato alkā syād dvimaṇḍalaparigrahe । dvābhyāṃ senāpatibhayaṃ yuvarājabhayaṃ tribhiḥ ।।

maṇḍalaiḥ purarodhaḥ syāt tribhir abhyadhikair dhryvan । trāṇi yatrāvarudhyante nakṣatragrahacandramāḥ ।।

tryahād varṣaṃ samācaṣṭe sa māsād vigrahaṃ vadet । senāpatikumārāṇāṃ senāyāś cāpi vidravaḥ ।।

lohitāṅgapariveṣe śastrāgnyutpāta eva ca । sthāvarāḥ karṣakāś cāpi kṣudradhānyaṃ ca pīḍyate ।।

vātavṛṣṭiṃ ca janayet pariviṣṭaḥ śanaiścaraḥ । rājyam eva hi garbhāṃś ca rāhuḥ pīḍayate dhruvam ।।

vyādhīṃś caiva prajanayet pariviṣṭaś ca candramāḥ । kṣucśvāsāgnibhayaṃ ghoraṃ rājato mṛtyutas tathā ।।

pariviṣṭo ambare ketuḥ śikhinaś ca hinasti saha । dvayoḥ saṃgrāmam ācaṣṭe grahayoḥ pariviṣṭayoḥ ।।

kṣudbhayaṃ triṣu vijñeyaṃ varṣanigraha eva ca । caturbhir mriyate rājā sāmātyaḥ sapurohitaḥ ।।

yugānta iva jānīyāt patriviṣṭeṣu pañcasu । brahmakṣatriyaviṭśūdrān hanyāt pratipadādiṣu ।।

grāmān puraṃ ca kośaṃ ca pañcamyādiṣv atas triṣu । aṣṭamyāṃ yuvarājānāṃ camūpālān hinasti saha ।।

navamyāṃ ca daśamyāṃ ca ekādaśyāṃ ca pārthivān । trayodaśyāṃ balakṣobho dvādaśyāṃ rudhyate puram ।।

rājapatnīṃ caturdaśyāṃ pajcadaśyāṃ nṛpasya ca । purohitāmātyanṛpā hanyur anyonyam eva tu ।।

purarodhaṃ vijānīyāt pariviṣṭe bṛhaspatau । mantriṇo lekhakāś cāpi rudhyante sthāvarāṇi ca ।।

vṛṣṭiṃ cāpi vijānīyāt pariviṣṭe budhe grahe । yāyinaḥ kṣatriyāś cāpi rājapakṣaś ca pīḍyate ।।

dhānyārghaṃ ca priyaṃ kuryāt pariviṣṭo bhṛgoḥ sutaḥ । tārāgrahapariveṣā nakṣatrāṇāṃ ca kevalam ।।

mahāgrahodayaṃ kuryān maraṇaṃ vā mahīpateḥ । rakte pīte asite tāmre kṛṣṇe ca harite aruṇe ।।

kṣucśastravyādhivarṣāgnimṛtyusasyānilānayoḥ । varṇānāṃ ca bhayaṃ jñeyaṃ yathā varṇaparigrahaḥ ।।

kāpotaḥ śabalaś cāpi tiryagyonibhayāvahau । mayūragalaśaṅkhendumuktāgokṣīrapāṇḍurāḥ ।।

madhūkaghṛtamaṇḍābhā dūrvāśyāmāś ca vṛṣṭaye । vimuktāriṣṭakākārās tailāmalakasaṃnibhāḥ ।।

snigdhāmalajalaprakhyā darpaṇābhās ca pūjitāḥ । babhravaḥ paruṣā rukṣā haridrāruṇasaṃnibhāḥ । vichinnā lohitā hrasvā vivarṇāś ca śubhāvahāḥ ।।

yāyināṃ sthāvarāṇāṃ ca tathaivākrandasāriṇām । pariveṣān vijānīyād bāhyābhyantaramadhyataḥ ।।

saṃraktaśyāmakaluṣo yeṣāṃ bhāgo hataprabhaḥ । teṣāṃ parājayaṃ vidyāt snigdhe śvete ca vai jayaḥ ।।

yenayenābhravarṇena yoyo bhāgo anurajyate । tattat teṣāṃ phalaṃ vidyāt tad bhūtyādiṣu kīrtitam ।।

chidrāṇy etāny ataś cāhur mahānti vimalāni ca । tair dvāraiḥ pārthivo yāyāt panthānas te vikaṇṭakāḥ ।।

kālāmbudaparisrāvair grahodayanimittakam । ityarthaṃ janma sarveṣāṃ śeṣam utpātalakṣaṇam ।।

raudrī sadakṣiṇā śāntir utpāteṣu prakīrtitā । samuccaye tu vijñeyā vaiśvadevy abhayā tathā ।।

atharvotpātahṛdayaṃ jñātvā svayam anāturaḥ । prayuñjīta mahāśāntiṃ sarvakalmaṣanāśinīm ।।

oṃ yān provācāṅgirāḥ pūrvaṃ yāṃśca vedo aśanāḥ kaviḥ । tān ahaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi utpātāṃs trividhān api ।।

prakṛter anyathābhavo yatrayatropajāyate । tatratatra vijānīyāt sarvam utpātalakṣaṇam ।।

pārthivaṃ cāntarikṣaṃ ca divyaṃ cotpātalakṣaṇam । nakṣatropadraveṣūktaṃ yathāvidhi tathaiva tat ।।

teṣūtpātagaṇeṣu āhū rasātalasamudbhavān । nirghātān bhūmikampāṃś ca kīrtyamānān nibodhata ।।

vāruṇāgneyavāyavyāḥ kampayanti vasuṃdharām । śubhāśubhārthaṃ lokānāṃ rātrau ahani cakravat ।।

teṣāṃ vakṣyāmi kampānāṃ lakṣaṇāni phalāni ca । yatrovācāuśanāḥ khyātān nāradāya sma pṛcchate ।।

saptāhābhyantare kampe bhaved vajradharātmake । sasvanair āptaparyantaṃ svastikābhraghanair nabhaḥ ।।

saindracāpāyudhā kampād vidyudgaṇagavākṣakaiḥ । pāśorminagarākārair naganāganibhair ghanaiḥ ।।

nabhaso antaṃ ca sevinyo vidyutaḥ svārkasaṃnibhāḥ । prānte susaṃvṛtāś cāpi śītāśītāś ca mārutāḥ ।।

dhārāṅkuraparisrāvair nīlotpaladalaprabhaiḥ । svanadbhiś chādyate vyoma kampayed varuṇaḥ svayam ।।

tārāpātair diśaṃ dāhair ulkāpātaiś ca sasvanaiḥ । hāhākṛtam ivābhūti pradīpitapathaṃ nabhaḥ ।।

saptāhābhyantare vāpi kṣitau vahniḥ prakupyate । sa āgneyo bhavet kampo rājarāṣtrabhayāvahaḥ ।।

niḥprakāśam ivākāśe bhāskaro nātibhāskaraḥ । diśas tu na prakāśante duḥkhāṛtā iva yoṣitaḥ ।।

saghoṣā mārutā rūkṣā vānti śarkarakarṣiṇaḥ । saptāhābhyantare kampe mārute atibhayāvahe ।।

subhikṣakṣemadau kampau vijñeyāv aindravāruṇau । vāyavyāgneyajau kampau rājarāṣtrabhayāvahau ।।

yasyāṃ yasyāṃ diśi dharā virauti vikṛtasvarā । tasyāṃ tasyāṃ diśi bhayṃ sārdhaṃ syād adhikāridbhiḥ ।।

nirghātā bhūmikampāś ca sasamāsam udāhṛtāḥ । ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi śeṣam utpātalakṣaṇam ।।

prāgyāmyāparasaumyānāṃ gandharvanagaraṃ tathā । raktapītāśitaiś caiva varṇair dikṣu pradṛśyate ।।

rājñaḥ senāpateś cāpi yuvarājapurodhasām । vyasanaṃ maraṇaṃ vāpi vijñeyam anupūrvaśaḥ ।।

varuṇāmāṇ ca bhayaṃ jñeyaṃ yathāvarṇaparigrahāt । vidikṣu ca vivarṇāsu pīḍā jñeyā vivarṇinām ।।

satataṃ dṛśyamāne ca rājarāṣṭrabhayāvaham । āśādhikārikāṇāṃ ca pīḍā jñeyā yathāvidhi ।।

viruddhayonigamanam anyasattvaprasūtayaḥ । hastapādākṣiśirasām adhikānāṃ pradarśanam ।।

abhyaṅgatā ca saṃyoge gatihīnaṃ ca ceṣṭitam । viruddhānāṃ ca sattvānām anyonyapratisaṃgamam ।।

calatvam acalānāṃ ca calānām acalakṛyā । bhāṣitaṃ cāpi abhāṣāṇām aśabdānāṃ ca bhāṣaṇam ।।

anagnau darśanaṃ cāgneḥ śītoṣṇasya viparyayaḥ । lohādīnāṃ plavaś cāpsu nodake cāmbhasāṃ sravaḥ ।।

akālapuṣpaprasavaḥ sasyāḥ pañcacaturguṇāha । saṃyogo lāṅgalānāṃ ca prabhānāṃ ceṣṭitāni ca ।।

vicitrair devatāsadbhir vṛkṣaprasravaṇāni ca । diśo dhūmāndhakārāś ca dīptāś ca mṛgapakṣiṇaḥ ।।

rajastamāśritaṃ vyoma kaluṣau candrabhāskarau । vastramāṃsāmbhasāṃ dīptirāgaprajvalitāni ca ।।

akasmād gopurāṭṭālaśailaprasādaveśmanām । daraṇaṃ jvalanaṃ vāpi kampo dhūmapravartanam ।।

abhīkṣṇā mārutāś caṇḍā vānti śarkarakarṣiṇaḥ । saṃhitā maṇḍalānāṃ ca nīlalohitapītakāḥ ।।

dhvajastambhendrakīlānāṃ śuṣkacaityādibhiḥ saha । chinne bhinne drumāṇāṃ ca skandhaśākhāṅkurodbhavaḥ ।।

gītānāṃ ca mṛdaṅgānāṃ vāditrāṇāṃ nisvanāḥ । bhaveyur ākāśapathe sagandharvapurogamāḥ ।।

chāyādarśanam adravye virātre virutāni ca । divārātricarāṇāṃ ca viparītapracāratā ।।

nirabhravṛṣṭayaś caiva nirabhrastanitāni ca । sasvanānām adhūmānām ulkānāṃ patanaṃ divā ।।

indor arkasya vā cāpi pāṃsvaśmādiṣu darśanam । abhīkṣṇapariveṣāśca kaluśā ravisomayoḥ ।।

mayūrakokilādīnāṃ madāvāptir anārtavā । vanānāṃ ca nagānāṃ ca devatānāṃ ca nirgamāḥ ।।

āraṇyānāṃ ca sattvānāṃ puragrāmaniveśanam । abhūtānāṃ pravṛtiśca pravṛttānāṃ ca nāśanam ।।

etad utpātajaṃ rājño yasyā deśe abhyudīryate । tasya deśo vinaśyeta kṣīyate ca sapārthivaḥ ।।

tyajanti vāpi yaṃ deśaṃ pāṣaṇḍā dvijadevatāḥ । vidveṣaṃ vāpi gacchanti so api deśo vinaśyati ।।

nartanaṃ ca kuśūlānāṃ dhānyarāśeśca kampanam । ulūkhālānāṃ saṃsarpo musalānāṃ praveśanam ।।

ceṣṭitaṃ rājadarvīṇāṃ mṛdbhāṇḍānāṃ tathaiva ca । dahanaṃ caiva śītānām [śabdā hy uttarāṇi ca] ।।

purīṣabhakṣaṇaṃcaiva dīnānāṃ mṛgapakṣiṇām । grāmyāṇāṃ dīnavapuṣāṃ pradhānyastanitāni ca ।।

vālukāṅgāradhānyānāṃ bhakṣaṇaṃ vāpi vṛṣṭayaḥ । puradvāre ca bakavad vāyasānāṃ ca ceṣṭitam ।।

biḍālamatsyamajjānāṃ jantūnāṃ kṣudrasaṃjñinām । anyonyabhakṣaṇāni syur ekasaṃsthāśca rātrayaḥ ।।

māṃsasasyānnavidveṣaḥ kriyāvyuparamas tathā । yasmin deśe pradṛśyante tasmin kṣudbhayam ādiśet ।।

śastrajvalanasaṃsarpaḥ sthūṇīsaraṇapūraṇam । chattravastradhvajānāṃ ca valmīkeṣu pradarśanam ।।

arke abhraparighādīnāṃ pariveṣo arkacandrayoḥ । lākṣālohitavarṇatvaṃ sarveṣāṃ ca vicāraṇam ।।

tvacmāṃsarudhirāsthīnāṃ medomajjāsthivṛṣṭayaḥ । nirabhravṛṣṭayaścāsya rajatakṣatasaprabham ।।

praghātākampanirghātāvidyutā cābhrapātanam । bhavecca devatādīnāṃ śiroabhiṣṭhānavarjanam ।।

strīṇāṃ nṛṇāṃ ca prasavaṃ tṛṇādīnāṃ ca mānuṣam । amānuṣāṇāṃ sattvānāṃ bhāṣitāni manuṣyavat ।।

vasāśoṇitagandhatvaṃ gajadaivatavājinām । yasmin deśe bhavet tasmin śastrakopabhayaṃ mahat ।।

śoṇitāśruparisrāvāḥ prahāsodvīkṣaṇakriyā । nṛtyavāditragītāni sākrośābhāṣitāni ca ।।

prakampanaṃ devatānāṃ tathaiva jvalanāni ca । apāṃ śoṣavikārāśca ceṣṭitaṃ ca manuṣyavat ।।

daraṇaṃ rasanaṃ rājño vaikṛtyodvartanāni ca । kṣiteḥ kampaprahāsāśca rodanotkrośāani ca ।।

pīṭhikāvyañjanaṃ chattra[m]śasatrakīlakamaṇḍalau । nīlāṅgalohitatalau udye arkaniśāakarau ।।

candrārkolkāprabhedāśca bhāskarendudvayaṃ tathā । pratisrotavahā nadya iṣavaḥ pratikomagāḥ ।।

dantabhaṅgāḥ sakūrmāśca naravarṇavājinām । chattrabhaṅgāḥ sakūrmāśca naravāraṇavājinām ।।

māṃsatailavipākaśca caityatailaparisravāḥ । śakradhvajapatākānāṃ bhaṅgakravyadasvanam ।।

biḍalolūkyor yuddhaṃ nṛpaprāsādasaṃnidhau । pāṃsunā cāvṛtaṃ vyoma rajasā tamasāpi vā ।।

lohitāgniprabhākāśaṃ dīptā dvijamṛgas tathā । vātāvartās tusaṃdhyāsu prasphuranto apasavyagāḥ ।।

maṇḍalāni samājāśca sarvato mṛgapakṣiṇām । kravyādair ārasadbhiśca vyākulāḥ sarvato diśaḥ ।।

trirātrād aparaṃ vṛṣṭiḥ pranaṣṭendudivākarau । anṛtau cāpi dṛśyeta ghorastanitadīrghatā ।।

vajrādayo rāhuputrā vṛkṣāḥ śakunayas tathā । maṇḍalābhyantarasthāśca bhavanti ravisomayoḥ ।।

ākāśe vā pradṛśyante prakampanti va parvatāḥ । viṣyeta ravisomau ca ābhīkṣaṃ tārakās tathā ।।

naradanaṃ ca biḍālāṇāṃ kṣīravṛkṣaniṣevaṇam । kharair dīptair ulūkaiśca rasadbhiḥ saha vigrahaḥ ।।

siṃhāsanāni chattrāṇi bhṛṅgārāḥ śayanās tathā । kampanti akasmād bhajyante saṃsarpanti ārasanti ca ।।

rājñāṃ bhayakaraṃ sarvam etad utpātalakṣaṇam । deśasya ca vijānīyād gargasya vacanaṃ yathā ।।

saṃdhyādaṇḍapariveṣā rajoarkaparighādayaḥ । maṇḍalānāṃ samūhāśca dikṣu pītāruṇaprabhāḥ ।।

kravyādā vānarā dvāri visphūrjanti ārasanti ca । tuṇḍaiśca vāyasā bhūmiṃ kuṭṭayanto ramanti ca ।।

mlāyate mālyam atyarthaṃ gandhāḥ kuṇapagandhinaḥ । vastreṣu bhakṣabhojyeṣu bhavati utpātalakṣaṇam ।।

kṣaudraṃ ghṛtaṃ ca dadhi ca prasravet prathitā drumāḥ । sārameyāḥ śmaśāneṣu rudanti viruvanti ca ।।

etad autpātikaṃ grāme yasmiṃś ca dṛśyate pure । tasmin grāme pure vāpi vidyād atibhayaṃ mahat ।।

aśvatthodumbaraplakṣanyagrodhe kusumodbhavaḥ । śvetalohitapītāni kṛṣṇānīndrāyudhāni ca ।।

evaṃ varṇaduṇānāṃ ca patanaṃ devaveśmanām । brahmakṣatriyaviṭśūdravināśo rājasaṃvṛtām ।।

rūkṣasrāvā citivṛkṣe tadbhayaṃ sumahad bhavet । ghṛtakṣīraphalāśrāve ghṛtakṣīrāmbhasāṃ kṣayaḥ ।।

surāśrāve mithobhedo rudhire rāṣṭravidravaḥ । rudhire goviṣāṇācca srute gobrāhmaṇakṣayaḥ ।।

phale phalaṃ yadā paśyet puṣpe puṣpaṃ samāvṛtam । garbhāḥ sravanti nārīṇāṃ yuddhaṃ rājavadho api vā ।।

phaṇābhṛto mahatsarpān maṇḍūlā atha vṛścikāḥ । maṇḍūkā grasate yatra tatra rājāvahanyate ।।

himapātānilotpātā vikṛtādbhutadarśanam । kṛṣṇāñjanābhram ākāśaṃ tārolkāpātapiṅgalam ।।

citrā garbhodbhavāḥ strīṣu goajāśvamṛgapakṣiṣu । pattrāṅkuralatānāṃ ca vikārāḥ śiśire śubhāḥ ।।

vajrāśanimahīkampāḥ saṃdhyānirghātanisvanāḥ । pariveṣarajodhūmā raktārkāstamanodayāḥ ।।

drumebhyo annarasasnehamadhupuṣpaphalodgamāḥ । gopakṣiśabdavṛddhiśca śivāni madhumādhave ।।

tārolkāpātakaluṣaṃ kapilārkendumaṇḍalam । anagnijvalanasphoṭadhūmareṇvanilāhatam ।।

raktapītāruṇāṃ saṃdhyāṃ nabhaḥ saṃkṣubhītārṇavam । saritāṃ cāmbusaṃśoṣaṃ dṛṣṭvā grīṣme śubhaṃ vadet ।।

śakrāyudhaparīveṣavidyutśuṣkavirohaṇam । akasmād varṇavaikṛtyaṃ rasanaṃ daraṇaṃ kṣiteḥ ।।

saronadyudapānānāṃ vṛddhir vā uttaraṇaplavāḥ । taraṇaṃ cārdravegānāṃ varṣāsu na bhayāvaham ।।

divyastrīgītagandharvavimānādbhutanisvanāḥ । grahanakṣatratārāṇāṃ darśanaṃ ca divāmbare ।।

gītavāditranirghoṣo vanaparvatasānuṣu । sasyavṛddhī rasotpattir na pāpāḥ śaradi smṛtāḥ ।।

śītānilatuṣāratvaṃ nardanaṃ mṛgapakṣiṇām । rakṣoyakṣādisattvānāṃ darśanaṃ vāg amānuṣī ।।

dīptadhūmarajasdhvastā diṅnāgā vanaparvatāḥ । uccais toyadasomārkā hemante śobhanāḥ smṛtāḥ ।।

ṛtusvabhāvā ete hi dṛṣṭāḥ svartau śubhapradāḥ । ṛtau anyatra ca utpātā dṛṣṭāḥ svartau śubhapradāḥ ।।

unmattānāṃ ca yā gāthā bālānāṃ ceṣṭitaṃ ca yat । striyaśca yat prabhāṣante tatra nāsti vyatikramaḥ ।।

pūrvaṃ vadati deveṣu paścād gacchati mānuṣe । nācoditā āg vadati satyā hi eṣā sarasvatī ।।

utpātāḥ sarva eva ete kadācid rājamṛtyave । jñeyā deśavināśāya rāhor āgamanāyā vā ।।

kālāmbudaparisrāvā grahāṇām udayāya vā । svacakraparacakrebhyo bhaye vā samupasthite ।।

rāṣṭre senāpatau putre pure vātha purodhasi । amātye vāhane dāre nṛpatau vā palanti ca ।।

etān samutthitāṃ jñātvā rājā sabalavāhanaḥ । praṇipatya guruṃ brūyād bhagavan śamayasva me ।।

bhayam utpātajaṃ sarvaṃ brūhi kiṃ karavāṇi te । iti uktaḥ śraddadhānena rājñā svahitam icchatā ।।

nimittāni samālokya kṛtvā pāvanam āditaḥ । mahāśāntiṃ prayuñjīta sarvopadravanāśinīm ।।

sarvarogapraśamanīm utpātaphalanāśinīm । raudrīṃ kuryān mahāśāntiṃ śraddhayā bahudakṣiṇāṃ śraddhayā bahudakṣiṇām ।।

om atha ato lakṣaṇopāṅge sadyovṛṣṭilakṣaṇaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ।।

snigdhavimalataladarśane arciṣmaty atitejasi sthūlaraśmau harijvalanasaṃnibhe savitari sadyo varṣati parjanyo viśuddhāsu ca dikṣu kākāṇḍavarṇeṣu giriṣv atirajaskandheṣu hradamagneṣu vimalavipulasnigdhaprasannahṛṣṭapradarśaneṣu nīcair iva jyotirgaṇeṣv anukūleṣu śive śite nīce mārute bhavati cātra ślokaḥ ।।

pūrvo abhrajanamo vāyur itaro abhravināśanaḥ । udag janayate vṛṣṭiṃ varṣaty eva ca dakṣiṇaḥ ।।

abhreṣu timiramakaranaganāganakragrāhaśiṃśumāraśaṅkhadrumakūrmormijhaṣamahiṣavarāhadigdviradanavakumudakhaṇḍākṛtinalakalaśakuḍmalāpīḍatoraṇāvartasvastikavardhamānaravauhvarajatamadrāṇipatākāśvatātyāsthānavividhajalacarapakṣivirutacatuṣpadākāreṣu naktanīlotpalakamalapalāśakomaleṣu ।।

[muktā]sphaṭikarajatavaiḍuryāñjanabhramarasarpasaṃnikāśeṣu । kṣaudrakṣīrapalāśadhūma[dūrvā]rajatakanakavidrumaprabheṣ ।।

dviguṇatriguṇadarśaneṣu mūlavatsu viśikhareṣu mahāvarteṣu taralarathanemighoṣeṣu udadhijalanirghoṣasaṃhrādeṣu kṣubdhadundubhininādeṣu kiñjalkāravindasaṃnibheṣu vā kumudamayūragalakālakeṣu cābhrajālāvanādeṣu chinnābhreṣu vā chinnamūleṣu kāleṣu kāñcanamanahśiloupameṣu suvarṇapūrṇeṣu jaleṣv asmin na cābhyantarato deśaśobhiteṣu dakṣiṇamāruteritaparitate grahāntargatastanitagambhīranisvaneṣu ardhāntareṣu sadyovarṣam ādiśet ।।

udayāstamaye meghā garbhabhūtā divākare । pradīptā iva citrāsu viṣamāsu khakoṭiṣu ।।

pañca mārutaparyaṅkā maṇayaḥ kāñcanā iva । yatrayatropalakṣyante tatratatra pravarṣati ।।

ghananicayaṃ virohaṇe vādhirohaṇāstagamane vā savitur dṛṣṭvā ca varṣad udadhijīvarādrariṣṭakavaiḍūryotpalakamalapalāśadhūmaśevālavadhrajabakasaṃnikāśasnigdhaghoṣagambhīragabhastividvanbhaiḥ pravṛddhaiḥ samārutān vañcibhiḥ pravṛddhaskandhaśākhānvitapāvanitalaruhān sadyovarṣam ādiśet ।।

antarājitadīptāgnikāñcanāmalasaṃnibhaiḥ । abhraiś cotpalavaidūryaprabhāvāñjanasaṃnibhaiḥ ।।

nīlarśmiprarohantaḥ śākhāvanta iva drumāḥ । yatrayatra pradṛśyante dhruvaṃ tara pravarṣati ।।

saṃdhyā ca jvalanaravīndīvarakaraṇdatapanīyārkodayaharitālanīlotpalaghṛtamadhubandhujīvakajapāpuṣpakiṃśukarāśisaṃnikāśā tathā drutakanakavidrumasphaṭikavaiḍūryavarṇam uddyotayanti diśaḥ śāntamṛgaśakuniviśeṣāḥ ।।

kiṃtanā snigdhā ghanā gabhastimālini saṃprati saṃdhyāṃ dṛṣṭvā nīcair nirmalasnigdhaparidhipariveṣābhravṛkṣapratisūryakā lohitākṣapakṣiptā sārdhaṃ pañcakāvaliptaiś ca mahiṣavṛṣavarāhādidviradajalagaṇair ivācaritaviṣayā atra ślokaḥ ।।

sāṃdhyaiś ca pariveṣaiś ca pratighaiḥ pratisūryakaiḥ । jalajaiś cāvṛtānindyaiḥ sadyaḥ saṃdhyā pravarṣati ।।

yathālakṣaṇaṃ śastrakāṃsyatāmrāyasānāṃ kledavatāṃ khadyotāni ।। tatra svedanti kāmahurdhunināś ca uttaṭaprākāragopuragṛhāgādhirohaṇapāṃsusnānam aṇḍajānām pracaraṇe taḍāgakūpān setubandhākrītāś ca śiśūnāṃ dṛṣṭvā prasaṃkhyāyāś ca citrāviśākhāsvātibahulāṣāḍhāhirbudhnyayāmyasya saṃgrahasaṃpāteṣu mahadvarṣasaṃvṛte ca tryahād ūrdhvaṃ cātra ślokau ।।

ākrīḍāś caiva matsyānāṃ gavāṃ dṛṣṭvāgamo gṛham । prācuryadaṃśamaśakair dhiṣṇyānāṃ cātha mokṣeṇe ।।

jalājalajasaṃtānān ekatra bilavāsinām । pipīlikāṇḍasaṃkrāntir athoṣṇaṃ cāmbu vṛṣṭaye ।।

satkṛtya ca daivajñaṃ palvalakūpataḍāganadītīre ।। sāddālagṛheṣu deśeṣv ārdravāsārdrapāṇiḥ prṛcchet ।। sadyovarṣam adiśet ।।

diśy aiśānyāṃ vā madhurasvarariṣṭavyāharaṇaṃ jalagotrasābhūtaṃ talliṅgānām antarālaṃ bālānāṃ śrutvā dṛṣṭvā varṣatīti brūyāt ।।

rātristanito divā vidyudbhir vādyamākṣetre varṇaḥ snigdho dviguṇendracāpa darśane vyomni nirabhre paśuvirāvābhradaṇḍābhasvalpāñ cābhrarājiprādurbhāvaiḥ sadyovṛṣṭir atra ślokāḥ ।।

pratisūryako bhaved yas tu raver uttarato yadā । toyaṃ nivārayen nityaṃ dakṣiṇe salilād bhayam ।।

tridhā nimittasaṃpannā vṛṣṭir bhavati pārthivī । nimitte tāvad ekasmin pañcayojanikaṃ bhavet ।।

yeṣuyeṣu nimitteṣu nakṣatreṣu ca vartmani । praśastam iti teṣv eva prādurbhūteṣu varṣati ।।

viparyayanimittāni pratibandhakarāṇi tu । teṣu śāntiṃ prakurvīta atharvā śamanāya vai ।।

sam ut patantu sūktena pra nabhasveti cāpare । vaitasyaḥ samidho anye tu śamīmayyo apare viduḥ ।।

[samidhāṃ vaitasīnāṃ tu agnāv arkendhanāhute । ahorātrikahomaḥ syāt parjanyo bahuvarṣadaḥ ।।

sam ut patantu sūktena maruto yajate pākayajñavidhānena yathā varuṇaṃ vṛṣṭikāmaḥ ।। pra nabhasvety ṛcau dve maruto yajate vṛṣṭikāmo yathā varuṇaṃ juhoti ।।] ādadhyāt samidhaḥ plākṣīḥ sakṣīrā ghṛtasaṃyutāḥ । tatas tac chamam āyāti kṛtsnam utpātalakṣaṇam ।।

aindrīṃ vā vāruṇīṃ vāpi mahāśāntiṃ vidhānataḥ । varṣādau tu prayuñjīta avṛṣṭes tu vināśanīm ।।

vṛṣṭer yāni nimittāni tāny apratihatāni tu । bhavanti vṛṣṭidāyīni sasyavṛddhikarāṇi tu ।।

vaitasānāṃ tu pattrāṇāṃ lakṣaṃ kṣīrasamāyutam । vratānte bhārgavo juhvad avarṣāsv api varṣayed iti ।।

oṃ bhagavan devadeveśa surāsuranamaskṛta । gavāṃ sarveṣu rogeṣu pratijñāteṣu vai prabho ।।

kathaṃ śāntiṃ dvijaḥ kuryāt kena mantreṇa prokṣaṇam । homamantrāś ca ke proktāḥ kasmiṃs tantre prayojayet ।।

uvāca paripṛṣṭaḥ san brahmā sarvajagatpatiḥ । śṛṇvantu ṛṣayaḥ sarve gośāntiṃ mahaduttamām ।।

atharvavihitāṃ samyak sarvarogavināśanīm । yāṃ śrutvā savarogās tu vidravanti sahasraśaḥ ।।

goṣṭhamadhye gṛhe vāpi govāṭe gokulāntile । ācāryas tu śucir bhūtvā kārayen maṇḍalaṃ śubham ।।

snātaś cāhatavāsāś ca ahorātroṣitaḥ śuciḥ । caturaśraṃ caturdvāram ālikhet tatra maṇḍalam ।।

tasya madhye tu deveśaṃ gomayena nidhāpayet । tataḥ kṣīraṃ ghṛtaṃ caiva gugguluṃ candanāgurum ।।

puṣpāṇi ca sugandhīni tathā vai sarṣapāṃs tilān । lājāś ca samidhaś caiva samāhṛtya vicakṣaṇaḥ ।।

prāṇāṃs tu tarpayet tatra dadhikṣīraghṛtādibhiḥ । tataḥ śāntiṃ prayuñjita namaskṛtvā svayaṃbhuvam ।।

ājyabhāgāntājyatantram abhyātānāni caiva hi ।।

namojñāya sureśāya namas te viśvatomukha । namaḥ kālāya tīkṣṇāya [jaṭilāya] sarvabhūtahitāya ca ।।

tataḥ sarṣapatilalājā ūrdhvāḥ samidhaś ca dadhimadhughṛtāktā juhuyāt ।।

yajāmi ।। piṅgalāya tīkṣṇāya jaṭilāya babhrave oṃ bhūr oṃ bhuva oṃ svar oṃ bhūr bhuvaḥ svar jayavijayāya jayādhipataye kapardine karālāya vikaṭāya kaṭiramāṭarāyāṅgirasabārhaspatyakakapilamaṇḍalamuṇḍajaṭilakapāleśvarādhipataye kapardine svāheti ।।

eṣa karmasu tu gośānteḥ saṃsṛṣṭa ṛṣibhiḥ purā । proktā svayaṃbhuvā caiṣā gośāntis tu hitāya vai ।।

yo vipraḥ paṭhatīmāṃ hi gokule cāpi hitāya vai । gāvas tasya pravardhante mahatīṃ cāśnute śriyam ।।

oṃ puruṣas putradāraṃ vā dhanadhānyam atha api vā । nimittair yair vinaśyeta śāntiṃ tatra nibodhata ।।

indrāyudhaṃ bhavet rātrau dṛśyate yasya kasya cit । darvī kare vā bhidyeta maṇis kumbhas tathā eva ca ।।

chattraṃ śayyā āsanaṃ ca eva anyat vā api svayaṃ kva cit । strī hanyāt ca striyaṃ vā api gaur avaghret ulūkhalam ।।

śvā pidet gām anaḍvāhaṃ kalis saṃpadyate kule । gajavājino mriyante vivādo rājakīyakas ।।

kuṭumbam aśubhaṃ sarvam aindrāṇi etāni nirdiśet । śāmyanti yena sarvāṇi nirvapet pāyasaṃ carum ।।

samāvaoya ghṛtaṃ tatra āhutiṃ jihuyāt imām । indram id devatātaye sthālīpākasya homayet ।।

indras śacīpatis śakro vajrapāṇis sureāśvaras । sarvādbhutānāṃ śamano mahāvyāhṛtayas tathā ।।

hutvā sviṣṭakṛtaṃ ca eva carutantraṃ samāpayet । vimuktotpātadoṣas tu jīvet tu śaradas śatam ।।

uddīpikā gṛhe yasya valmīkā madhujālakam । abjānāṃ maṇike śabde tailaṃ sthīyata eva vā ।।

aśubhā vikṛtir dadhnāṃ dugdhānāṃ vā yadā bhavet । akasmāt ca praroheyur bījāni kṛmayas tathā ।।

kāryo varuṇayāgas tu vāruṇīvidhipūrvakas । ud uttamaṃ pradhānaṃ syāt pañcājyāhutayas tathā ।।

varuṇas pāśapāṇis ca yadāsāṃ patir eva ca । śeaṃ tu pūrvavat ca eva carutantraṃ samāpayet ।।

vimuktotpātadoṣas tu jīvet tu śaradas śatam ।।

gṛhe yasya patet gṛdhra ulūko vā kathaṃ cana । kapotas praviśet ca eva jīvā vā araṇyasaṃbhavās ।।

dhuryau ca patato yuktau gostrījanma ca vaikṛtam । jāyante yamalāni eva ghoras svapnas ca dṛśyate ।।

abhidravanti rakṣāṃsi yatra ca eva kumārakān । unnidrako atunidro vā atyalpam atibhojanam ।।

ālasya ca evam eteṣāṃ devatā yama ucyate । nāke suparṇam iti etat sthālīpākasya homayet ।।

yamas pretapatis ca eva daṇḍapāṇis tathā īśvaras । śamanaḥ sarvādbhutānām ।।

anagnir utthito yasya dhūmo vā api gṛhe kva cit । āmaṃ vā jvalate māṃsaṃ bhaveyur visphuliṅgakās ।।

chattradhvajapatākās ca jvalante toraṇāni ca ।। āsanaṃ ca eva ;ayyā ca vastrāṇi kusumāni ca ।।

hastyaśvānāṃ ca pucchāni varṣatyaṅgāravarṣaṇam । akāle ca diśāṃ dāha oṣadhīnāṃ ca pācanam ।।

hastinyas ca eva madyante agnirūpaṃ tad adbhutam । agniṃ dūtaṃ vṛṇīmahe sthālīpākasya homayet ।।

agnir hiraṇyapatis ca arciṣpāṇis tathā īśvaras । śamanas sarvādbhutānām ।।

suvarṇaṃ rajataṃ vajraṃ vaiḍūryaṃ mauktikāni ca । pravālavastranāśas ca mitrāṇāṃ ca viparyayas ।।

ārambhās ca vipadyante na soddhis karmaṇām api । carur vaiśravaṇas tatra abhi tyaṃ devam ṛk smṛtā ।।

vaiśravaṇo yakṣapatis arthapāṇis tathā īśvaras । śamanas sarvādbhutānām ।।

atha yasya svanakṣatre ulkā nirghāta eva vā । rāhur grasati candrārkau kabandhaṃ darpaṇe bhavet ।।

patet svayaṃ vā musalaṃ devatā vā kathaṃ cana । unmīlate ca eva yadā tathā ca api nimīlate ।।

prachidyate ca yadi vā tathā vā api prakampate । prayāto vā api dṛśyeta pratisroto nadī vahet ।।

vimale na eva arkachāyā pratīpā vā api tu sāyakās । pariveṣas tu anabhreṣu dṛśyate candrasūryayos ।।

kośāt khaḍgā nirgirante tūṇāt ca eva tu sāyakās । anāhatāni vādyante nadante śabdam āturam ।।

caruṇā vaiṣṇavena eṣāṃ yāgas kartavyas eva tu । idaṃ viṣṇus pradhānaṃ syāt pañcājyāhutayas tathā ।।

sarvabhūtapatis viṣnus cakrapāṇis tathā īśvaras । śamanas sarvādbhutānām ।।

ativāto yatra bhavet rūpaṃ vā yatra vaikṛtam । kharakarabhamahiṣā varāhā vyāghrasiṃhakās ।।

gṛdhrās ca tathā gomāyus kṛkalāsā vadanti ca । māṃsapeśaṃ ca rudhiraṃ pāṃsuvṛṣṭis tathā eva ca ।।

vāyurūpam idaṃ sarvam adbhutaṃ parikīrtitam । vāta ā vātu bheṣajaṃ vāyau ā yāhi darśata iti sthālīpākasya homayet ।।

vāyur mahān nabhapatir vajrapāṇis tathā īśvaras । śamanas sarvādbhutānāṃ mahāvyāhṛtayas tathā ।।

hutvā sviṣṭakṛtaṃ ca eva carutantraṃ samāpayet । vimuktotpātadoṣas tu jīvet tu śaradas śatam ।।

atha ced anyaśākhasu kartā bhavati vedavit । japtvā sa ṛgyajuḥsāmnaṃ śatamātraṃ samāhitas ।।

gāyatryaṣṭaśataṃ japtvā yayajamānas samāhitas । vācayet tam upādhyāyaṃ vastreṇa kanakena vā ।।

dṛṣṭāṃ ca eva adbhutaṃ yasmins tat ca api pratipādayet । etās tu dakṣiṇās sarvās śaktiyukto na hāpayet ।।

yajamānas tatsuto vā yas svayaṃ kartum arhati । brāhmaṇāya viśeṣeṇa dadyāt tāṃ dakṣiṇāṃ śubhām ।।

japtvā atharvaśiras ca eva kuryāt vipreṣu pūjanam । śaktyā atha bhojanaṃ ca eva kuryāt vipreṣu pūjanam ।।

etad evaṃ samākhyātam adbhutānāṃ viśodhanam । caturṇām api varṇānāṃ yas kuryāt śraddhayā anvitas ।।

maraṇaṃ na bhavet tasya na duḥkhaṃ na daridratā । sidhyanti sarvakāryāṇi dharme ca asya matir bhavet ।।

etat puṇyaṃ paritraṃ ca devatāyāgapūjanam । sarvaśāntikaṃ ca eva pratipuruṣaṃ nibodhata ।। pratipuruṣaṃ nibodhata iti ।।

om athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi yad uktaṃ padmayoninā । upāṅgaṃ śukracārasta śubhāśubhanivedakam ।।

svapnādhyāyaṃ pravakṣyāmi kroṣṭuker vacanaṃ yathā । śaśaṃsire purā yaṃ hi śaunakāya mahātmane ।।

nimittajñānakuśalāḥ sarvaṃ tasya tu pṛcchataḥ । grahā bhārgavabhaumārkāḥ paittikā dīptitejasaḥ ।।

kaphaprakṛtayo madhyā bṛhaspatibudhendavaḥ । vātaprakṛtayaḥ krūrā rāhuketuśanaiścarāḥ ।।

teṣāṃ tathā phalaṃ vidyāt saṃnipāte yathākramam । ete nava grahā jñeyā vātapittakaphātmakāḥ ।।

eṣāṃ prakṛtitulyānāṃ niṣiktānāṃ tu teṣu vai । saṃyogeṣu ca jātānāṃ tulya prakṛtitā bhavet ।।

arkenduprabhavā deham upatiṣṭhanti dehinaḥ । tasmān niṣicyamāneṣu vātapittakapheṣu yaḥ ।।

eṣām anyatamo deho yātiriktaḥ prakāśate । pracakṣate sā prakṛtiḥ prakṛtijñānakovidāḥ ।।

tatra ye mānisvāṅgāni ṛjavaḥ kalahapriyāḥ । uṣṇāḥ kapilaromāṇāaḥ svedanā anavekṣaṇāḥ ।।

bahvāśidurbhagāś caiva mṛdvaṅgāḥ śiśirapriyāḥ । lālanāḥ śithilāṅgāś ca priyāś ca priyāś ca lavaṇās tathā ।।

tanutvaṅnakharomāṇas tv ācāryās tīkṣṇa eva ca । valīpalitabhūyiṣṭhās tathā khalatino narāḥ ।।

glayate śuṣyate caiṣām āśu mālyānulepanam । dāhātmikāḥ śaśāṅke api pittaprakṛtayas tu te ।।

svapne caiva prapaśyanti diśaḥ kanakapiṅgalāḥ । maṇḍalāni samūhāṃś ca dikṣu pītāruṇaprabhān ।।

śṛṅgārimadirān deśāñ śuṣkāṃ malajalāṃ mahīm । śuṣkagulmadrumalatā dahyamānaṃ mahad vanam ।।

viśuṣkāṇi ca vastrāṇi rudhirāṅgāṃs tathaiva ca । dahanādīṃś ca devāṃś ca raktam induṃ sugandhikān ।।

palāśāni ca puṣpāṇi karṇikāravanāni ca । digdāhavidyucchulkāś ca dīpyamānaṃ ca pāvakam ।।

bhūyiṣṭhaṃ bhūṣitāś cāpi pibanti subahūdakam । saritsaravanānteṣu kūpaprasravaṇeṣu ca ।।

uṣṇārtāḥ śītakāmās tu nimajjanti pibanti ca । kalahaṃ caiva kurvanti duḥkhāny anubhavanti ca ।।

strībhiś caiva vimānyante kṣayante klāmayanti ca । ity evaṃ paittikā jñeyāḥ prakṛtisvapnalakṣaṇe ।।

prakṛtisvapnabhāvaiś ca śleṣmikāṇy api me śṛṇu । snigdhakeśanakhaśmaśrutatatvagroma[bhāṣiṇaḥ] ।।

mahodarabhojoraskadīrghakeśanakha[dvijāñ] । vaiḍūryopalabaddhe tu saṃnibhair niyamaiḥ śubhaiḥ ।।

sthiropacitasarvāṅgā bhavanti sukhabhāginaḥ । śirodarakaṭiskandhapakṣayor vimalekṣaṇāḥ ।।

priyāḥ priyamvadāḥ śūrāḥ kṛtajñā dṛḍhabhaktayaḥ । cirād gṛhṇanti suciraṃ gṛhītaṃ dhārayanti ca ।।

na krudhyanti cirāt kruddhāḥ saṃbhavanty antakopamāḥ । pūjābhir vipulāṃ bhūmim āvahanti kulasya ca ।।

khyāpayanti ca sarvatra guṇaiś ca vipulair yaśaḥ । māṃśoṣṇatātimadhurapayohārātha suprajāḥ ।।

na cirāc chuṣyate caiṣāṃ toyamālyānulepanam । nimīlitāsyanayanā niḥśabdā niḥprakampinaḥ ।।

svapanty ekena pārśvena ciraṃ sukhanibodhanāḥ । nātiduḥkhena jīvanti votpadyante sukhena tu ।।

śyāmāḥ śyāmāvadātāś ca śrīmanto adṛḍharogiṇaḥ । alpāśidīrghakāmās tu bhavanty arthasahiṣṇavaḥ ।।

kṣutpipāsāsahāś cāpi kaphaprakṛtayo narāḥ । svapneṣu caiva paśyanti ramyaṃ candanakānanam ।।

vikuḍmalapalāśāni pauṇḍarīkavanāni ca । śubhāś ca śiśiraprāyā nadyaḥ śubhajalāvahāḥ ।।

tuṣāreṇāvṛtāś cāpi himavāghapaṭalāni ca । muktāmaṇisuvāśṛṅgā mṛṇālaphalakāni ca ।।

varāhakhaḍgamahiṣā mṛgāś ca rathakuñjarāḥ । spaṣṭatāraṃ tu haṃsāś ca vyopoḍhanti nabhastalam ।।

kundagokṣīragaurābhir indoḥ kīrṇagabhastiṣu । protphullakumudākārā vyomni sudhāmbusaprabhaiḥ ।।

rājahaṃsapratīkāśaṃ śaśāṅkaṃ cāmaladyutim । śubhrāṇi ca vimānāni phalāni madhurāṇi ca ।।

kṛtapuṣpopahārāṇi mahānti bhavanāni ca । brāhmaṇān yajñavādāṃś ca dadhikṣīrāmṛtāni ca ।।

striyaś ca paramodāktāḥ suveṣāḥ svabhyalaṃkṛtāḥ । madhuraśvetapītāni prāyaśaś ciram eva tu ।।

svapneṣu caivaṃ paśyanti kaphaprakṛtayo narāḥ । prakṛtisvapnabhāveṣu vātikāny api lakṣayet ।।

calāś ca calavikrāntāḥ kṣipramkṣipraṃ pralāpinaḥ । suptāḥ pralāpinas tv anye kaṣāyakaṭukapriyāḥ ।।

tvagromanakhadantoṣṭhapāṇipādatalādiṣu । rūkṣasphuṭitadurdarśā durbalā duḥkhabhāginaḥ ।।

kaṭhinopacitāṅgāś ca bhrāntacittāphutekṣaṇāḥ । lāpino mṛdavaḥ krūrā vidyād asthirabuddhayaḥ ।।

nṛtyagītakathāśīla jambhino duḥkhabhāginaḥ । hrasvalomāḥ suvapuṣo durbalā dhamanās tathā ।।

kṣāmā bhinnāḥ sadoṣāś ca satataṃ vānavasthitāḥ । hastanakhatvagoṣṭhānāṃ pādānāṃ ca vikāriṇaḥ ।।

akasmāt kopanāś cāpi rodanā dhamānās tathā । paraprakṛtiśīlāś ca valganāsphoṭanapriyāḥ ।।

durbalāḥ śiśirāś cāpi vātaprakṛtayo naraḥ । svapneṣu caiva paśyanti vātābhravimalā diśaḥ ।।

mārutavegatuṅgāni bhuvanāni vānāni ca । śyāmatārāgrahagaṇaṃ vidhvastārkendumaṇḍalam ।।

dhārācaradbhir viśvābhaiḥ saṃkulaṃ gaganaṃ ghanaiḥ । bhramantaḥ pakṣisaṃghāś ca mṛgāś codbhrāntayūthapāḥ ।।

anyāś cāpu śambarāś ca girigahvarakānanāḥ । bhramanti ghnanti dhāvanti ūrdhvebhyaḥ prapatanti ca ।।

svapneṣv etāni paśyanti vātaprakṛtayo narāḥ । miśrasvapnasvabhāveṣu saṃnipātātmakāḥ viduḥ ।।

etās tisraḥ prakṛtayaḥ saṃsṛṣṭāś ca sarvaśaḥ ।।

samyak karaṇavijñānaṃ tathā svapnād bhavet phalam । śubhaṃ vāpi aśubhaṃ vāpi nirdeṣṭavyam aśeṣataḥ ।।

yenayenendriyārthena viddhaḥ svapiti mānavaḥ । tasyatasyendriyārthasya suptaḥ karmāṇi paśyati ।।

prakṛtyākṛtasaṃkalpasaṃbhavā devatāsv api । svapnamālāṃ tu yaḥ paśyed yāṃ tu dṛṣṭvā na tu smaret ।।

naite phalaṃ prayacchanti gargasya vacanaṃ yathā । prakṛtyānūkajān āhur eke śubhaphalodayān ।।

sārasvataṃ yathānūkaṃ saṃghātasaṃśrayaṃ śṛṇu । dṛṣṭvā bhogam asuptavyaṃ tataḥ prāpya śubhaṃ phalam ।।

svapnaprakṛtibhāvaṃ tu jñātvā tattvaṃ samādiśet ।।

gṛhṇīta samudgendvindravāyvagnyarkanadīṃ kṣitim । samudraṃ vāhinīṃ dvīpaṃ laṅghayed vā vasuṃdharām ।।

vāhinīṃ caturaṅgāṃ ca jīvachattrapatākinīm । dorbhyāṃ ca pratigṛhṇīyāt tathāketuvasuṃdharām ।।

ekapuṣkariṇīparṇe sauvarṇe bhāhane api vā । sarpiṣā pāyasaṃ bhuṅkte gāṃ duhan yaś ca budhyati ।।

pariveṣaḥ svayaṃ candre yo anavastravasuṃdharām । parvatāgraṃ samāruhya kṣitiṃ yaś cāvalokayet ।।

ā kaṇṭhaṃ majjate yo hi mānavaḥ śoṇitārṇave । rathena siṃhayuktena parvataṃ cādhirohati ।।

mahīṃ vā kampayed yas tu cālayed vā punar girīm । śvetam aśvam athāruhya pāṇḍuraṃ vāpu yo gajam ।।

bhuṅkte puṣkariṇīparṇe pāyasaṃ vāpi sarpiṣā । aṅgavṛddhiṃ śirovṛddhiṃ prāpnuyād yas tu mānavaḥ ।।

brāhmaṇo vāpi rājā vā svapne yad abhiṣecayet । rājā tu pārthivo jñeyaḥ kroṣṭuker vacanaṃ yathā ।।

śiro vā chidyate yasya vimānaṃ śoṇitaṃ tathā । senāpatyaṃ mahac cāyur arthalābhaṃ tathaiva ca ।।

vibhūṣaṇaṃ ca vidyāṃ ca karṇachedam avāpnuyāt । hastachede labhet putraṃ bāhuchede dhanāgamam ।।

uraḥ sahasralābhaḥ syāt pādachede tathaiva ca । uraḥprajananachede atyantaṃ sukhaṃ dedhate ।।

chatrādarśaphaloṣṇīṣaśuklamālyāgame tathā । matsyamāṃsadadhikṣīrarudhirāgama eva ca ।।

śaktyaṅkuśapatākānāṃ chattrāsidhanuṣāṃ tathā । vimalānāṃ jalānāṃ ca pūrvoktaṃ tu nidarśanam ।।

sūkarakharavāhyānāṃ vadhaś caikapaśor api । narayuktasya yānasya nikṣiptasya gavasya ca ।।

darśanaṃ cāpy adṛṣṭānām agamyāgamanaṃ tathā । kṣīriṇāṃ phalamvṛkṣāṇāṃ darśanārohaṇāni ca ।।

viṣadarśanadaṃsparśo dhānyenotsaṅgapūraṇam । dasyubhir hanyamānasya rudataḥ pratibodhanam ।।

dvijebhyo dadhimāṃsasya lābhaḥ piśitabhakṣane । abhakṣyabhakṣaṇe cāpu śvetamālyānulepanam ।।

ghātanaṃ śvāpadānāṃ ca pāṇau ca rudhirāgamaḥ । arthalābhāya boddhavyaḥ suhṛnmitrasamāgamaḥ ।।

labhate nātra saṃdeho bhārgavasya vaco tathā । śuklāḥ sumanasaḥ kanyā dadhi gobrāhmaṇaṃ vṛṣam ।।

daivatāni nṛpādhyakṣāḥ pāṇḍurāṇi gṛhāṇi ca । suhṛdaḥ saphalā vṛkṣā nakṣatrāṇy amalaṃ jalam ।।

iṣṭakalyāṇaśabdāś ca śuklāmbaradharāḥ striyaḥ । nabho vimalanakṣatraṃ pāvakaṃ viṣamārciṣam ।।

dṛṣṭvā yas tatkṣaṇaṃ budhyet tasya kalyāṇam ādiśet । vṛkṣān gulmāṃś ca vallīś ca svagṛhe puṣpitā naraḥ ।।

śuklavāsāḥ striyaś cāpi yaḥ paśyec chrīs tu taṃ bhajet । viṣaśoṇitadigdhāṅgaḥ prītīm āpnoti mānavaḥ ।।

dīptāṅgo labhate bhūmiṃ vardhamānāṅga eva ca । parivāryābhirudito bāndhavaiḥ karuṇaṃ naraḥ ।।

śokārto labhate tuṣṭiṃ mṛtaś cāyur avāpnuyāt । śuklamālyāmbaradharo dahyamānaḥ pralīyate ।।

yaḥ svapne saṃbhayed ugraṃ pārakyaṃ so artham āpnuyāt । nāgadantakamudrāṃ ca vīṇāṃ mālāñjanaṃ tathā ।।

kāñcanaṃ paśyate yas tu tathā strīṃ labhate naraḥ । uḍḍīyamānān vihagān tathā puṣkariṇīgatān ।।

mattaṃ kareṇum āruhya parastrīṃ labhate naraḥ । kumārīṃ labhate nārīm āyasair nigaḍair naraḥ ।।

baddhvā navāṃ tu yo mālām utpālānāṃ vibudhyate । kavāṭale ca saṃyukte tathaivotpalahastake ।।

bhṛṅgāro darpaṇo vāpi labdhvā putrāgamaṃ vadet । taḍāgārāmakūpānāṃ purārañjanayor api ।।

pūrṇakumbhasya cādeśyaṃ varṣam uttaraṇād bhruvam । cipiṭaḥ kālako nagnaḥ śravaṇo mehate yadi ।।

vidikthaḥ sravate cārmiḥ svapne varṣaṃ samādiśet । sūkarīṃ mahiṣīṃ vāpi hastinīṃ śakunīṃ tathā ।।

svapne yadā prasūyeta subhikṣaṃ nirdiśet tadā । śayanāsanayānāni gṛhagrāmapurāṇi ca ।।

yeṣāṃ svapne pralīyante teṣāṃ vṛddhim athādiśet । govṛṣaṃ puruṣaṃ vṛkṣaṃ hastinaṃ parvataṃ gṛham ।।

narasyārohaṇād vṛddhiḥ pāṇḍurāṇi viśeṣataḥ । daivatāni dvijā gāvaḥ pitaro liṅgino grahāḥ ।।

yad vadanti naraṃ svapne tat tathaiva vinirdiśet । saritsarasamudrāṇāṃ taraṇe śokatāraṇam ।।

narasya śoṇitaṃ pītvā prakṛtāṇl labhate naraḥ । candrendradhvajasūryāṇāṃ patane nṛpater bhayam ।।

mahārṇavamahendrāṇāṃ kṣobhe kṣobhaṃ vinirdiśet । keśaśmaśrunakhānāṃ ca patane śokasaṃbhavaḥ ।।

kṛmiṇatvaṃ bhaved dhanyaṃ kroṣṭuker vacanaṃ yathā । kravyādair damṣṭribhiś cāpi vināśo bhūtavigrahe ।।

śastramuṣṭiprahāreṣu vijānīyāj jvarāgamam । yadyad ujjvalavad dravyaṃ tattat sukhakaraṃ bhavet ।।

yadyad virudhyate vāpi svapne tat tasya nirdiśet । [nopānena] prajātānāṃ darśane sthānam ādiśet ।।

upānahabalachattradarśane ca grhe tathā । hasadbhir vā parivṛto nṛtyadbhiḥ svajanair api ।।

saṃyuktaṃ sūkarakharair uṣṭraiḥ kṛṣṇacatuṣpadaiḥ । ratham āruhya yo yāyād akṣatas tu yugaṃdharaḥ ।।

prakīrṇakeśo hriyate dakṣiṇenāpareṇa vā । dakṣiṇenāgatā kanyā kālikākulavāsinī ।।

nīyate puruṣair yaś ca pāśahastair viśeṣataḥ । nirastānāṃ viṣamāṇāṃ pretenākuśalaṃ bhavet ।।

piṇyākasya tilānāṃ ca karṣāsu lavaṇasya ca । rūḍhaśmaśrunakhānāṃ ca duścelānāṃ ca vāsasām ।।

virāgavāsasāṃ vāpi vikṛtānāṃ tathaiva ca । sarīsṛpāṇāṃ vyālānāṃ śatrūṇāṃ cāpi darśanam ।।

kṛṣṇānāṃ vāpi sarveṣāṃ rājadvijavṛṣād ṛte । darśanaṃ gamanaṃ vāpi śokam āyāsavedanam ।।

padmair vā jalabhāṇḍair vā krīḍitāyāsadarśanam । padmāni vāharet svapne hastachedam avāpnuyāt ।।

prasanne tu dhruvaṃ śoko rajjuchede mriyeta saḥ । rūḍhasya srotasā śoko mṛtyuḥ sriotasi naśyataḥ ।।

dantā bāhuṃ tathā śīrṣṇo chinnāṃśadravyadarśanam । bhrātaraṃ pitaraṃ vāpi putraṃ vā nāśayanti te ।।

dvāre vā sārgale vāpi śayyāṃ śakhāṃ tathaiva ca । svapne yasya pranaśyanti bhāryā tasya vinaśyati ।।

kṛkalāso vṛko vāpi puruṣo vāpi piṅgalaḥ । śayyāṃ yasyādhirohanti bhāryā tasyāpi duṣyati ।।

svapne yo mārayet sarpaṃ śvetapītakalohitam । kṛṣṇasya vā śiraś chindyāt putras tasya vinaśyati ।।

rājaputraś ca coraś ca rājabhṛṭyaś ca yo bhavet । tasya svapnāḥ phalaṃ dadyur eteṣu yad udāhṛtam ।।

yeṣāṃ lābhe bhaved vṛddhis teṣāṃ nāśe guṇo bhavet । yeṣāṃ lābhe bhaved dhānis teṣāṃ lābhe guṇo bhavet ।।

śubhaṃ dṛṣṭvā tu yaḥ svapne punaḥ paśyaty apūjitam । śubhaṃ vāpy aśubhaṃ vāpi yat paścāt tatphalaṃ labhet ।।

svapnās tu prathame yāme saṃvatsaravipākinaḥ । dvitīye aṣṭasu māseṣu tṛtīye tu tadardhabhāk ।।

māsiko govisarge tu sadyaḥpākaḥ prabhātike kālaḥ pañcasv avasthāsu śarvaryāḥ kīrtitaḥ pṛthak ।।

viprebhyaḥ śaktito dānaṃ śāntiḥ svaṣṭyayanādayaḥ । vināśayanti duḥsvapnaṃ prātaś cāśvatthasevanam ।।

aśvatthasevā tilapātradānaṃ gosparśanaṃ brāhmaṇatarpaṇaṃ ca । śāntikriyā svastyayanakriyā ca duḥsvapnam etāni vināśayanti ।।

vasnakanakadānadevapūjāgurugoṣṭhaniṣevitāni kuryuḥ । dvijavṛṣabḥgavāśvapārthivānāṃ darśanam itihāsamaṅgalāḥ syuḥ ।।

imān dṛṣṭvāśubhān svapnān prātar utthāya satvaraḥ । nadīsaṃgamatoyena mukhaṃ saṃmārjya tattvataḥ ।।

hiraṇyavarṇābhir udakaṃ śaṃtātīyamayobhuvā । abhimantrya prayatnena mukhaṃ saṃmārjya tattvataḥ ।।

yo na jīvaḥ paro apehi vidma te svapna vedanam । rocanā sarṣapā mṛdā samit sakusumaṃ dadhi ।।

gām ajaṃ kanakaṃ sattvaṃ kumārīṃ brāhmaṇaṃ śubham । abhivandya nṛpo yāyāt suhṛdāṃś ca manoharān ।।

yadā tu yātrāṃ nṛpatiḥ kartum icched vidhānavit । atha svastyayanaiḥ [saumyaiḥ saumyais tam abhimantrayet ।।

tataḥ śuklāmbaradharo vāgyataḥ saṃyatendriyaḥ । tāṃ niśaṃ saṃviśed rājā bhūmau caivābhimantrayet ।।

[anyathaiva hi na svapnadarśanārthanidarśanam] । evam uktvā narapatiḥ prayatātmā tataḥ svapet ।।

praśastasvapnatāṃ dṛṣṭvā tato yāyān narādhipaḥ । svapneṣu vāpraśastreṣu tataḥ śāntiṃ samārabhet ।।

māhendrīm amṛtāṃ raudrīṃ kuryād vāpy aparājitām । kauberīṃ vā prayuñjīta ādityāṃ vā sadakṣiṇām ।।

rajanikaradivākarau karābhyāṃ spṛśati yadā grasate atha vā narendraḥ । lavaṇajalanidhiṃ nadīṃ ca dorbhyāṃ tarati hradāpadakardamaṃ tamo vā ।।

naraturagamahīruhān nagān vā bhavanacarān na virohayed gajān vā । jvalanamaraṇakālavṛddhayogān yadi nṛpa ātmagatāṃś ca paśyatīha ।।

yadi ca nṛpatir ātmano abhracārair bhramati mahīṃ sapurāṃ parikṣipet । yadi ca sa ciramagnagātramātro bhramati nṛpo grasate atha medinīṃ vā ।।

yadi ca jayati damṣṭriṇo narān vā yadi ca bhavet sitamālyadānadhārī । yadi ca ruditi caivam ādi dṛṣṭvā paraviṣayaṃ hṛṣitas tatas tu yāyāt ।।

sa kaluṣasalilāvapāṃsumagno madhugh}ṛtatailavasāpradigdhagātraḥ । malinavasanajīrṇaraktavāsā yadi sumanobhir alaṃkṛtaḥ svayaṃ vā ।।

svapiti jayati khādati prahṛṣṭo vilapati nartati gāyanaprahāsaiḥ । bhavati ca mudito labheta kanyāṃ yadi nṛpatir nayaśo bhavej jayārthī ।।

mayakharasūkaravānarādhirūḍho hṛtamukuṭāṅgadavastracihnanagnaḥ । vinihataturagadvipo narendro yadi patitadhvajavāṃs tato na yāyāt ।।

narapatir aparājitaḥ parair yo yadi ca paraiḥ parihasyate madadbhiḥ । yadi ca bhavati durdṛśograrūpo na sa īdṛśakaḥ parān prayāyāt ।।

svapnān dṛṣṭvā śubhān rājā japadbhir abhimantritaḥ । yuktaḥ sa śakunair bhūpa utpātagaṇavarjitaḥ ।।

sahāyavān susaṃnaddho nimittajñaiḥ samanvitaḥ । sumuhūrte sunakṣatre prayāyād vasudhādhipaḥ ।।

tailābhyaktaś ca kṛsarāṃ bhuṅkte tailapariplutām । mātaraṃ praviśed yaś ca jvalitaṃ ca hutāśanam ।।

prāsadāt parvatāgrād vā pated yaś cāpi mānavaḥ । magnaḥ kardamakūpeṣu jale yaś cāpi naśyati ।।

drumam unmūlayed yas tu paśyed rājñopasevakam । kumārīvadane yaś ca vānarīṃ vādhigacchati ।।

raktakaṇṭhagate vāpi yasya kaṇṭhe visarjati । vivarṇo vāpi pāśair yo badhyate mriyate tu saḥ ।।

kāṃsyaṃ vā kāṃsyapātrīṃ vā yasya tejo adhirohati । acireṇaiva kālena so asinā vadhyate naraḥ ।।

yūpāgram adhiruhyātha nāvāgram adhirohati । acireṇaiva kālena śūlāgraṃ so adhirohati ।।

muṇḍaḥ kāṣāyavāso vā śvetaraktapaṭo api vā । svapne yasyādhirohanti vyādhis tasyādhirohati ।।

śvā vā ajagaro godhā tarakṣu śalyako api vā । kṛkalāso rurur vyāghro dvīpī yasyādhirohati ।।

ahiś ca raudrajaṭilaḥ śvetaraktapaṭo api vā । svapne yam upatiṣṭhanti vyādhis tam upatiṣṭhati ।।

mahībhasmapradigdhāṅgo nirāvaraṇa eva ca । samasyānāṃ sajātānām utsavānāṃ ca darśanam ।।

durgam adhvānagamanam anūpānāṃ ca sevanam । abhyaṅgaś caiva gātrāṇāṃ tilagomayakardamaiḥ ।।

suvarṇamaṇimuktāni bhūṣaṇaṃ rajatāni ca । darśanaṃ vāpy athaiteṣāṃ vyādhīnāṃ saṃpraveśanam ।।

gāyanaṃ nartanaṃ hāsyaṃ vivāhakaraṇaṃ tathā । ānandaś ca pramodaś ca vyasanasya ca darśanam ।।

purāṇaghṛtadigdhāṅgo naro maraṇam āpnuyāt । evam uktā mahotpātā vividhāḥ pūrvacoditaḥ ।।

ulkābhedās tathā pañca pariveṣā nava smṛtāḥ । digdāho aṣṭavidhaḥ prokto vidyud aṣṭavidhā tathā ।।

catvāro bhūmikampāś ca nirghāto aṣṭavidhas tathā । viṃśatī dve ca vijñeyā bhedā hy ulkādiṣu smṛtāḥ ।।

mahotpātāś ca bahavaḥ śāntiyogeṣu kīrtitāḥ । teṣu sarveṣu vidhivac chāntikāmo narādhipaḥ ।।

atharvāṇaṃ ca vṛṇuyāt sarvaśāstravidaṃ nṛpaḥ । sa vṛto bhayabhītena śamanārthaṃ mahātmanā ।।

prajānām abhayaṃ samyag dāpayet pṛthivīpatiḥ । anantaraṃ gavāṃ pūjā brāhmaṇānāṃ viśeṣataḥ ।।

devatāyatane sadyo dohān bhūmau prakārayet । satataṃ cānulipyas tu puṣpair dhūpair yathoditaiḥ ।।

pradīpair vividhaiḥ śubhraiḥ sarvadikṣuprakalpitaiḥ । tathā balyupahāraiś ca pāyasāpūpasaṃyutaiḥ ।।

hṛdyair bahuvidhair bhakṣaiḥ sarvadikṣuprakalpitaiḥ । tasminn evāntare śānte goṣṭhe vā jalasaṃnidhau ।।

nirgatya nagarād vāpi śucau deśe samāhitaḥ । vṛṇuyāc chāntitattvajñān utpātavihitāñ śubhān ।।

ṣoḍaśāṣṭau vṛtās te ca puraścaraṇaśodhitāḥ । aṅgāni kuryur anye ca śatasaṃkhyā dvijottamāḥ ।।

udayāste sukhāsīnā japaṃ kuryur atandritāḥ । te sadasyā iti proktā vācane yajñakarmaṇi ।।

teṣāṃ variṣṭhaḥ śāntijña upadraṣṭā manoharaḥ । sarvakarmasu vettā ya ānayet so apy athādarāt ।।

bhūmiṃ saṃśodhya vidhivat kṛtvā tatra ca maṇḍapam । vidhivat kalpayed vediṃ yajñapātrāṇi ca svayam ।।

evaṃ yathoktavidhinā agnimanthanapūrvakām । mahāśāntiṃ prayuñjīta sarvopadravanāśinīm ।।

annair vastraiś ca vividhaiḥ saṃyuktāṃ bahudakṣiṇām । kārayitvā mahāśāntiṃ varaṃ gāṃ ca nivedayet ।।

gṛham ābharaṇaṃ chattram anaḍudvājinaṃ tathā । kuñjaraṃ vā tathā dattvā ghaṇtābharaṇabhūṣitam ।।

mahat sukham avāpnoti kāryasiddhiṃ ca vindati । kāryasiddhiṃ ca vindati ।।

om upasaṃgamya munayaḥ sarvajñaṃ śāntamānasam । apṛcchan gatamātsyaryaṃ bhṛguṃ brahmavidāṃ varam ।।

kāmā hi bahavo loke saṃsthitā bhinnasādhanāḥ । ekam eva paraṃ teṣāṃ samyak tvaṃ brūhy asaṃśayam ।।

samāsena pravakṣyāmi yena sarvaṃ pradadyate । atipraśno ayam udgīrṇas tathāpi kathayāmy aham ।।

sarvārthasādhanārthāya śrutir āṅgirasī hitā । svatejasā prajvalantī hṛdayaṃ tad athārvaṇām ।।

prabhāvaṃ tasya vakṣyāmi upariṣṭād yathāvidhi । duḥsādhyāni nimittāni tāni vedmi hi kāni cit ।।

akāle yasya jāyante dantāḥ keśair vivarjitaḥ । prabhūtalambakeśo vā tathā hīnādhikāṅguliḥ ।।

dvidantaś cāpi jāyeta tasya karma svaśākhikam । svaśākhāyāṃ tu yat proktaṃ kuryād vātharvaṇaṃ vidhim ।।

dvimūrdhā vā trinetro vā tathaikākṣir dvināsikaḥ । hīnahasto aparo hy arthe na tv atharvaśirāḥ sa ca ।।

kṛtopacāraḥ pañca sapta śuddhātmā sādhyasatkṛtaḥ । sa śāntyudakam ācamya śāntavṛkṣasamīpataḥ ।।

śāntavṛkṣasamidbhis tu tilais trimadhurais tathā । homaṃ kuryād atharvā tu tena nandati satkulam ।।

na labhed yady atharvāṇaṃ kuryād daśaguṇaṃ svayam । mahāvyāhṛtihomaṃ ca sāvitraṃ japam eva ca ।।

vikṛtāṅgo adhikāṅgo vā jāto hīnāṅgo eva vā । kulasyādbhutam atyarthaṃ tad atharvā śamaṃ nayet ।।

kapyuṣṭrebhagavādīnāṃ jāyante aṅgamukhaiḥ samāḥ । yasmin rāṣṭre nṛpas tatra ṣaṇmāsādd hi vinaśyati ।।

kapyādayo va jāyante anyasya tulyagātrakāḥ । vṛkṣe anyavṛkṣajaṃ puṣpaṃ jāyate phalam eva vā ।।

dvijottamam atharvāṇaṃ tatrecchec chāntim ātmanaḥ । kārayeta mahāśāntiṃ rāṣṭrasya ca purasya ca ।।

upasthite rājyanāśe mahāraurava eva vā । durbhikṣe marake vāpi anāvṛṣṭibhaye api vā ।।

sarvaṃ rāṣṭre vinaśyeta sasyaṃ śalabhamūṣakaiḥ । akasmān nirjalā vā syād aśoṣā vā mahāsarit ।।

tathānyeṣv apu anukteṣu ghoreṣūpasthiteṣu ca । kuryuḥ śāntim atharvāṇo dvijā hy eteṣu bheṣajam ।।

labhate rājyayogyo api na rājyaṃ raja^nandanaḥ । paṭhan na labhate vidyāṃ dvijaḥ śṛṇvann api śrutam ।।

ādhitsur api nādhānaṃ kuryād āvāsam eva ca । kanyā pariṇinīṣur vā kāmyeṣv iṣṭapatiṃ na ca ।।

vandhyā vā mṛtavatsā yā durbhagā strīprasū ca yā । sakṛtprasūtā yā nārī garbhaṃ gṛhṇāti naiva ca ।।

sūtikāle apy atikrānte garbhe sphuraṇavaty api । na sūtiṃ labhate yā tu bahuputrīyate ca yā ।।

kṛṣīvalaḥ kṛṣīvalaṃ jayaty āyudhajīvy api । jayāpsur vyavahāre vā saubhāgyaṃ sārvabhautikam ।।

athāpahantuṃ bhayam evamādikaṃ yadābhilaṣyet phalam uktam eva vā । tadāṅgirasyaṃ varamantrasaṃpadā sphurantam uccaiḥ śaraṇaṃ vrajed dvijam ।।

rātrau dvichāyavṛkṣaṃ vā kusvapnaṃ vāpi riṣṭadam । divā grahān nirīkṣeta bhūmikampaivamādikam ।।

jvālādbhutāny atha proktāni yāni ulkādibhedā gaditās tathā ye । svapnādbhutāny api vānyādbhutāni gṛheṣu yāny arthavido vadanti ।।

eteṣu śāntiṃ kurvīta amṛtāṃ vā sadakṣiṇām । raudrīṃ vā vaiśvadevīṃ vā abhayāṃ vāparājitām ।।

gobhūhiraṇyavastrānnais tilair vā saphalaiḥ śubhaiḥ । upānacchattrasaṃyuktāṃ gurvābharaṇasaṃyutām ।।

pratipatīyathoktaṃ vā yaḥ kurvīta vidhānvit । etad utpātajaṃ sarvaṃ mahāśāntyā pralīyate ।।

yasya rājño janapade atharvā śāntipāragaḥ । nivasaty api tadrāṣṭraṃ vardhate nirupadravam ।।

yasya rājño janapade sa nāsti vividhair bhayaiḥ । pīḍyate tasya tad rāṣṭraṃ paṅle gaur iva majjati ।।

tasmād rājā viśeṣeṇa atharvāṇaṃ jitendriyam । dānasaṃmānasatkārair nityaṃ samabhipūjayet ।।

nityaṃ ca kārayec chāntiṃ grahaṛkṣāṇi pūjayet । bhūmidohān prakurvīta devatāyataneṣu ca ।।

catuṣpatheṣu goṣṭheṣu tīrtheṣv apsu ca kārayet । gotarpaṇaṃ ca vidhivat sarvadoṣavināśanam ।।

evaṃ tu khyāpayan rājā sarvakālaṃ jitendriyaḥ । anantaṃ sukham āpnoti kṛtsnāṃ bhuṅkte vasuṃdharām ।।

upasthitaṃ mṛtyum api dvijottamaḥ śamaṃ nayet । adhītyātharvāṅgirasas tādṛśam ādhṛtavrataḥ ।।

dyutiṃ prabhāṃ sadā sphuran mantrapavitravān naraḥ । nṛpe dhanini cānyatra śāntyāptvā dakṣiṇāṃ budhaḥ ।।

sīdan kuṭumbakaḥ poṣaṃ gṛhītvānyat samutsṛjet । triḥ saṃhitāṃ haviṣyādyaṃ japet kṛcchraṃ ca śuddhaye ।।

sāvitrīlakṣam ayutaṃ sahasaram atha cottaram । japtvā daśāṃśako homaḥ kāryo doṣānusārataḥ ।।

śatīranirmalo yas tu nārcito api dvijottaram । amatsarī nitāntaṃ yaḥ so atra śāntiṃ samārabhet ।।

evaṃvidho aṅgirā yatra yāni sādhyāni sādhayet । na nyūnaṃ tatra kiṃcit syād iti tad bhṛgubhāṣitam ।।

laghuśāntyudakavidhinā gāyatryā vāpu atharvakaḥ । kuryāt sarvam idaṃ jānann atharvahṛdayaṃ budhaḥ ।।

ye na jānanty adhītā api śrutim āṅgirasīṃ dvijāḥ । atharvahṛdayaṃ cāpi na te vedavidaḥ smṛtāḥ ।।

atharvahṛdayaṃ vettā atharvā paramaḥ smṛtaḥ । nātharvaṇe apy idaṃ deyaṃ guror vidveṣayāyini ।।

anyaśākhyaṃ dvijo mohāt pāṭhayan pravilīyate । atharvahṛdayaṃ buddhvā yaḥ paṭhed bhaktipūrvakam ।।

atharvā nādbhutaṃ tasya śāntir eva sadā bhavet । śāntir eva sadā bhavet ।।

oṃ saṃpūjya vidhivat prājñaṃ vidvāṃso munayaḥ purā । apṛcchan bhṛgum avyagraṃ sarvasattvahite ratam ।।

lokatrayaniviṣṭānām utpātānām anekadhā । bhinnānāṃ śamanaṃ noktaṃ vada tv asaṃśayaṃ mune ।।

pratyuvāca bhṛgur viprān śṛṇutāhitamānasaḥ । utpātaśamanatritvaṃ kathyamānam asaṃśayam ।।

tatra viprān pravakṣyāmi duriṣṭaśamanakṣamān । atharvāṅgiraso vede vidhijñān sarvakarmaṇām ।।

ahiṃsāsatyadākṣiṇyaśaucaśraddhāsamanvitāḥ । śrutismṛtisadācārāḥ kulaśīlavayo anvitāḥ ।।

teṣām ekaḥ pradhānatve yaḥ śānto dvijasattamaḥ । bhṛgvaṅgirovid atyarthaṃ śuciḥ syāt sādhusaṃmataḥ ।।

brahmāṇaṃ taṃ nṛpaḥ kuryād dhotāraṃ sarvavedinam । evam ukte bhṛguṃ viprāḥ procur vigatakalmaṣam ।।

hotāro bhūmibhartṝṇāṃ mahāśānteḥ prakīrtitāḥ । nanu kṣīṇe vidvan svadharmapracyute api vā ।।

tatra śāntau prayuktāyāṃ kasya śāntiphalaṃ bhavet । nṛpo apy adhārmikaḥ kuryād brahmaṇas tarpaṇaṃ purā ।।

tataḥ kṛtā mahāśāntī rājānaṃ pāti sarvataḥ । sa vṛtaḥ pāvanaṃ gacched dvijānāṃ pāvanāya vai ।।

dvādaśāhaṃ vrataṃ tatra payomūlaphalāśanaiḥ ।।

trīṇi tryahāṇi kurvīta payomūlaphalaiḥ śubhaiḥ । anaśnaṃś ca tryahaṃ dhīraḥ sa puraścaraṇo bhavet ।।

tathaikonaṃ śataṃ nṝṇāṃ śuśrūṣūṇām akalmaṣam । anuktavac ca tryahaṃ tat karmaṇaḥ karaṇe kṣamam ।।

kṛcchraṃ cāpi hitaṃ kṛtvā kuryuḥ karma samāhitāḥ । śuddhātmāno japair homair vaidikair vītamatsarāḥ ।।

tataḥ paraṃ purodhaḥsu divyaṃ tatram avāpnuyāt । grahātithyaṃ ca saṃrabhya diśāṃ yāgaṃ ca sarvataḥ ।।

nakṣatreṣu ca sarveṣu yāgaṃ kṛtvā vidhānataḥ । tato amṛtamahāśāntyā sthāpayet padmasaṃbhavam ।।

sāvitryā lakṣahomaṃ tu bhaume tiṣṭhed viśāradāḥ । kuryur deyaṃ ca dānānāṃ viprebhyo yasya yat priyam ।।

gobhūmikāñcanāśvānāṃ ratnānāṃ dhānyavāsasām । rathānāṃ vāraṇānāṃ ca dānaṃ kāmam ataḥ param ।।

tuṣyeyur yena vā viprāḥ saṃbhavo yasya yasya hi । tat tat sarvam upādeyam eṣa dānavidhiḥ smṛtaḥ ।।

dadyāc ca gurave grāmaṃ dhenuṃ vāsoyugaṃ tathā । alaṃkāraiś ca saṃpūjya prīṇayet prītamānasaḥ ।।

anena vidhinā bhaumam adbhutaṃ śamayed guruḥ । eṣa eva vidhir jñeyo viyatye apy adbhutāśraye ।।

viśeṣo ayaṃ tu sāvitryā daśalakṣāṃs tu homayet । homasamāhitamanāḥ kuryāc ca ghṛtakambalam ।।

dhenūnāṃ dvādaśaṃ deyaṃ śataniṣkasamanvitam । gurave dīyamānaṃ tac chamayaty ambarādbhutam ।।

divyādbhuteṣu kartavyaḥ koṭihomasamanvitaiḥ । gosahasraṃ ca dātavyaṃ gurave dakṣiṇāvidhiḥ ।।

eṣa prokto vidhiḥ samyag divyāniṣṭavipatkare । subhikṣakṣemasaṃpattyā prajānāṃ puṣṭivardhanaḥ ।।

koṭihomeṣu sarveṣu dravyabhedāśrayaṃ phalam । śāntipuṣṭyabhicārārthaṃ tan me nigadataḥ śṛṇu ।।

saumyavṛkṣāśrayāḥ kāryāḥ samidhaḥ śāntim icchatā । arkakāśmaryanimbānāṃ samidbhiḥ śatruśātanam ।।

durnāmakaṇṭakambūnāṃ samidbhiś ca viśeṣataḥ । bhagnasphuṭitavṛkṣāṇāṃ phalaṃ śatrunibarhaṇam ।।

bilvapadmotpalānāṃ tu śucideśaprarohiṇām । sarvadā sarvakāmāṃs tu homaiḥ prāpnoti mānavaḥ ।।

tilavrīhiyavādīnāṃ dadhno madhughṛtasya ca । payogodhūmaśālīnāṃ hotā śāntiṃ samārabhet ।।

sarveṣāṃ haviṣāṃ caiva ghṛtaṃ śāntikaraṃ smṛtam । sarvadravye ghṛtaṃ tasmād dhome prakṣepam arhati ।।

yajñopavītinā kāryaṃ śāntikarma vipaścitā । upavītaṃ tu pitryeṣu sarveṣv eva samārabhet ।।

madhvājyadadhidugdheṣu bhakṣyamāṇe vilepane । yantravāhanaśastreṣu bhavaneṣv āyudheṣu ca ।।

darpaṇe bhaktapātre ca maṇimuktāphaleṣu ca । bhūṣaṇeṣu tathānyeṣu śayyāyām āsaneṣu ca ।।

kākolūkakapotānāṃ madhor vā darśanaṃ bhavet । anyeṣāṃ cāpraśastānām āgamo mṛgapakṣiṇām ।।

aśvetānāṃ ca puṣpāṇāṃ sarīsṛpagaṇasya ca । vasālohitamāṃsānām asthimajjāśiroruhām ।।

akasmāc caiva saṃghāte darśane nakhabhasmanām । rasānyatve rasānāṃ ca durgandhe vānimittaje ।।

padmapuṣpākṛtir yatra dṛśyate madhusarpiṣi । kṛsarāpāyase caiva kṣayas tasya dhanāyuṣoḥ ।।

ghṛte vā madhudadhni vā yadā padmākṛtir bhavet । svastiko vāpi dṛśyeta tadā maraṇam ādiśet ।।

vikāro yatra dṛśyeta kṣīrodanahavihṣu vā । śrotriyāya tu tad dadyād bhāvaiva śamayen naraḥ ।।

yatrasthaṃ cādbhutaṃ paśyet tatrāpi pratipādayet । kuryād vā vāruṇīṃ śāntiṃ parameṇa samādhinā ।।

anyākṛtiṣu vāpy etad ye sthāne śāntikārakāḥ । teṣām athākṣayaṃ vidyād āyuṣārthadhanena vā ।।

calite jvalite pāte sphurita utpatite tathā । mahājanagajāśvānāṃ sthāne vidyān mahad bhayam ।।

tatra yudhyanti jātīnāṃ bhayaṃ tat syād asaṃśayam । tatrāpi cārthanicayaiḥ paśubhir vidyayāpi vā ।।

utpātaśamanārthaṃ tu ye kriyā na prayuñjate । narāḥ kṣipraṃ vinaśyante sānvayāḥ saparicchadāḥ ।।

viprāṇāṃ bhojanaṃ kāryaṃ sahasrasyāyutasya vā । balipuṣpopahāraiś ca devatānāṃ prasādanam ।।

kartavyaṃ ca yathānyāyaṃ śāntikarma vipaścitā । evaṃ kṛte bhayaṃ sarvaṃ tatkṣaṇād eva naśyati ।।

śubhāśubhasthitaṃ caiva munayo bhṛgum abruvan । sa pratyuvāca puruṣu saṃvatsarasamāśraye ।।

śītoṣṇavṛṣṭikāleṣu vītadoṣeṣu sarvadā । saṃvatsarākhyaḥ puruṣo nirupadrava ucyate ।।

yadi nirghātabhūkampadigdāhādivivarjitaḥ । ketubhiś caiva yujyeta yadi vādityakīlakaiḥ ।।

anyair vā lokanāśārthair adbhutair nāśanākulaiḥ । tata eṣa viśuddhātmā puruṣaḥ sukham edhate ।।

atha cet sa bahuvidhair adbhutaiḥ parisaṃyutaḥ । saṃvatsaraṃ bhavec chīghraṃ kuryus tacchamanaṃ budhāḥ ।।

tatra śāntiṃ pravakṣyāmi sarvapāpapraṇāśinīm । divyatantravid ācāryo yayā phalam avāpnuyāt ।।

pūrvaṃ tāvad viśuddhātmā sa puraścaraṇo bhavet । devatānāṃ tato yāgaṃ yathāśruti samācaret ।।

yāgaṃ kṛtvā grahāṇāṃ tu nakṣatrāṇāṃ tataḥ param । ṛtūn athārtavāṃś caiva mahādevagaṇādhipān ।।

diśaś ca vidiśaś caiva yamendravaruṇāṃs tathā । viśveśvaraṃ ca viṣṇuṃ ca yajetādbhutakarma ca ।।

sūryācandramasāv agniṃ sarvān grahagaṇāṃs tathā । vāyuṃ tathāśvinau caiva mahāśāntiṃ vidhānataḥ ।।

kuryād devādṛto dhīmān evaṃ doṣaḥ praśāmyati ।।

śvetaṃ vā bhavati payo vilohitaṃ vā pītaṃ vā bhavati hi kṛṣṇapiṅgalaṃ vā । utpātaḥ phalati yathā catuḥprakāras tat sarvaṃ śṛṇuta samāsato mayoktam ।।

viprāṇāṃ bhavati hi śuklam ambudoṣe rājānaṃ sapadi nihanti lohitaṃ ca । pītaṃ ced bhavati nihanti vaiśyavargaṃ śūdrāṇāṃ bhavati hi kṛṣṇapiṅgadoṣe ।।

bījaṃ yatra praroheta phalam atha pramādataḥ । etad atyadbhutaṃ nāma dampatyos tu vināśanam ।।

apūjanāt tu pūjyasya tathāpūjyasya pūjanāt । antaḥkaraṇadoṣāc ca hetoḥ śāntir na jāyate ।।

tasmād vedārthaśāstrajñān vītarāgān amatsarān । paricārakamukhyāṃś ca kārayet kuśalān dvijān ।।

vicāritaṃ ca vidvadbhir niścitaṃ sudhiyā punaḥ । deśakālasamāyuktaṃ karma kuryād vicakṣaṇaḥ ।।

codite karmaṇy anyasmin nānyat kuryād vidhānavit । na ca prārabhya karmāṇi sthātavyaṃ kva cid antare ।।

nāpi kurvīta matimān kadā cit karmasaṃkaram । kurvaṃs tu na tathā karma doṣam utpādayed bhṛśam ।।

anyathākaraṇe doṣān samīkṣya tu bahūn iha । saṃkalpavān na samāptiḥ [sāvīryākṛtikarmaṇī] ।।

dṛṣṭvādbhutaṃ tu kārtsnyena tataḥ śāntiṃ samārabhet । asamīkṣya tu kurvāṇo na śāntiṃ labhate naraḥ ।।

vātikasya yathā vaidyaḥ paittikasya ca niścaye । rogasya bhaiṣaje datte karmasiddhim avāpnuyāt ।।

tasmāt tāvat parīkṣeta yāvan niṣpannam adbhutam । asadasyasadasyānāṃ kartuḥ kārayitus tathā ।।

viguṇaṃ kriyamāṇaṃ tu karma kuryād upadravam । viśeṣato nihanyeta kartāraṃ saparicchadam ।।

hetuśrutaṃ ca dṛṣṭaṃ ca tasmāt sāguṇyam ācaret । saguṇe ca kṛte tasmin sarvasaṃpad bhaved dhruvam ।।

aśokapuṣpair home tu madhukṣīrasamanvitaiḥ । prāpnoti sukṛtair vipro gandharvapadam uttamam ।।

brahmādistambaparyantaṃ yaṃ yaṃ kāmaṃ samīhate । tat tat prāpnoty ayatnena satyam etad dvijottamāḥ ।।

oṃ praṇamya viṣṭarāsīnāṃ brahmāṇaṃ kavisattamam । praṇamya śirasā devaṃ gautamaḥ paryapṛcchata ।।

adbhutāni suraśreṣṭha prajānām ahitāya vai । śamanaṃ ca tathā teṣāṃ prabrūhi vinayena me ।।

tasya tad vacanaṃ śrutvā brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ । abravīt paramaḥ prītaḥ sarvotpātapratikriyām ।।

śṛṇu vatsa yathānyāyaṃ dvādaśādhyāyasaṃgraham । pracyamānam aśeṣaṃ taṃ vātavaikṛtanoditam ।।

yasmāc ca vāyur valavāñ śreṣṭhaḥ sarvādbhutodbhavaḥ । tasmāt tam eva prathamaṃ pravakṣyāmi yathāvidhi ।।

yānti yānāny ayuktāni vinā nṛbhis tathā । yuktāni vā na gacchanti narendrāṇāṃ mahad bhayam ।।

bheryo mṛdaṅgāḥ paṭahā vādyante vāpy anāhatāḥ । āhatāś ca na vādyante acalāni calanti vā ।।

araṇye tūryanirghoṣo yadi śrūyeta nābhasaḥ । śarīraṃ vyathate tatra yadi vā veśmani śrutaḥ ।।

śrūyante ca mahāśabdā gītagāndharvanisvanāḥ । śarīraṃ bādhyate tatra vyādhir vā sumahān bhavet ।।

koṣṭhe vā patate yatra hastād darvī kadā cana । patate musalaṃ cāpi śūrpaṃ vā dhūyate yadi ।।

golāṅgalānāṃ saṃsargo vikāraś candrasūryayoḥ । nārīṃ vā dhayate nārī jāyate tumulaṃ bhayam ।।

pratyāharanti sarpanti stambhaprāsādapādapāḥ । śayanāsanayānāni niyataṃ nṛpater vadhaḥ ।।

vāti cākālilo vāyur ghoraḥ śarkarakarṣaṇaḥ । pātayan vṛkṣaveśmāni kalpānta iva bhīṣaṇaḥ ।।

saptāham atha vā pakṣaṃ nibadhnāty atidāruṇam । tryahād yadi na varṣeta ghoraṃ śastrabhayaṃ bhavet ।।

vāyavyeṣv eva nṛpatir vāyuṃ saptabhir arcayet । dvāv imāv iti tisro hi japtavyāḥ prayatair dvijaiḥ ।।

bahvannadakṣiṇo homaḥ kartavyo atiprayatnataḥ । vāyavyām eva śāntau ca vāyoḥ savitur āvapet ।।

ādāv ante ca madhye ca tathaivam anuyojayet । gurave dakṣiṇāṃ dadyād vāyavīśāntisiddhaye ।।

yamakaṃ jāyate puṣpaṃ phalaṃ vā yamakaṃ yadi । kumudotpalapadmāni ekanāle bahūny api ।।

bahuśīrṣā dviśīrṣā vā tathānyaprasavā api । yavā vā vrīhayo vāpi svāmino maraṇāya te ।।

ekavṛkṣe ca saṃpaśyen nānātvaṃ phalapuṣpayoḥ । vyatyāsam anyathātvaṃ vā paracakrāgamo bhavet ।।

[the manuscripts contain no khaṇḍikā five] anṛtu phalapuṣpaṃ vā na yathartu phalanti vā । oṣadhīvīrudho vāpi janamārabhayaṃ bhavet ।।

atha dhānyaviparyāse abhadraṃ cāpi śaṃsati । tilā vā samatailāḥ syuḥ surātailā bhavanti vā ।।

agrāmyaṃ kārayet puṣpaṃ phalaṃ vā vikṛtaṃ nṛpaḥ । dhānyānāṃ vaikṛte kṣetraṃ saha sasyena dāpayet ।।

sauryaṃ caruṃ puṣpaphale vikṛte paśum eva ca । kṣaitrapatyaṃ ca bhaumaṃ ca nirvapet sasyavaikṛte ।।

sauryī śāntiḥ prayoktavyā sauryair mantrair yathāvidhi । uccā patantam ity ṛgbhyāṃ garbhaṃ tu parikīrtitam ।।

bhaumena cānuvākena garbhayet sasyavaikṛte । sadakṣiṇair dvijair bhuktaiḥ kartāraṃ cārcayet tataḥ ।।

pureṣu yeṣu dṛśyante pādapā devacoditāḥ । rudanto vā hasanto vā sravanto vā bahūn rasān ।।

arogā vā nivāte ca śākhā muñcanty asaṃbhrame । phalaṃ puṣpaṃ tathā bālā darśayantīti hāsanam ।।

sarvāvasthāṃ darśayantaḥ phalapuṣpam anārtavam । [kṣipraṃ tatra bhayaṃ ghoraṃ ghoraṃ pravaryteta caturvidham ।।

sarpān matsyān pakṣiṇo vā yatra devaḥ pravarṣati । tatra sasyopaghātaḥ syād bhayaṃ vātipravartate ।।

surāsavaṃ tathā kṣaudraṃ sarpis tailaṃ tathā dadhi । yatra varṣati parjanyaḥ kṣudragas tatra jāyate ।।

ulkātārāś ca dhiṣṇyeṣu yadāṅgārāṃś ca varṣati । tadā vyādhibhayaṃ ghoraṃ teṣu deśeṣu nirdiśet ।।

nārācāḥ śaktayaḥ khaḍgāḥ pradīpyante yadā muhuḥ । tadā śastrabhayaṃ ghoraṃ teṣu deśeṣu nirdiśet ।।

pumān aśvo gajo vāpi yadā yatra pradīpyate । naśyanti sevakās tatra pradhānaś ca vinaṅkṣyati ।।

yatra sravec caityavṛkṣaḥ sahasā vividhān rasān । pṛthakpṛthak samastān vā tat pravakṣyāmi lakṣaṇam ।।

ghṛte madhuni dugdhe ca ghṛte dugdhe tathāmbhasi । kṣaudre madhuni pānīye ghṛte caivāparaṃ payaḥ ।।

yatraitac ca mahotpātaṃ vṛkṣeṣu syāt sudāruṇam । surāsave mithobhedaḥ śoṇite śastrapātanam ।।

taile pradhānā vadhyante bhakte kṣudbhayam ādiśet । anṛtau cet phalaṃ yatra puṣpaṃ vā dṛśyate drume ।।

dhruvaṃ syād daśame māsi rājñas tatra viparyayaḥ । puṣpe puṣpaṃ bhaved yatra phale caiva tathā phalam ।।

parṇe parṇaṃ vijānīyāt tatra nānāvidhaṃ bhayam । śuklena vāsasā yatra caityavṛkṣaḥ samāvṛtaḥ ।।

brāhmaṇānāṃ bhayaṃ ghoraṃ tadā tīvraṃ vinirdiśet । raktavastrāvṛtaiś cānyaiḥ kṣatraiyāṇāṃ mahābhayam ।।

pītavastraiś tu vaiśyānāṃ śūdrāṇāṃ kṛṣṇavāsasaiḥ । nīlaiḥ sasyopaghātāya miśrais tu mṛgapakṣiṇām ।।

vivarṇair vāyavas tīvrāḥ paraṃ syur daśamāsataḥ । daivatāni pralapanti yasya rāṣṭre hasanti vā ।।

udīkṣante puro vāpi tatra vidyān mahad bhayam । vihasanti nimīlanti liṅgāni vikṛtāni ca ।।

māsāntareṇa jānīyāt tatra tatra mahad bhayam । yatra citram udīkṣeta gāyate ceṣṭate muhuḥ ।।

eteṣv aṣṭasu māseṣu rājño maraṇam ādiśet । citrāṇi yatra liṅgāni tathaivāyatanāni ca ।।

vikāraṃ kuryur atyarthaṃ tatra vidyān mahābhayam । utpāṭanaṃ tadāgānāṃ saraso vā fires tathā ।।

samuddeśe pradīpyante vidyāt tatra bhayaṃ mahat । yatra vṛkṣā akālīnaṃ darśanaṃ phalapuṣpayoḥ] ।।

kṣīraṃ snehaṃ surāṃ raktaṃ madhu toyaṃ sravanti vā । śūṣyanty arogāḥ sahasā śuṣkā ruhanti vā punaḥ ।।

uttiṣṭhanti niṣīdanti tat pravakṣyāny ataḥ param ।।

hasane dehanāśaḥ syād yodhā naśyanti śakhayā । saṃbhramo deśanāśāya phalī śilpikṣayāya ca ।।

bālānāṃ maraṇaṃ kuryād bālānāṃ phalapuṣpatā । svarāṣṭrabhedaṃ kurute phalapuṣpam anārtavam ।।

kṣayaḥ kṣīrasrave jñeyaḥ snehe durbhikṣalakṣaṇam । vāhanāpacayaṃ madye rakte saṃgrāmam ādiśet ।।

madhusrāve bhaved vyādhir jalasrāve na varṣati । arogā yadi śuṣyante vidyād durbhikṣalakṣaṇam ।।

bhedaḥ svapatitotthāne rudatsv annakṣayo bhavet । jalpane dhananāśaḥ syād gulmavallīlatāsu ca ।।

pūjitānāṃ jalasrutau rājño mṛtyuṃ samādiśet । ācchādayitvā taṃ vṛkṣāṃ gandhamālyair vibhūṣayet ।।

bhojanaṃ cātra viprāṇāṃ madhusarpiḥsamanvitam । chattradhvajaṃ ca dātavyaṃ parṇahomas tathā param ।।

mantrair auṣadhasaṃyuktair bhvoradāban ataḥ param । baliṃ caivopahārāṃś ca gītanṛtyaṃ samantataḥ ।।

gandhamālyaṃ ca dhūpaṃ ca dīpaṃ dadyāt tathaiva ca । bhakṣabhojyānnapānaṃ ca rudrasyopaharen niśi ।।

pākaś ca daśame māsi śukrasya vacanaṃ yathā । bṛhaspatis tathāditye bruvete yat tathaiva tat ।।

raudrī caivātra kartavyā vṛkṣādbhutavināśinī । durave dakṣiṇāṃ dadyān niṣkaṃ bhūmiṃ ca tatra vai ।।

akālaprasuvo nāryaḥ kālātītāḥ prajās tathā । saṃbaddhayugmaprasavā dviyugmaprasavā api ।।

amānuṣāṇi ruṇḍāni saṃjāyante yadā striyām । atyaṅgāni anaṅgāni hīnāṅgāny atha vā punaḥ ।।

catuṣpatpakṣisadṛśāny ardhamānuṣavanti ca । vināśas tatsya deśasya kulasya ca vinirdiśet ।।

aprāptavayaso garbho dvicatuṣpatstriyo api vā । vidhvastaṃ vikṛtaṃ cāpi prajāyeta bhayāya tat ।।

tāny āśu parabhūmiṣu tyaktavyāni śubhārthibhiḥ । śāntiś cātra prakartavyā brāhmaṇair brahmavādibhiḥ ।।

vaḍavā hastinī gaur vā yadi yugmaṃ prasūyate । vijātaṃ vikṛtaṃ vāpi ṣaṇmāsair mriyate nṛpaḥ ।।

apatyāni ca yūthebhyas tyājyāni parabhūmiṣu । svāmino nagaraṃ yūtham anyathā tu vināśayet ।।

viyoniṣu yadā yānti ṃśrībhāvaḥ prajāsv api । kharoṣṭrahayamātaṅgāḥ pakṣiṇo vā na sādhu tat ।।

akāle vāpi mādyante kāle vāpu amadā yadi । śivoṣṭrahayamātaṅgāḥ pakṣiṇo vā na sādhu tat ।।

athānaḍvān anaḍvāhaṃ dhenur dhenuṃ pibed yadi । śunī vā dhayate dhenuṃ śunīṃ dhenur athāpi vā ।।

[tiryagyonau mānuṣī vā paracakrāgamo bhavet । amānuṣā mānuṣāṇi jalapante prāṇino yadi ।।

viceṣṭāṃ vā virāvaṃ vā māsena mriyate nṛpaḥ] । catuṣpatpakṣibhujagān mānuṣī janayed yadi ।।

tiryagyonau mānuṣaṃ vā paracakrāgamo bhavet । jaṅgame sthāvaraṃ jātaṃ sthāvare vātha jaṅgamam ।।

tasmin yoniviparyāse paracakrāgamo bhavet । tyāgo vivāso dānaṃ vā dattvāpy āśu śubhaṃ bhavet ।।

sthālīpākena yaṣṭavyaṃ paśunā vā purohitaḥ । prājāpatyena mantreṇa yajed bahvannadakṣiṇām ।।

yāmyākarmaprayogas tu prathamaṃ tatra dṛśyate । prājāpatyāṃ tataḥ śāntiṃ prājārthī kārayen nṛpaḥ ।।

ādāv ante ca madhye ca śāntāv uktas tu tadgaṇaḥ । ārogyaṃ ca śivaṃ caiva deśe tasmin nṛpe bhavet ।।

yatrādbhutāni dṛśyante vicitrāṇi samantataḥ । susamṛddho api deśaḥ sa kṣipram eva vinaśyati ।।

rājaveśmasu vaikṛtye prāsādadhvajatoraṇe । autpātikāni dṛśyante rājñas tatra mahad bhayam ।।

prāsādatoraṇāṭṭāladvāraprāsādaveśmanām । akasmāt patanaṃ teṣāṃ rājamṛtyukaraṃ smṛtam ।।

devarājadhvajānāṃ ca patanaṃ bhaṅga eva vā । niṣevaṇaṃ vā kravyādaiḥprabhraṣṭair vītaraśmikaiḥ ।।

prabhraṣṭagrahanakṣatrair diśaḥ sarvāḥ samākulāḥ । saṃdhyā cobhayathā dīptā tatra vidyān mahad bhayam ।।

yadi vā dīryate akasmād bhūmiś chidrībhaved yadi । prakampate atimātraṃ vā sarveṣu ca bhayāya tat ।।

rakṣaḥpataṃgaiḥ panthāno na vahanti bhayānvitāḥ । rakṣorūpāṇi dṛśyante na ca rakṣā gṛheṣv api ।।

saṃpraviṣṭaiḥ piśācair vā rakṣobhir vāpi tannibhaiḥ । acirān nagaraṃ tatra janamāreṇa māryate ।।

ṛtavas tu viparyastā brāhmaṇāś ca vidharmiṇaḥ । nakṣatrāṇi viyogīni bhayam īdṛk pradarśanam ।।

apūjyā yatra pūjyante na pūjyante ca pūjitāḥ । pūjyeṣv adānaniṣṭhā ca bhayam īdṛk pradarśanam ।।

nādīyante na pūjyante brāhmaṇā balibhiḥ surāḥ । na caivātmīyadharmeṣu ratiṃ kurvanty adharmataḥ ।।

bhinnāḥ kauṭilyabahulā gajāḥ puruṣavājinaḥ । kalahe syur nirutsāhāḥ sasatyāḥ satyavarjitāḥ ।।

śīlācāravihīnāś ca madyamāṃsānṛtapriyāḥ । nagnapāṣaṇḍabhūyiṣṭhā vināśe paryupasthite ।।

mahābaliṃ mahāśāntiṃ bhojyāni sumahānti ca । prājāpatyaṃ mahendraṃ ca mahādevam athāpi vā ।।

aindrasthāne tu māhendrīṃ raudre raudrīṃ prayojayet । gavām aṣṭaśataṃ dadyād viprebhyo manujādhipaḥ ।।

gurave tu śataṃ niṣkaṃ prajāsv evaṃ śivaṃ bhavet । anāvṛṣṭyātivṛṣṭyā vā durbhikṣeṇa bhayaṃ bhavet ।।

akālavarṣo rogāya ativṛṣṭir bhayāya ca । anabhraṃ varṣate akasmād vaidyutaṃ garjitaṃ tathā ।।

anabhre vāpi nirghātaḥ patito rājamṛtyave । tīkṣṇaṃ ca varṣaty anṛtau ṛtuṣv eva na varṣati ।।

yadā coṣṇe bhavec chītaṃ śīte coṣṇaṃ tathaiva ca । dṛṣṭo bhāvas tu vikṛto na yathartu svarūpakaḥ ।।

anārogyaṃ bhavec caiva prajānām iti nirdiśet ।।

saptarātraṃ yadā varṣet prabaddhaṃ pākaśāsanaḥ । anṛtau tasya deśasya pradhānasya vadho dhruvam ।।

śoṇitaṃ varṣate yatra tatra śastrabhayaṃ bhavet । majjāsthisnehamāṃsaṃ vā janamārībhayaṃ bhavet ।।

aṅgārapāṃsuvṛṣṭes tu nagaraṃ tad vinaśyati । phalaṃ puṣpaṃ śamīdhānyaṃ hiraṇyaṃ vā bhayāya tat ।।

jantavo dīnavikṛtāḥ palālo api vināśanaḥ । chidrāvartāḥ plavaṅgaś ca sasyānām ativardhanam ।।

anabhre vā divā rātrau śvetam indrāyudhaṃ bhavet । pūrvapaścāduttare vā dakṣiṇe vāpi dṛśyate ।।

susamṛddham api sthānaṃ durbhikṣeṇa vinaśyati ।।

yady anabhre api vimale sūryachāyā na dṛśyate । na nirabhre pratīpā vā tatra deśabhayaṃ bhavet ।।

sūryendravāyuparjanyā yaṣṭavyā varṣavaikṛte । annāni sahiraṇyāni dhānyaṃ gāvaś ca dakṣiṇāḥ ।।

vaiśvadevī ca kartavyā sarvādbhutavināśinī । gurave ca hayaḥ śvetaḥ sarvalakṣaṇalakṣitaḥ ।।

śataṃ niṣkaṃ suvarṇasya dātavyaṃ vā gavāṃ śatam ।।

athāto agnivaikṛtam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmo yathovāca bhagavāñśukraḥ ।।

anindhano agnir dīpyeta yatra tūrṇam aghasvanaḥ । na dīpyate sendhano vā sarāṣṭraṃ pīḍayen nṛpam ।।

prajvaled dadhi māṃsaṃ vā tathā dūrvāpi kiṃ cana । agniṃ vinā yadāśuṣkaṃ niyataṃ nṛpater vadhaḥ ।।

prāsādaṃ toraṇaṃ dvāraṃ prākāraṃ kāśyapaṃ gṛham । śayanāsanayānaṃ ca dhvajaṃ chattraṃ sacāmaram ।।

anagninā yadi dahed vidyutā vāpi nirdahet । saptāhābhyantare tatra niyataṃ nṛpater vadhaḥ ।।

aniśāyāṃ tamāṃsi syur yadi vā pāṃsavo rajaḥ । dhūmāś cānagnijā yatra tatra vidyān mahad bhayam ।।

rātrau divā cānabhre vā yadi jvālā pradṛśyate । garhitaṃ jyotiṣāṃ caiva darśanaṃ vā bhaven niśi ।।

purāṇāṃ caiva patanaṃ jvalatāṃ ca muhurmuhur । dṛśyate anyac ca sahasā tatrāpy agnibhayaṃ vadet ।।

prāsādādiṣu caityeṣu yadi dhūmo vināgninā । bhavaty agnir adhūmo vā tathaivātibhayāvahaḥ ।।

jvalanti yadi śastrāṇi vinamanty unnamanti vā । kośebhyo vāpi niryānti saṃgrāmas tumulo bhavet ।।

pradīpyante ca sahasā catuṣpatpakṣimānuṣāḥ । vṛkṣā vā parvatā vāpi tatra vidyān mahad bhayam ।।

śayanāsanayāneṣu keśaprāvaraṇeṣu ca । dṛśyate atīva sahasā tatrāpy agnibhayaṃ bhavet ।।

garjanty āyudhaśastrāṇi vinamanty unnamanti vā । dhanunā saha vā bāṇāḥ saṃgrāmas tumulo bhavet ।।

samidbhiḥ kṣīraṛkṣāṇāṃ sarṣapais tu ghṛtena ca । hotavyo agniḥ svakair mantraiḥ mantraiḥ suvarṇaṃ cātra dakṣiṇā ।।

pāyasaṃ sarpiṣā miśraṃ dvijātīn bhojayet tataḥ । tebhya eva yathāśaktyā dakṣiṇāṃ dāpayen nṛpaḥ ।।

agnir bhūmyām iti tribhir āgneyaṃ tatra kārayet । gurave dakṣiṇāṃ dadyān niṣkam aśvaṃ ca sundaram ।।

gārgyeṇoktaṃ pravakṣyāmi kṛtsnam utpātalakṣaṇam । bhūmikampo bhaved yatra devatāpratimā haset ।।

devatā bhramate yatra mṛtyus tatra vinirdiśet । garjanaṃ vāpi kūpānām upasargas tu jāyate ।।

pratisrotavahā nadyo bhavanti ca kathaṃ cana । ṣaḍbhir māsair vijānīyāt paracakrābhimarśanam ।।

akālajaṃ phalaṃ puṣpaṃ śītoṣṇatvam akālajam । anyaṃ svāminam icchanti nadyaś cākālasaṃbhavāḥ ।।

acalaṃ ca calaṃ yatra calaṃ vā acalaṃ bhavet । rājā vinaśyate tara deśo vāpi vinaśyati ।।

divā tārā yatra paśyec chvetaḥ pakṣy atha vā bhavet । rātrau cendrāyudhaṃ paśyed deśabhaṅgaṃ vinirdiśet ।।

śaśakaṃ jambukaṃ vāpi sūkaraṃ hariṇaṃ tathā । sthānamadhye yadā paśyec chūnyaṃ bhavati niścayam ।।

araṇyamṛgajātīyāḥ svayaṃ yānti nṛpālayam । tat sthānaṃ tu bhavec chūnyaṃ bhagnaprākāratoraṇam ।।

prākāraveśmabhiṭṭīṣu toraṇe gokule api vā । madhūni yatra dṛśyante tatra vai kasya kiṃ phalam ।। kālanaṣṭapathaṃ sīmāṃ tṛṇavallīsamākulām । sa deśo mānuṣair mukto mṛgāṇāṃ gocaro bhavet ।।

pratyādityaṃ yadā paśyet pure devakule api vā । api śakrasamo rājā abdamadhye vinaśyati ।।

vāpīkūpataḍāgeṣu nadyāṃ vā tarate śilā । rājabhaṅgaṃ bhavec caiva cauravyādhibhayaṃ tathā ।।

rājagāmiṣu puṣpeṣu vastreṣv ābharaṇeṣu ca । anagninā yadi dahet parighaṃ tatra vai dhruvam ।।

tat pātaparityakta kadā cid api budhasyādayaṃ bhavati । dahanaṃ pavanajalamaraṇarogarakṣakṣayāya buddhivāk karoti budhaḥ ।।

tatra kuryān mahāśāntim amṛtāṃ viśvabheṣajīm ।।

om āsīnaṃ tu himavati bṛhaspatiṃ sukhāvaham । gautamaḥ paripṛcchati vinayāt saṃśitavrataḥ ।।

katham agniḥ parīkṣyo ayaṃ mantrakarmaṇi śobhanaḥ । svarūpaṃ jñāpaya tvaṃ hi śubhāśubhanibodhane ।।

bṛhaspatiḥ pratyāha taṃ gautam ।। śvetaḥ sugandhiḥ padmābho nirbhūmo dundubhisvanaḥ । asakto amuṭitaśikhaḥ snigdhotthāyī pradakṣiṇaḥ ।।

hūyamānaḥ pradīptaḥ syād dīptatejāḥ sukhapradaḥ । śāntikarmaṇi yatrāgnir niyataṃ siddhilakṣaṇam ।।

svastikā vardhamānā ca śrīvatsā ca pradakṣiṇā । jvālārūpeṇa dṛśyeta sā vai śrīḥ sarvatomukhī ।।

yadā hotra prasannena hūyamāno yathā śikhī । ghoṣam utpādayan snigdhaṃ kalyāṇaṃ tad vinirdiśet ।।

dīptaś ca ratnasaṃkāśaḥ kṣemo dundubhivad ghanaḥ । dhūmaḥ praśasto bhavati svārthasiddhikaro nṛṇam ।।

snigdhaghoṣo alpadhūmaś ca gauravarṇo mahān bhavet । piṇḍitārcir vapuṣmān vā pāvakaḥ siddhikārakaḥ ।।

yadā tv agniḥ sarvadikthā jvālāgraiḥ spṛśate haviḥ । tadāsya nṛpatiḥ śīghraṃ pararāṣṭraṃ ca mardati ।।

tiṣṭhantaṃ sthāvaraṃ snigdhaṃ śrūyate yatra gītakam । vācaḥ prasannā homeṣu maṅgalyāś caiva siddhaye ।।

kokilasya māyurasya bhāsasya kuralasya ca । homeṣu śravaṇaṃ caiva prādakṣiṇyaṃ ca śasyate ।।

śatapattrā rudantī ca cāṣasya nandanaṃ tathā । rambhaṇaṃ caiva dhenūnāṃ havaneṣu praśasyate ।।

padmavaiḍūryanikāśā vāditrāṇāṃ ca nisvanāḥ । gāvaḥ savarṇavatsā ca dṛṣṭā home praśasyate ।।

vikāsipadmasadṛśaḥ prasannārcir hutāśanaḥ । susamānābhir arcābhiḥ snigdhābhir anupūrvaśaḥ ।।

gambhīraṃ nardate yatra tad agryaṃ siddhilakṣaṇam । akṣatān phalapuṣpāṇi vardhamānam apāṃ ghaṭam ।।

dṛṣṭvā vā yadi vā śrutvā karmasiddhiṃ samādiśet । pīṭhachattradhvajanibhā jvālā vāraṇasaṃnibhāḥ ।।

praśastā ujjvalāś caiva vajrakuṇḍalasaṃnibhāḥ । pradakṣiṇagatiḥ śrīmān agniḥ kartur manoharaḥ । yasya syād vijayaṃ kuryāt kṣipraṃ narapater dhruvam ।।

bhūmyāṃ meghābhivṛṣṭānāṃ madhupāyasasarpiṣām । kṛṣṇavartmā sugandhiḥ syāj jayaṃ kṣitipater vadet ।।

śaṅkhasvastikarūpāṇi cakrarūpaṃ tathā gadā । śiromālā ca dṛśyeta tad vai vijayalakṣaṇam ।।

ghṛtavarṇanibhas tv agniḥ snigdhaghoṣo mahāsvanaḥ । citrabhānuḥ prasanno vā niyataṃ siddhilakṣaṇam ।।

mṛgapakṣiṇa āraṇyāḥ praviśanti yadā puram । grāmyā vā tyaktvā nagaram araṇyaṃ yānti nirbhayāḥ ।।

divā rātricarā vāpi rātrau vāpi divācarāḥ । divā vā puramadhyasthā ghoraṃ vāśyanti nirbhayāḥ ।।

rājadvāre puradvāre śivā vāpy aśubhaṃ vadet । [tyaktvāraṇyaṃ ca tiṣṭhanti nagaraṃ mṛgapakṣiṇaḥ] ।।

āṣāḍhe śrāvaṇe vāpi śūnyaṃ bhavati tatpuram । [tyaktvā siṃhāḥ sahariṇā mūṣikaṃ sūkaraṃ rurum ।।

dṛṣṭvā praviṣṭān nagare śūnyaṃ bhavati tatpuram] । abhivācaṃ vadante ca paśavyā mṛgapakṣiṇaḥ ।।

śyenā gṛdhrā bakāḥ kākāḥ sarve maṇḍalacāriṇaḥ । vāśante bhairavaṃ yatra tad apy āśu vinaśyati ।।

niśāyāṃ bahavaḥ śvāno roruvanti yadā tu te । hanyamānā na gacchanti tatra vāso na rocate ।।

prāsādadhvajaśālāsu prākāradvāratoraṇaiḥ । gardabhaṛśyabhāsānāṃ piṇḍān dṛṣṭvā puraṃ tyajet ।।

pūrvamukhaś ca saṃdhyāyām apraśāntasvaro mṛgaḥ । grāmīṇaghātaṃ śaṃset sa grāmaṇyapraticārataḥ ।।

grāmadvāre ca vāśyeta vanād āgatya jambukaḥ । tīkṣṇasvareṇa mahatā diṣṭo grāmavadho hi saḥ ।।

yad yāti veśma kapotaḥ praviśeta viśeṣataḥ । rājaveśmany ulūko vā tat tyājyam acirād gṛham ।।

akasmād veśmaprākāre prāsāde toraṇe dhvaje । patanti bahavo gṛdhrāḥ kākolūkā bakaiḥ saha ।।

athāpy eteṣu sthāneṣu madhu saṃjāyate yadā । nalinī caiva valmīkaḥ ṣaṇmāsair mriyate nṛpaḥ ।।

mṛgaḥ paśur vā pakṣī vā sūkaro vāpi vāśyate । yadi cotthāya śṛṇute sa manuṣyo vinaśyati ।।

kākamūṣikamārjārāñ śvapataṃgān bhayāvahān । atīva bahuśo dṛṣṭvā durbhikṣeṇa kṣayaṃ vadet ।।

śvānaḥ śivābhir vāśyanto bhramantaḥ puramadhyataḥ । asthīni vā mṛtādīnāṃ janamārabhayaṃkarāḥ ।।

kāṣṭhaṃ vā yadi vā śṛṅgaṃ gṛhītvā śunakaḥ svayam । grāmamadhyena dhāvan syāt tathaivāhur mahad bhayam ।।

purohitas tu kurvīta kāpotīṃ śāntim uttamām । devāḥ kapota iti ca sūktaṃ tatra samādiśet ।।

āvāpe vyatiṣaṅge ca upariṣṭāc ca hūyate । kāmikāṃ dakṣiṇāṃ dadyād gurur vā yena tuṣyati ।।

devatārcāḥ pranṛtyanti dīpyanti prajvalanti vā । udvijanti rudante vā prasvidyante hasanti vā ।।

uttiṣṭhanti niṣīdanti pradhāvanti pibanti vā । ejanti vikṣipante vā gātrapraharaṇadhvajān ।।

avāṅmukhā vadante vā sthānāt sthānaṃ vrajanti vā । vapante vāgnim udakaṃ snehaṃ raktaṃ payo vasām ।।

jalpanti vā niśvasanti viceṣṭante rudanti vā । citraṃ saṃvīkṣyate yatra gātrair vāpi viceṣṭitaiḥ ।।

yatraite saṃpradṛśyante vikārāḥ sahasotthitāḥ । liṅgāyatanacaityeṣu tatra vāso na rocate ।।

rājño vā vyasanaṃ tatra sa vā deṣaḥ pralīyate । kṣucśastramaraṇair vāpi kiṃ cit tatrābhiśasyate ।।

devatāyatanair vāpi prayātāḥ sumahotsavaiḥ । japahomaś ca kalpantā sīdatāṃ ca same pathi ।।

same pātam akasmāc ca udāsīnāṃ tathaiva ca । dṛśyate tad vināśāya rājño janapadasya vā ।।

yatra prasthāni bhūtāni liṅgasyāyatanāni ca । tatra śāmyanti ghorāṇi japahomaś ca kalpate ।।

prasādaḥ puṇḍarīkaṃ vā viśīryeta pateta vā । vātavajrahato vāpi puramukhye bhayaṃ bhavet ।।

pitāmahasya dharmeṣu yan nimittaṃ dvijeṣu tat । aśvakrāntāgniyāneṣu yāni tāni purohite ।।

paśūnāṃ rudrajaṃ jñeyaṃ nṛpāṇāṃ lokapālajam । jñeyaṃ māṇḍalikānāṃ ca yat tat skandaviśākhayoḥ ।।

laukikaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ jñeyaṃ vaiśvadevaṃ ca sarvadā । senāpatau gaṇeśānāṃ gāndharvaṃ saciveṣu ca ।।

devapreṣyaṃ nṛpapreṣye devastrīṇāṃ nṛpastriyām । kāśyapaṃ yantraprāsāde vāstoṣpatyaṃ pure sthitam ।।

kumārīṣu kumārījaṃ kumāreṣu kumārajam । yakṣarākṣasanāgaiś ca yathoktaiḥ pānakarma ca ।।

athātaḥ sarvasarvasamucchayaḥ ekam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmo yathovāca bhagavān bṛhaspatiḥ ।।

yad dvādaśabhir adhyāyair vyākhyānaṃ parikīrtitam । tat samāsena bhūyo api śṛṇu paryāyam āgatam ।।

parājito rāhunipīḍitamaṇḍalo vivarṇaḥ saṃdhyāvikṛto niḥprabho yadā । astamanaṃ yāti divākaraḥ tadāśu vidyāt subrahmajanakṣayam ।।

gṛhīto rāhuṇā sārdham uttiṣṭhati divākaraḥ । tadā dharmaphalaṃ kṣīṇaṃ kalim āviśate prajā ।।

amukto rāhuṇā sārdham uttiṣṭhati yadā śaśī । tadā dharmaphalaṃ kṣīṇaṃ kalim āviśate prajā ।।

amukto rāhuṇā sārdham astaṃ gacchati candramāḥ । tadā tato bhayaṃ vidyān mṛtyum āviśate prajā ।।

avādyamānāḥ paṭahāḥ pravadanti muhurmuhuḥ । śastrāṇi vāhanāni ca jvalanty aśubhadāruṇam ।।

vātaprakopo rajasānuviddhā diśaś ca saṃdhyā ca ghanānuyātā । drakṣanti saṃdhyā yadi pañcavarṇā bhayāni rājñaḥ prativedayanti ।।

anabhre stanate yatra nabhogulma gulmāyate । kṣipraṃ vidravate rāṣṭraṃ daśavarṣāṇi pañca ca ।।

anabhre patate vidyud darśayed vāghanotthitām । anabhre vāpi nirghātaḥ patito rājamṛtyave ।।

yady ahni vāteṣu mahendrarekhā mahendracāpaḥ samudeti rātrau । tadā bhayaṃ pārthivamaṇḍalānāṃ vadanti śāstrārthavido dvijendrāḥ ।।

nikalkayukto niśi sendracāpo vivardhamānaḥ samudeti rātrau । viśīryamāṇā patate tatholkā tadā bhayaṃ pārthivamaṇḍalānām ।।

muñcanti nāgā rudhiraṃ karaiś ca lomāni dīpyanti turaṃgamāṇām । dīpyanti khaḍgāni ca khecarāṇi cihnāni rājñaḥ prativedayanti ।।

girivarapatanaṃ svabhūmicālaḥ pratibhayatā ca tathaiva mānuṣāṇām । vikṛtajananam uktim ugravācā mahati bhaye mṛgapakṣiṇo vadanti ।।

chattre gṛhe vāsarathe dhvaje ca dhūmaḥ samuttiṣṭhati yasya cāgniḥ । sa pārthivaḥ kṣīnamanuṣyakośaḥ prāpnoti nāśaṃ ca janakṣayaṃ ca ।।

mahormibhiḥ svair vitatair jaloghair nadyaḥ svakūlāc ca haranti vṛkṣān । yadi pratisrotavahās tadā syur vināśanā deśaparā nṛpasya ।।

yadā tu ghāte ca divākaraprabhāḥ svareṇubhir vāpi vidhūmasaṃbhramāḥ । na tasya vāsaṃ viṣaye vadanti āhur gaṇānāṃ ca vivṛddhināśaḥ ।।

hutāśanasy jvalanaṃ niredhaṃ tathā na caiva jvalate ca sedhmā । bhayāni rājñaḥ prativedayanti ।।

śiloccayānāṃ ca śilānipātaḥ puradrumāṇāṃ ca viṣāṇapātaḥ । caityadrumāṇāṃ ca tathaiva pāto bhayāni rājñaḥ prativedayanti ।।

acālyavatsāḥ puragopureṣu bhramanti gāvaḥ kṛtaraudraśabdāḥ । mṛṇālabāddhāś ca gajā bhavanti bhayāni rājñaḥ prativedayanti ।।

prāsādagopuramukhāś ca patanti yatra indradhvajotthitavanaspativājināṃ ca । teṣāṃ vadanti pacanāni sukhāvahāni saumyādi saṃprabhayatā ca tathādiśanti ।।

ūrdhvaṃ vilokya nagaraṃ pratisaṃniviṣṭāḥ sūryodaye khalu rudanti śivātiraudram । gṛdhrāś ca maṇḍalasamutpatitā bhramanti prāptaṃ bhayaṃ janapadasya samādiśanti ।।

daṇḍāśaniḥ patati yatra savisphuliṅgā bhūḥ kampate dinakarasya bhavet praśāntiḥ । candhre ca yatra vikṛtaṃ ca bhaved aśāntaṃ māsāt samudbhavati tatra bhayo atighoraḥ ।।

caityadrumāṇāṃ rudhiraprakopāḥ kabandhayānāni bhavanti yatra । saṃdhyāsu rakṣo adhipater janānāṃ prabhūti rājño atibhaye bhavanti ।।

vṛṣṭir yadā varṣati reṇuvarṣais tatopariṣṭād dharitālavarṣam । tataḥ paraṃ varṣati śailavarṣaṃ tadā balaṃ naśyati pārthivasya ।।

āraṇyo grāmavāsī mṛgaśakunigaṇo grāmavāsī vanānte gṛdhrāṇāṃ saṃnipāto narapatibhavane gopure vā pure vā । yatra syān mānuṣīṇāṃ kharakarabhamukhānekarūpā prasūtis tatsthāne jīvitārthī sthitim ati kurute naiva pātaiḥ praduṣṭe ।।

prayānti devāḥ sahasāyatasthā vanāni vā yatra patanti bhūmau । sthānāni mucyanti nadanti ke cit tathā paraṃ śoṇitajagdhagātrāḥ ।।

utpātasaṃghair atyugraiḥ kṣātrahāniḥ prajāyate । lokānāṃ pīḍanaṃ caiva rogacaurāgnisaṃbhavam ।।

agnīnāṃ saṃpradoṣāḥ pratibhayajananā dīpyamānā diśaś ca madhyāhne cāntarikṣe grahagaṇakhacitā gṛdhrasaṃghaiḥ prakīrṇāḥ । nirghātaiḥ pāṃsuvarṣaiḥ satatamalinatā bhūpracālaś ca ghoro devānāṃ cāśrupāto nṛpatibhayakarā rāṣṭranāśāya caite ।।

śivādaye yatra divākarasya jvālāvimucy ūrdhvamukhī praroditi । samāvṛtā vāyasagṛdhrasaṃghais tadā bhayaṃ vedavido vadanti ।।

rudanti nāgās tu vimuktahastā vimuktadantās turagā rudanti । rudanti nāryaś ca samāgame ca tadā bhayaṃ syāc chrutiliṅgamūlam ।।

yadā tu vastrāṇi varadrumāṇāṃ prakāśavṛṣṭyā nipatanti mūrdhni । samīkṣya pātaṃ ca yathārthadṛṣṭaṃ bhayāya rāṣṭrasya nṛpasya vidyāt ।।

śakaṭādyāni yānāni yadāyuktāni saṃcalet । tadā janapade vidyān mahābhayam upasthitam ।।

yathaiva nityaṃ dṛśyante tathaiva samudāharet । na tasyātikramaḥ kaś cid akṛte śāntikarmaṇi ।।

kṣayo janapadastrīṇāṃ vidyād gajapurohite । japaṃ homaṃ ca śāntiṃ ca utpāteṣu prayojayet ।।

viśeṣeṇāmṛtāṃ kuryād bṛhaspativaco yathā । homaṃ lakṣamitaṃ kuryāj japed vā vedasaṃhitām । dānāni tu hiraṇyāni śāntikarmaṇi yojayet ।।

papracchośanasaṃ kāvyaṃ nāradaḥ paryavasthitaḥ । divyāṃś caivāntarikṣāṃś ca utpātān pārthivāṃs tathā ।।

ṛtūnāṃ ca viparyāse tathaiva mṛgapakṣiṇām । amānuṣāṇāṃ vyāhāre sthāvarāṇāṃ vyatikrame ।।

yonivyatikare caiva māṃsaśonitavarṣaṇe । anagnijvalane caiva tathā yānānusarpaṇe ।।

śastraprajvalane caiva caityaśuṣkavirohaṇe । liṅgāyatanacitrāṇāṃ rodane garjane tathā ।।

udapānataḍāgābān jvalane garjane api vā । matsyasarpadvijātīnāṃ rasānāṃ ca pravarṣaṇe ।।

āyudhānāṃ prajvalane garjane ca viśeṣataḥ । puṣpe phale ca vṛkṣāṇām akāle ca virohaṇe ।।

prāsādādrivimānānāṃ prākārāṇāṃ ca kampane । gītavāditraśabdāś ca yatra syur animittataḥ ।।

ye cānye ke cid utpātā jāyante vikṛtātmakāḥ । teṣāṃ phalaṃ ca kālaṃ ca tattvenācakṣva bhārgava ।।

sa tasmai pṛcchate samyaṅ nāradāyāśanāḥ kaviḥ । trividhān apy athotpātān vyākhyātum upacakrame ।।

yadā śīte bhavaty uṣṇam uṣṇe śītam atīva ca । navamāsāt paraṃ vidyāt teṣu deśeṣu vai bhayam ।।

yatrānṛtau prabaddhena tryahād ūrdhvaṃ pravarṣati । tasmin deśe pradhānasya puruṣasya vadho bhavet ।।

kokilāś ca mayūrāś ca akāle madabhāginaḥ । saṃsargaṃ vāpi gaccheyur vidyāj jānapadaṃ bhayam ।।

ruravaś caiva raudrāś ca pṛṣatā hariṇās tathā । yeṣu deśeṣu dṛśyante tān araṇyāya nirdiśet ।।

pradhānāś caiva vadhyante pakṣe saptadaśe tathā । tasmiñ janapade caiva mahad utpadyate bhayam ।।

gāvo aśvāḥ kuñjarāḥ śvānaḥ kharoṣṭrā vānaroragāḥ । nakulāḥ pakṣiṇo vyālāḥ sūkarā mahiṣā mṛgāḥ ।।

sattvāny etāni jalpanti yeṣu deśeṣu mānuṣam । teṣu deśeṣu rājā tu ṣaṣṭhe māsi vinaśyati ।।

utpātā vikṛtātmāno dṛśyante yatra tatra vai । deśe bhavati śīghraṃ hi ṣaṇmāsād bhayam uttamam ।।

āsanaṃ śayanaṃ yānaṃ yadā yatra prasarpati । vipakṣāt tatra tatsvāmī bhayaṃ prāpnoti dāruṇam ।।

dhānyakoṣṭhāyudhāgārāḥ pāṣāṇāḥ kūpaparvatāḥ । etāni yatra sarpanti vikṛtāni vadanti ca ।।

bahu vā jāyate tīvraṃ tasmin deśe bhayaṃ mahat । trīn māsān parakāle tu śeṣe saumyātikaṃ phalam ।।

deśe vā yadi vā grāme yonivyatikaro bhavet । tatra saṃvatsarād ūrdhvaṃ mahad utpadyate bhayam ।।

gaur aśvaṃ vaḍavā vāpi yasmin deśe prasūyate । abhyantareṇa tadvarṣād rājño maraṇam ādiśet ।।

mānuṣī janayed yatra tṛṇādān vividhān paśūn । ṣaṇmāsotthaṃ bhayaṃ tīvraṃ tatra tūtpadyate mahat ।।

paracakrāgamaṃ caiva nirdiśed iha śāstravit । saṃgrāmāś cātra vipulā jāyante vikṛtātmakāḥ ।।

sarpaṃ vā pakṣiṇaṃ vāpi janayed yatra mānuṣī । pracalas tasya deśasya ṣaṇmāsāt tu paraṃ bhavet ।।

uṣṭraṃ vā yā prasūyeta vānaraṃ vāpi mānuṣī । anyad vā jaṅgamaṃ kiṃ cit sthāvaraṃ vāpi kiṃ cana ।।

rogeṇa śastrapātena durbhikṣeṇa ca pīḍitaḥ । sa deśo vyathate śīghraṃ rājā tatra vinaśyati ।।

amānuṣī mānuṣaṃ vā mānuṣī vāpy amānuṣam । prasūyate tu jānīyāt paracakrāgamaṃ dhruvam ।।

caturakṣaṃ dviśīrṣaṃ vā gātrair nyūnādhikais tathā । vyañjanaiś copasaṃpannaṃ mānuṣī yā prasūyate ।।

dvisaṃvatsaraparyantād rājā tatra vinaśyati । uṣṭro vṛṣo vāpy aśvo vā gajo vā yatra jāyate ।।
