pakṣān māsāc ca bhavati rājñas tatra bhayaṃ mahat । paracakrasamutthaṃ vā sa deśo bhayam ṛcchati ।।

yonivyatikaraṃ yatra kuryur evaṃvidhaṃ striyaḥ । gaur vā sūyet tathānyāni tatra rājyaṃ vinaśyati ।।

vasanti yeṣu deśeṣu teṣu vidyān mahad bhayam । tasmād etāni sattvāni rājā kṣipraṃ pravāsayet ।।

aśvā kiśoraṃ janayec chṛṅgiṇaṃ yatra tatra tu । ādiśen maraṇaṃ rājño varṣābhyantara eva hi ।।

māghe budhe ca mahiṣī śrāvaṇe vaḍavā divā । siṃhe gāvaḥ prasūyante svāmino mṛtyudāyakāḥ । iti śāstrasamuccayāt ।।

nārī kharavṛṣoṣṭrāśvāñ śunaḥ sūkaragardabhān । rākṣasān vā piśācān vā yadāpy evaṃ prasūyate ।।

vyāpadyante atra dhānyāni sasyāni ca dhanāni ca । caturvidhaṃ bhayaṃ ghoraṃ kṣipraṃ tatra pravartate ।।

vadhyante hi pradhānās tu sārdhamāsāṣṭame tathā । vyādhīṃś ca teṣu deśeṣu trīṇi varṣāṇi nirdiśet ।।

anagnir jvalate yatra deśe tūrṇam anindhanaḥ । yo rājā tasya deśasya sadeśaḥ sa vinaśyati ।।

māṃsavarṣeṇa maghavā yatra deśe pravarṣati । asthīni rudhiraṃ majjāṃ vasāṃ caiteṣu vai dhruvam ।।

paracakrāgamaḥ śīghraṃ vijñeyas tu mahad bhayam । āhavāś cātra jāyante vipulā vikṛtātmakāḥ ।।

aṅgāravālukādhānyaṃ yatra devaḥ pravarṣati । kṣipraṃ tatra bhayaṃ ghoraṃ pravarteta caturvidham ।।

sarpān matsyān pakṣiṇo vā yatra devaḥ pravarṣati । tatra sasyopaghātaḥ syād bhayaṃ cātipravartate ।।

surāsavaṃ tathā kṣaudraṃ sarpis tailaṃ payo dadhi । yatra varṣati parjanyaḥ kṣudrogas tatra jāyate ।।

ulkātārāś ca dhiṣṇyeṣu yadāṅgārāṃś ca varṣati । tadā vyādhibhayaṃ ghoraṃ teṣu deśeṣu nirdiśet ।।

pumān aśvo gajo vāpi yadā yatra pradīpyate । daśamāsāt paraṃ tatra jānīyād rāṣṭrasaṃplavam ।।

nārācāḥ śaktayaḥ khaḍgāḥ pradīpyante yadā muhuḥ । tadā śastrabhayaṃ ghoraṃ teṣu deśeṣu nirdiśet ।।

caityavṛkṣāḥ prabhajyante visvaraṃ vinadanti ca । prahasanti prasarpanti gāyanti ca rudanti ca ।।

āgamaḥ paracakrasya teṣu cāpadyate tvaram । sacakrā vāpi naśyanti pradhānaś cātra vadhyate ।।

yatra sravec caityavṛkṣaḥ sahasā vividhān rasān । pṛthakpṛthak samastān vā tat pravakṣyāmi lakṣaṇam ।।

ghṛte madhuni dugdhe ca ghṛte dugdhe tathāmbhasi । kṣaudre madhuni taile vā vyādhayaḥ syuḥ sudāruṇāḥ ।।

surāsave mithobhedaḥ śoṇite śastrapātanam । taile pradhānā vadhyante bhakṣe kṣudbhayam ādiśet ।।

anṛtau cet phalaṃ yatra puṣpaṃ vā sūyate drumaḥ । vidyād dvādaśame māsi rājñas tatra viparyayam ।।

puṣpe puṣpaṃ bhaved yatra phale vā syāt tathā phalam । parṇe parṇaṃ vijānīyāt tatra jānapadaṃ bhayam ।।

śuklena vāsasā yatra caityavṛkṣaḥ samāvṛtaḥ । brāhmaṇānāṃ bhayaṃ ghoram āśu tīvraṃ vinirdiśet ।।

raktavastrāvṛtaiś cānyaiḥ kṣatriyāṇāṃ mahad bhayam । pītavastrais tu vaiśyānāṃ śūdrāṇāṃ kṛṣṇavāsasaiḥ ।।

nīlaiḥ sasyopaghātaḥ syāc citrais tu mṛgapakṣiṇām । vivarṇair vyādhayas tīvrāḥ paraṃ syur daśamāsataḥ ।।

daivatāni prasarpanti yatra rāṣṭre hasanti vā । udīkṣante atha rodhāṃsi tatra vidyān mahad bhayam ।।

vihasanti nimīlanti gāyanti vikṛtāni ca । māṃsaśonitagandhāni yatra tatra mahad bhayam ।।

yatra citram udīkṣeta gāyate ceṣṭate muhuḥ । eteṣv aṣṭasu māseṣu rājño maraṇam ādiśet ।।

citrāṇi yatra liṅgāni tathaivāyatanāni ca । vikāraṃ kuryur atyarthaṃ tatra vidyān mahad bhayam ।।

udapānaṃ taḍāgaṃ vā saraḥ parvata eva vā । samuddeśeṣu dīpyante vidyād bhayam upasthitam ।।

[prahaseyuḥ staneyur vā] śvā vā mārjāravad vadet । tasya deśasya rājā tu pīḍām āpnoti dāruṇām ।।

śaṅkhavaiṇavatūryāṇāṃ dundubhīnāṃ ca nisvanaḥ । deśe yatra bhṛśaṃ tatra rājadaṇḍo nipātyate ।।

yasya rājño janapade nityodvignāḥ prajāḥ kṣayam । gacchanti na citrāt tatra vināśam api nirdiśet ।।

yasya rājño janapade nityam eva gavāṃ kṣayaḥ । bhayaṃ tatra vijānīyād acirāt samupasthitam ।।

yasya rājño janapade nadī vahati kardamam । kāṣṭhaṃ tṛṇaṃ copalaṃ vā mṛtamatsyān grahāṃs tathā ।।

madyaṃ kṣaudraṃ ca māṃsaṃ ca sarpis tailaṃ payo dadhi । anyarājāgamabhayaṃ tatra deśe samādiśet ।।

yasya rājño janapade pratisroto nadī vahet । māsāṣṭakāj jānapadaṃ bhayaṃ syāc chastrapāṇinaḥ ।।

kūpo vā garjate yatra yadā vāpy avadīryate । lohitaṃ vātha pūyaṃ vā bhayaṃ tatra vinirdiśet ।।

āyudhāni pradhāvanti tīvraṃ pratyāharanti ca । tūṇīrāt sahasā bāṇā udgiranti nadanti ca ।।

svabhāvataś ca pūryante dhanūmṣi prajvalanti ca । saṃgrāmo dāruṇas tatra deśe bhavati biścitaḥ ।।

akāle puṣpavantaś ca phalavantaś ca pādapāḥ । dṛśyante yasya rāṣṭreṣu tasya nāśo vibhāvyate ।।

vṛkṣā vallyaś ca taruṇā yatra syuḥ phalapuṣpadāḥ । akāle cāpi dṛśyeyus tatra vidyān mahad bhayam ।।

prāsādāni vimānāni prajvalanti tu yatra vai । dṛḍhāni ca viśīryante yasya sa mriyate acirāt ।।

vadanty araṇye tūryāṇi śrūyante vyomni nityaśaḥ । nivaseta tadā rājā samāgamya diśo daśa ।।

yasya veśmani śrūyante gītavāditranisvanāḥ । akasmān mriyate samyag dhanaṃ cāsya vilupyate ।।

śaṅkhavaiṇavavīṇāś ca bherīmurajagomukhāḥ । vādyamānāḥ pradṛśyante deśe yatrāpy aghaṭṭitāḥ ।।

saṃbhṛtyaiva tato bhāram anyaṃ janapadaṃ vrajet । mṛgavāṃs tu sa deśo hi vāyuś cātropajāyate ।।

anāhatā dundubhayo vāditrāṇi vadanti ca । chidrāṇi ca gṛhe yasya sa śīghraṃ bhayam ṛcchati ।।

devarājadhvajānāṃ ca patanaṃ bhaṅga eva vā । kravyādānāṃ praveśaṃ ca rājñaḥ pīḍākaraṃ bhavet ।।

vājivāraṇamukhyānām akasmān maraṇaṃ bhavet । itarakṣamāpates tatra vijñeyā satvarāgatiḥ ।।

aśvatthe puṣpite kṣatraṃ brāhmaṇaṃ cāpy udumbare । plakṣe vaiśyāś tu pīḍyante nyagrodhe dasyavas tathā ।।

śvetam indrāyudhaṃ viprān raktaṃ kṣatriyanāśanam । vaiśyānāṃ pītakaṃ rātrau kṛṣṇaṃ śūdravināśanam ।।

nirghāte bhūmikampe ca caityaśuṣkavirohaṇe । deśapīḍāṃ vijānīyāt pradhānaś cātra vadhyate ।।

indrayaṣṭir bhajyate vā viśasto vā paśur vrajet । yadā tadā vijānīyād rājñaḥ pīḍām upasthitām ।।

pitāmahe vāsudeve somadharmāryameṣv api । nimittam aśubhaṃ yatra brāhmaṇānāṃ bhayāvaham ।।

bṛhaspatau vā śukre vā pāvake pākaśāsane । yāni rūpāṇi dṛśyante vidyāt tāni purohite ।।

mahādeve kubere ca tathā skandaviśākhayoḥ । nimittaṃ tat pārthiveṣu vijñeyaṃ saṃpravartitam ।। [akasmād dṛśyate yat tu nimittaṃ saṃprakīrtitam ।।] devānāṃ pārthivānāṃ ca ratho yatra nimajjati । bhayaṃ tatra vijānīyāt pārthivasyāśuradbhutam ।।

some ca vāsudeve ca varuṇe pākaśāsane । yad bhayaṃ dṛśyate tadd hi jñeyaṃ bhāṇḍādhike kane ।।

vāte prājāpatau caiva viśvakarmaṇi caiva hi । pravartate yan nimittaṃ taj jānapadikaṃ bhavet ।।

kumārīṣu kumārīṇāṃ kumārāṇāṃ kumārajam । tathā preṣyeṣu sarveṣu kalpayec chāstrataḥ phalam ।।

indrāṇi varuṇānī ca bhadrakālī mahābalā । vīramātā ca yad brūyus tad rājamahiṣībhayam ।।

ekaivāsāṃ tathā cānyā yāś cānyā devatāḥ striyaḥ । kuryur nimittaṃ tat strīṇāṃ pradhānānāṃ ca nirdiśet ।।

gandharveṣu nimittaṃ yat tad anyeṣu pradṛśyate । senāpatīnāṃ bhayakṛt sacivānāṃ bhayāya ca ।।

rakṣapannagayakṣeṣu liṅgasyāyataneṣu ca । yathārūpaṃ yathākarma puruṣeṣu vyavasthitam ।।

dakṣiṇeṣu śarīreṣu devatānāṃ ca veśmasu । sarveṣv aṅgeṣu nārīṇāṃ tulyaṃ syād ubhayor bhayam ।।

svaśarīre yathotpātā vihitā daivacintakaiḥ । tathaiva parisaṃkhyeyaṃ sarvatraiva śubhāśubham ।।

māṇibhadrādayo yakṣā gandharvāś citrasenayaḥ । tadbhayaṃ tu pradhānānām amātyānāṃ vibhāvayet ।।

yeṣu deśeṣu dṛśyeta daivateṣu śubhāśubham । te ca deśā vinaśyanti rājā vātha vinaśyati ।।

brāhmaṇā yatra vadhyante grāme rāṣṭre atha vā pure । rājadhānīṣu vā yatra tad abhāvasya lakṣaṇam ।।

yatrābalaṃ vadhyamānaṃ rājā naivābhirakṣati । tatra daivakṛto daṇḍo nipataty āśu rājani ।।

chattradhvajapatākāsu devasthāne gṛheṣu ca । dvārāṭṭālaka^harmyeṣu [kārayedd homavācanam] ।।

yatra prakṛtibhūtāni liṅgāni vikṛtāni ca । devatāś cāpi nadyaś ca kṣarakṣāmamahīruhāḥ ।।

senā caiva na dṛśyeta hastyaśvaiś ca padātibhiḥ । hīnāṅgā vikṛtāṅgā vā pralayaṃ tatra nirdiśet ।।

stambhavṛkṣā dhvajā yatra sraveyū rudhirāmbu ca । dhūmayeyur jvaleyur vā mantriṇāṃ tatra vai vadhaḥ ।।

jagatsvāmini jānīyād yadi ced divi jāyate । āntarikṣaṃ tu deśe syād bhaumaṃ sasyopatiṣṭhati ।।

bhāryāyāṃ vāhane putre kośe senāpatau pure । purohite narendre vā patate daivam aṣṭadhā ।।

māhendrīm amṛtāṃ raudrīṃ vaiśvadevīm athāpi vā । utpāteṣu mahāśāntiṃ kārayed bahudakṣiṇām ।।

śāmyanti yena ghorāṇi yogakṣemaṃ ca jāyate । rājāno muditās tatra pālayanti vasuṃdharām ।।

atha mahādbhutāni vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ।।

kṣipravipākīny amoghāni ghorāṇi grahopahatam ulkābhihataṃ grastaṃ nirastam upadhūpitaṃ vā yadā syāj janmanakṣatraṃ karmanakṣatram abhiṣecanīyajanapadanakṣatram eteṣu kṣipram eva mahāśāntim amṛtāṃ kārayed rājāṣṭame ca candramasaḥ sthāne ca devopasṛṣṭe skambhe vā 
atha vā nānāvarṇe bahurūpe śṛṅgiṇi cāditye kīlavati c[ādbhutāny] ulkābhihate
kacandha eva niśvasati hasati bhramati
hāse bhāse nāde śabde vāsane ca vaiśvānare aprajvalite antarikṣe bhasmāsthyaśmāṅgārā vīthī cendradhanuṣi rātrau vīdhra eva tu ।।

candrārkau yasya rāṣṭre pariviṣyetātāṃ tān vipakṣān parolakasaṃsthāñ janapadāṃs tathaiva kākakapotakaṅkagṛdhrayakṣarākṣasapiśācaśvāpadeṣu naktaṃ vadatsv abhivadatsu gāyatsu rāyatsu vā cakradhvajaveśmāvasathaprāsādāgre vāpīkūpa udapāne codgirati nadati vidyotati vā rathayantravāraṇapravahaṇavāditrādiṣūlkādayo aṅgārā dhūmo arcir vā prādurbhāve liṅgaṃ viliṅge rājñaḥ kālolūkakṛkalāsaśyenanipatite rājachattre bhagne dhvaje cakrasya rājño daṇḍe rājñaś ca dante 
hastinyāṃ ca mattāyāṃ grāme ca prasūtāyām
rājarathaś ca rājādhirūḍho bhagnākṣaḥ saptarātrād rājño hanti purohitam amātyaṃ senāpatiṃ jāyāṃ hastinaṃ mahiṣīṃ kumāraṃ rājānam eva vā ṛdhnuyād ya evaṃ veda
dvādaśaṃ śataṃ gavāṃ dhenūnāṃ kaṃsavasanaṃ hiraṇyaṃ niṣko aśva etāś ca dakṣiṇāḥ ।।

nānutpanneṣu daiveṣu rājñāṃ śāntir vidhīyate । asthāneṣu kṛtā śāntir nimittāyopapadyate । tasmāt sthānaṃ samuddiśya kārayec chāntim ātmanaḥ ।।

sarpasamitau vāyusaṃbhrame udakaprādurbhāvagamaneṣu dhanuḥsaṃdhyolkāpariveṣavidyuddaṇḍāśaniparighaparidhinirghāte rajovarṣam upalavarṣaṃ dadhimadhughṛtakṣīravarṣaṃ majjārudhira varṣati hīnagabhastī dve mārge vīthyau vittakṣaye somasya kṣaye apūrṇapūraṇe kṣayasyāvabhāsāḥ sadyo apararātrād digdāhopadhūpanam grahavaiṣamyam ārohaṇam ākramaṇaṃ gandharvanagaraṃ mārutaprakopas tithikaraṇamuhūrtanakṣatragrahādīnāṃ somaviyogaḥ pratisrotogāminyo nadyaḥ prāsādatoraṇadhvajeṣu vāyasasamavāyā vṛkaśakaṭārohaṇaṃ vṛṣadaṃśātimārjanam ulūkapratigarjanaṃ śyenagṛdhrādīnāṃ dhvajābhilapanam vikṛtāś ca mānuṣāmānuṣaprabhavāḥ strībālavṛddhapralāpāḥ pradīptendrayaṣṭipādabhagne adravyeṣv ekavṛkṣe dvichāye pratichāye parivṛktam ata ūrdhvam [chāyo] akasmāc caityavṛkṣastambhapatane virohatsv aviroheṣv achinnaparṇaprapātāc chuṣkaśākhino drumā dhūmarajodakaprādurbhāvagamaneṣu vanaspatiṣu bahuśastrabhaṅga indrakīlagopurāṭṭālakadhvajādīnāṃ bhaṅga ucitānāṃ vyucchedane anucitānāṃ pravardhane dṛḍhabhaṅgesu śuṣkavirohe gṛhe valmīke śayanadeśe darhastambotpattau mitravirodhe amitraprītau ca devatārcayo tathachedane yatra rājāprasādamukhaḥ paureṣu ca bhṛtyādiṣu bhavati bhavanti cātra ślokāḥ yadā tu pratipat somo vikṛtyā vikṛto bhavet । anudbhinno vilūno vā rājño maraṇam ādiśet ।।

āyudhākārarūpāṇi śvetavarṇākṛtīni ca । pañcavarṇāni cābhrāṇi tathā daṇḍanibhāni ca ।।

yadā candrārkayor madhye kṛṣṇaṃ bhavati maṇḍalam । sa śaṅkur iti vijñeyo grahaḥ paramadāruṇaḥ ।।

tatra rājño vadhaṃ vidyāt sarvabhūtabhayāvaham । tatra kuryān mahāśāntim amṛtāṃ viśvabheṣajīm iti ।।

atha yasminn eva janapade gobrāhmaṇasūtasāṃvatsaravaidyānāṃ parivrājakacāraṇavānaprasthabrahmacāriṇāṃ vāpi saṃkaraḥ pravartate tad adbhutaṃ vidyāt
karmasaṃkaraṃ yajñasaṃkaraṃ vyavahārasaṃkaraṃ ca yatra ca dharmo adharmeṣa pīḍyate tad adbhutaṃ vidyāt
teṣām ajñātaprāyaścittaṃ yad ajñātam anāmnātam iti madhye juhuyāt puruṣasūktaṃ ca teṣv akṛtaprāyaścitteṣu mahādbhutāni prādurbhavanti ।।

divyānīty ācakṣate devagṛheṣv atha hasanti gāyanti rudanti krośanti prasvidyanti pradhūmāyanti prajvalanti prakampanty unmīlayanti nimīlayanti lihitaṃ sravanti parivartayanti vā
teṣām prādurbhāvagamaneṣv anyarājāgamanaṃ vā vidyād udagraṃ vā[ṅgegam] avṛṣṭiśastrabhayaṃ bubhukṣāmāraṃ jānapadam amātyānāṃ rājño vināśam
teṣu sarveṣu bhṛgvaṅgirovidam ity uktaṃ sa catuṣpatha īśānaṃ prapadyeta ।। oṃ prapadye bhūḥ prapadye bhuvaḥ prapadye svaḥ prapadye janat prapadya iti prapadyeta

kapilānām aṣṭaśatasya kṣīreṇa pāyasaṃ śrapayitvā kapilāsv alabhyamānāsu dogdhrīṇāṃ śatasya kṣīreṇa pāyasaṃ śarapayitvā prāñcam idhmam upasamādhāya paristīrya barhī raudreṇa gaṇena śāntā juhuyāt ।। sarpir juhuyāt pāyasaṃ juhuyāc chuklāḥ sumanasa upahared brāhmaṇān bhaktenopepasanti tā eva gā dadyād rājyaṃ vā parimitakālaṃ tasya parituṣṭaye gosahasraṃ kartre dadyād grāmavaraṃ ca ।।

atha yatraitac chayane vātha vastre vā jāyate yad dhutāśanaḥ । etad atyadbhutaṃ nāma sarvakṣayakaraṃ nṛṇām ।।

atra brāhmīṃ mahāśāntiṃ kārayed bahudakṣiṇām । bahvannāṃ bahusaṃbhārām anūcānasudakṣiṇām । rājyakāmo arthakāmo vā pūjayet tu bṛhaspatim ।।

sṛjanti devā divyādbhutāni prāg upasargāt pratibodhanārtham । kāryāṇi vighnāni tathā janānāṃ karmākule varṇasamākule ca ।।

daivyopasṛṣṭena balena kāryaṃ kārya ca śāntiḥ praṇipatya devān । tatopasargād vighnāt pramucyate divi ced aniṣṭaṃ na punaḥ sa kuryāt ।।

pṛthivyām antarikṣe ca divi cāpy upalakṣayet । ceṣṭitaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ rutaṃ ca mṛgapakṣiṇām ।।

grāme kule vā yadi vāpi deśe rājany amātyeṣu tathā dvijeṣu । bhāvaḥ paśūnāṃ vikṛto virūpas tad adbhutaṃ tasya deśasya vidyāt ।।

amātyabhedo vividhaikaśīrṣa ekadviśīrṣe bhavati dvirājyam । apādahaste mriyate hy amātyo jāte kavandhe nṛpatir vinaśyet ।।

yadādhikāṅgo yadi vāṅgahīno bhavet paśūnāṃ vikṛto virūpaḥ । strīṇāṃ tathaiva vikṛto virūpas tad adbhutaṃ tasya deśasya vidyāt ।।

anāsyaṃ vāpy anoṣṭhaṃ vā jāyate ced vidūlakam । arūpam asarūpaṃ vā jāyate ced vidūlakam ।।

adharādīnn acakṣur vā jāyate ced vidūlakam । etad atyadbhutaṃ nāma rāṣṭre rājyakṣayamkaram ।।

tam adbhiḥ snātaṃ surabhiṃ sugandhiṃ gatāsum agnau juhuyād ghṛtāktam । ganeṇa raudreṇa ghṛtaṃ ca hutvā tathā mahātmā śivam asya kuryāt ।।
